条予以警告和撤销注册资格的除外），被指控违规人 员有机会通过向听证会提交口头或书面材料为自己 辩护。


224.8      仲裁委员会的所有决定均应有书面记录，并应包含 以下内容 ：

224.8.1             所犯违规行为。

224.8.2             违规证据。

224.8.3             违反的规则或仲裁委员会的指令。

224.8.4             实施的制裁。
224.9      处罚应与违规情节相对应。由仲裁委员会实施的任 何制裁的幅度均应考虑所有减轻和加重情形。


224.10      救济
224.10.1            除本规则第 224. 11 条规定的以外，对仲裁委员会的 处罚决定，可按照《国际雪联滑雪竞赛规则》中的 规定申诉。

224.10.2           未在《国际雪联滑雪竞赛规则》规定的最后期限 内提起申诉的，仲裁委员会的处罚决定即成为最 终决定。






THE INTERNATIONAL SKI
COMPETITION RULES (ICR)

1st Section 第一部分






224.11         The following decisions of the Jury are not subject to ap- peal:

224.11.1           Oral penalties imposed under art. 223.5 and 224.2

224.11.2           Monetary fines less than CHF  1’000.-- (One Thousand Swiss Francs) for single offence and a further CHF 2’500.-- for repeated offences by the same person.

224.12        In all remaining cases, appeals are to be directed to the Appeals Commission, as per the ICR.

224.13        The  Jury shall have the right to submit to the Ap- peals Commission recommendations for penalties in excess of monetary fines of CHF 5’000.-and  suspen- sions beyond the event in which the offence occurred (art.223.4).

224.14         FIS Council shall have the right to submit to the Appeals Commission comments with respect to any written pen- alty decisions by the Jury.

224.15        Costs of Proceedings
Fees and cash expenses, including travel expenses (costs of the proceedings) are to be calculated comparable to costs paid to TD’s and are to be paid by the offender. In the case of a reversal of Jury decisions, in whole or in part, the FIS covers all costs.

224.11     不得对仲裁委员会的下列决定提出申诉 ：


224.11.1           按照本规则第 223.5 和 224.2 条实施的口头处罚。

224.11.2           对单次违规人员处以罚金金额低于 1000 瑞士法郎， 对同一人员重复违规加处罚款金额低于 2500 瑞士 法郎。

224.12     其他所有案件，可按照《国际雪联滑雪竞赛规则》 的规定直接向申诉委员会申诉。

224.13     仲裁委员会有权向申诉委员会提出建议 ：处以 5000 瑞士法郎以上的罚款以及超出发生犯规行为的比赛 的禁赛（本规则第 223.4 条）。



224.14     国际雪联理事会有权就由仲裁委员会提出的任何书 面处罚决定向申诉委员会提出意见。


224.15     申诉费用
包括旅行费用在内的费用和现金花销的审理费用， 按照付给技术代表的费用标准计算，由违规者支付。 仲裁委员会决的定被完全或部分推翻的案件，国际  雪联承担所有的费用。

COMPETITION RULES (ICR)

1st Section 第一部分






224.16        Enforcement of Monetary Fines

224.16.1           The FIS oversees the enforcement of monetary fines and the costs of proceedings. Enforcement costs are consid- ered costs ofthe proceedings.

224.16.2           Any outstanding monetary fines imposed on an offender is considered a debt of the National Association to which the offender is a member.

224.17         Benefit Fund
All monetary fines are paid into the FIS Youth Promo- tion Fund.
224.18        These rules are not applicable to any violation of FIS Doping rules.

225            Appeals Commission

225.1          Appointments

225.1.1             The FIS Council shall appoint from the Discipline Sub-Committee for Rules (or Discipline Committee if there is no Rules Sub-Committee) a Chair and a Vice Chair of the Appeals Commission. The Vice Chair shall preside when the Chair is either unavailable or is dis- qualified for bias and prejudice.

225.1.2            The Chair shall appoint 3 members, to the Appeals

224.16     罚款的强制执行
224.16.1           国际雪联监督罚款和审理费用的执行情况。执行费 用视为审理费用的一部分。


224.16.2           对违规者科处但未缴之罚款均视为违规者所属国家 滑雪协会之债务。


224.17      福利基金
所有罚款都交给国际雪联青少年发展基金。


224.18     以上规则不适用于违反国际雪联反兴奋剂规则的 案件。
225       申诉委员会
225.1       任命
225.1.1             国际雪联理事会必须从纪律规则分委员会（若无纪 律规则分委员会则为纪律委员会）中任命 1 名申诉 委员会主任和 1 名副主任。当主任未出席或因偏见 回避事由而丧失资适格时，由副主任主持。



225.1.2             主任应从纪律规则分委员会或纪律委员会中任命 3 名





THE INTERNATIONAL SKI
COMPETITION RULES (ICR)


Commission from the Discipline Rules Sub-Committee or Discipline Committee for each case appealed or sub- mitted to be heard, which may include the Chair, whose decisions shall be by majority vote.

225.1.3             To avoid either actual bias and prejudice or the appear- ance of bias and prejudice, members appointed to an Appeals Commission shall not be members of the same National Association as the offender whose case is under appeal. In addition, members appointed to an Appeals Commission must report voluntarily to the Chair any bias and prejudice they may hold for or against the of- fender. Persons who are biased and prejudiced shall be disqualified from serving on the Appeals Commission by the Chair or, in the event the Chair is disqualified, by the Vice Chair.

225.2          Responsibility

225.2.1             The Appeals Commission shall only hold hearings with respect to appeals by offenders or by the FIS Council from decisions of competition juries, or matters referred to it by competition juries recommending penalties in excess of those provided for in the Sanction rules.

225.3           Procedures

225.3.1             The Appeal must be decided within 72 hours of receipt of the Appeal by the Chair, unless all parties involved in

1st Section 第一部分


委员组成申诉委员会（任命人员中可包括主任本人）， 负责每宗申诉或呈交听证的案件。其决定按简单多 数制通过。


225.1.3             为避免偏袒嫌疑或真正的偏袒行为，被指派的申诉  委员会成员与在审申诉案件所涉违规者不能同属一  个国家滑雪协会。此外，被指派的申诉委员会成员， 如果发现自己对违规者可能持有正面或者反面的先  入之见，必须主动向主任报告。对于任何持有偏见  者，主任（如果主任的资格也被取消，则为副主任） 应取消该委员在该案的申诉委员会工作的资格。






225.2       职责
225.2.1              申诉委员会仅在下列情况举行听证会 ：违规者提起 申诉的 ；国际雪联理事会对比赛仲裁委员会的决定 提起申诉的 ；比赛仲裁委员会建议的处罚超出制裁 规则的。


225.3       程序
225.3.1             申请应在申诉委员会主任收到申诉材料后 72 小时内 作出决定，除非申诉各方均书面同意为举行听证会

the Appeal agree in writing to an extension of time for the hearing.

225.3.2             All appeals and responses must be submitted in writing, including any evidence the parties intend to offer in sup- port of or in response to the Appeal.

225.3.3             The Appeals Commission shall decide on the location and format for the Appeal (phone conference, in person, e-mail exchanges).
The Appeals Commission members are required to re- spect the confidentiality of the appeal until the decision is made public and to consult only with the other mem- bers ofthe panel during the deliberations.
The Chair of the Appeals Commission may request addi- tional evidence from any of the parties involved, provid- ing this does not require disproportionate means.

225.3.4             The Appeals Commission shall allocate costs of the ap- peal pursuant to art. 224.15.

225.3.5            Decisions  of the Appeals Commission may be an- nounced orally at the conclusion of the deliberations or hearing should one take place. The decision, together with its reasoning, shall be submitted in writing to the FIS, which shall deliver them to the parties involved, their National Associations and all members of the Jury whose decision was appealed.
In addition, the written decision shall be available at the

225.3.3             申诉委员会应决定申诉的地点和形式（电话会议、 当面、电子邮件交流）。

申诉委员会成员要在决定公布之前尊重申诉的保密 性，并且在审议过程中只可与委员会其他成员商讨。


申诉委员会主任可要求任何当事方提交补充证据， 前提是举证方手段必须得当。


225.3.4             申诉委员会应当根据本规则第 224.15 条分配各方应 当承担的申诉费用。

225.3.5             申诉委员会的决定在审议或听证会结束时可以口头 宣布。决定及其理由应以书面形式提交国际雪联， 国际雪联再将上述材料分送各当事方、各方所属国 家滑雪协会以及其决定被申诉的仲裁委员会的所有 成员。


此外，决定的书面材料可在国际雪联办公室获取。

FIS Office.

225.4          Further Appeals

225.4.1             Decisions of the Appeals Commission may be appealed to the FIS Court in accordance with Article 52; 52.1 and 52.2 of the Statutes.
225.4.2             Appeals to the FIS Court shall be in writing and submit- ted to the FIS Secretary-General in accordance with the time limits prescribed in Article 52; 52.1 and 52.2 of the Statutes from the date of the publication of the Appeals Commission decision.
225.4.3             An Appeal to the Appeals Commission or to the FIS Court will not delay the implementation of any penalty decision of the Competition Jury, Appeals Commission or Council.

226            Violation of Sanctions
Where there is a violation of a sanction that has been im- posed (according to ICR art. 223 or the FIS Anti-Doping Rules, the Council may impose such further and other sanctions that it considers appropriate.
In such cases, some or all ofthe following sanctions may apply:

226.1          Sanctions against individuals involved:
- a written reprimand;and/or



225.4       再申诉
225.4.1             根据《国际雪联章程》第 52、52. 1 和 52.2 条，对申
诉委员会的决定还可向国际雪联法庭申诉。


225.4.2              自申诉委员会的决定公布之日起，申诉方应以书面 形式，在《国际雪联章程》第 52、52. 1 和 52.2 条规 定的时限内，将向国际雪联法院提出的再申诉提请 国际雪联秘书长转交。


225.4.3             向申诉委员会或者国际雪联法院提出申诉，不影响 比赛仲裁委员会、申诉委员会或者国际雪联理事会 的处罚决定的执行。


226       违规行为
对于违规则行为（依据本规则第 223 条或《国际雪 联反兴奋剂规则》），国际雪联理事会可以采取进一 步和其认为合理的其他制裁措施。

在这种情况下，可以采取如下部分或全部制裁措施：


226.1       对个人的制裁包括 ：
- 书面警告 ；或者






THE INTERNATIONAL SKI
COMPETITION RULES (ICR)

1st Section 第一部分






- a monetary  fine not to  exceed the  sum  of CHF 100’000.--and/or
- competition suspension at the next level of sanction-
for example if a three month suspension for a doping offence was imposed, a violation of the suspension will cause a two year suspension; if a two year suspension for a doping offence was imposed, a violation of the suspension will cause a lifetime suspension;and/or
- withdrawal of accreditation from individuals involved.

226.2           Sanctions against a National Ski Association:
- withdrawal ofFIS funding to the National Ski Associa- tion;and/or
- cancellation of future FIS events in the country in- volved;and/or
- withdrawal of some or all FIS membership rights, in- cluding participation in all FIS calendar competitions, voting rights at the FIS Congress, membership of FIS Committees.

- 不超过 10 万瑞士法郎的罚款 ；或者

- 禁赛期限升级一档。例如，某运动员因违反反兴奋 剂规则而被禁赛 3 个月，如果违反该禁赛的制裁则 会导致禁赛 2 年 ；某运动员因违反反兴奋剂规则而 被禁赛 2 年，违反该禁赛的制裁则会导致终身禁赛； 或者

- 取消其个人参赛资格。

226.2       对国家滑雪协会的制裁包括 ：
- 收回国际雪联对该国家滑雪协会的资助 ；或者

- 取消涉事国家今后举办国际雪联比赛的资格 ；或者

- 撤销其作为国际雪联成员的部分或者全部权利，包 括参加《国际雪联竞赛日历》中的所有比赛的权利、 在国际雪联代表大会上的表决权以及国际雪联各委 员会的会员资格。

Rules Common to Alpine Events

高山滑雪竞赛通则






THE INTERNATIONAL SKI
COMPETITION RULES (ICR)

2nd Section   Rules Common to Alpine Events 第二部分    高山滑雪竞赛通则






The rules of the FIS Alpine World Cup apply to the tech- nical organisation of the Olympic Winter Games and FIS World Ski Championships (Alpine Events) unless further specific rules have been detailed in the ICR.

600            Organisation
Reference is made to art. 211.

601           Organising Committee and Jury

601.1           Composition
The Organising Committee consists of those members (physical or legal) who are delegated by the organiser and by the International Ski Federation. It carries the rights, duties and obligations of the organiser.

601.2           Appointments by the International Ski Federation
The International Ski Federation appoints the Technical Delegate for all competitions and:

601.2.1             In World Cup Races:
- the Referee (Chief-Race-Director) and the Assistant Referee (Race-Director)
601.2.2             For the Olympic Winter Games and FIS World Ski Championships
- all Jury members (see art. 601.4. 1)

国际雪联《高山滑雪世界杯规则》适用于冬季奥林  匹克运动会和国际雪联世界锦标赛（高山滑雪赛事） 的技术组织，《国际雪联滑雪竞赛规则》另有进一步  的详细规定的除外。
600       组织
参见本规则第 211 条。

601       组委会和仲裁委员会
601.1       机构组成
组委会由组织方和国际雪联委派的成员（实体自然 人或法人代表机构）组成，享有组织方的权利、承 担组织方的义务和履行组织方的职责。


601.2            国际雪联任命

国际雪联为所有比赛任命技术代表并任命下列比赛 官员 ：
601.2.1       世界杯比赛 ：
裁判长（竞赛总主任）和副裁判长（竞赛主任）


601.2.2      冬季奥林匹克运动会和国际雪联世界锦标赛 ：

仲裁委员会全体成员（参见本规则第 601.4. 1 条）。






THE INTERNATIONAL SKI
COMPETITION RULES (ICR)

2nd Section   Rules Common to Alpine Events 第二部分    高山滑雪竞赛通则






601.2.3             In all other races the Technical Delegate appoints:
- the Referee and
- for Downhill and Super-G the Assistant Referee

601.2.4             By these appointments the above persons become mem-
bers ofthe Organising Committee.

601.3          Appointments by the organiser
The Organiser appoints all other members of the Organ- ising Committee(OC). The Chair or a representative rep- resents the Committee in public, leads the meetings and makes decisions concerning all matters that arenot made by other persons or groups. Before, during and after the competition(s) they work closely with the International Ski Federation and its appointed officials and takes on all other duties that are necessary for carrying out the competition.
The following officials must be appointed:

601.3.1             The Chief of Race
The Chief of Race directs all preparation of the compe-     tition and supervises the activities in the technical area.     The Chief of Race summons meetings for consideration     of technical questions and leads the team captains ’ meetings after consultation with the Technical Delegate.

601.3.2             The Chief of Course
The Chief of Course is responsible for the preparation of the courses in accordance with the directive s  and

601.2.3      在其他所有比赛中，技术代表任命 ：
- 裁判长
- 滑降和超级大回转比赛副裁判长

601.2.4       获得上述任命者为组委会成员。


601.3       组织方任命
组织方任命组委会其他成员。组委会主任或组委会  的代表在公开场合代表组委会、主持组委会会议、 决定其他人员或团组未决事宜。组委会及其成员在  赛前、赛中和赛后，与国际雪联及其任命的官员在  工作中密切合作，承担办好比赛必需的其他所有职责。




下列官员应当由组织方任命 ：

601.3.1      竞赛长
竞赛长指导比赛的所有准备工作，并监督技术领域 的活动，召集会议研究讨论技术问题，经商技术代 表后主持领队会议。



601.3.2      赛道长
赛道长根据仲裁委员会的指令和决定负责做好赛道 的准备工作，必须熟悉比赛当地与雪道相关 的地形






THE INTERNATIONAL SKI
COMPETITION RULES (ICR)

2nd Section   Rules Common to Alpine Events 第二部分    高山滑雪竞赛通则






decisions of the Jury. The Chief of Course must be familiar with local snow conditions on the terrain concerned.

601.3.3             The Start Referee
The Start Referee must remain at the start from the be- ginning of the official inspection time and until the end of a training/event to:
- Make sure that the regulations for the start and the start organisation are properly observed.
- Determine late and false starts.
- Be a point of contact for the Jury at all times and im- mediately (see art.705.5).
- Report the names of the competitors who did not start to the Referee, and informs the Jury of all infringe- ments against the rules, such as false or delayed starts or violations against the rules for equipment.
- Ensure that reserve bibs are available at the start.

601.3.4             The Finish Referee
The Finish Referee must remain at the finish from the beginning of the official inspection time until the end of a training/event to:
- Make sure that all the regulations for the organisation of the finish and the finish in-run and out-run are prop- erly observed.
- Supervise the finish controller, the timing and the crowd control in the finish area.
- Be a point of contact for the Jury at all times and im- mediately.

及其雪况。


601.3.3       起点裁判长
从官方视察线路开始直至当天的训练或比赛全部结 束，起点裁判长都必须始终坚守在起点，以便履行 下列职责 ：
- 确保有关出发和组织出发方面的规定切实得到 遵守。
- 决定延迟出发和出发犯规。
- 作为仲裁委员会可以随时并能即时联系的联系点 （参见本规则第 705.5 条）。
- 向裁判长报告未出发运动员的姓名，向仲裁委员会 通报所有犯规行为，如出发犯规或延迟出发以及违 反竞赛器材规则的行为。

- 确保起点处有备用号码布。

601.3.4      终点裁判长
从官方视察线路开始直至训练和比赛全部结束，终 点裁判长必须始终坚守在终点，以便履行下列职责：
- 确保终点区、终点冲刺区和终点停止区的组织规定 切实得到遵守。

- 监督终点监督员、计时工作以及终点区观众管理。

- 作为仲裁委员会可以随时并能即时联系的联系点。






THE INTERNATIONAL SKI
COMPETITION RULES (ICR)

2nd Section   Rules Common to Alpine Events 第二部分    高山滑雪竞赛通则






- Report the names of the competitors who did not finish to the Referee and informs the Jury of all infringements against the rules.

601.3.5             The Chief Gate Judge
The Chief Gate Judge organises and supervises the work of the gate judges. The Chief Gate Judge designates the gates each will supervise and places them in position. At the end of the first run and the end of the race, the Chief Gate Judge collects the gate judges’control cards and delivers them to the Referee.
The Chief Gate Judge distributes, in good time, the ma- terial that is needed (control card, pencil, start list, etc.) to each gate judge and is prepared to offer assistance either to help keep the spectators off the competition course or to help maintain the course, etc. The Chief Gate Judge make sure that the numbering and the mark- ing of the gates is completed within the required time.

601.3.6             The Chief of Timing and Calculations
The Chief of Timing and Calculations is responsible for the coordination of officials at the start and finish, in- cluding timing and calculations. In Slalom, the Chief of Timing and Calculations or a special assistant will decide the interval between starts. The following officials are un- der The Chief of Timing and Calculations direction:
- starter
- assistant starter
- start recorder

- 向裁判长通报未通过终点的运动员的姓名，向仲裁 委员会通报所有犯规行为。


601.3.5      旗门裁判长
旗门裁判长组织和监督旗门裁判员的工作。旗门裁 判长指定（每一位旗门裁判员所负责）监控的旗门 并把各旗门裁判员安排到适当的位置 ；第 1 轮滑行 和比赛结束后，负责收集旗门裁判员的监督卡并交 裁判长。

旗门裁判长适时向各旗门裁判员分发所需用品（监 督卡、铅笔、出发顺序表等），随时准备协助把观众 清出赛道或帮助维护赛道等。旗门裁判长确保在规 定时间内完成旗门的编号和标记工作。




601.3.6      计时计算长
计时计算长负责协调起、终点的官员以及计时与计 算。在回转比赛中，计时计算长或一位特别助理决 定出发的间隔时间。计时计算长指挥下列官员 ：



- 发令员
- 助理发令员
- 起点记录员





THE INTERNATIONAL SKI
COMPETITION RULES (ICR)


- chief timekeeper
- assistant timekeepers
- finish controller
- chief of calculations and the assistants
The Chief of Timing and Calculations oversees the preparation of the Timing and Data Technical Report (TDTR) and xml file for the electronic transmittal to FIS following the competition. A copy of the report may also be printed (only if the TD has no access to the TD re- port) for review prior to the transmission of the xml file. The TDTR Software can be found on the FIS website.

601.3.7             The Race Secretary
The Race Secretary is responsible for all secretarial work for the technical aspects of the competition and amongst others for the preparation of the draw. The Race Secretary ensures that the official results contain the in- formation required by art. 617.3.4. and is responsible for the minutes of the technical officials, the Jury and team captains’meetings.
The Race Secretary ensures that all forms for start, finish, timing,calculations, and gate-judging are well prepared, and handed over to the officials concerned in good order at the proper time.
The Race Secretary facilitates the calculation of results by appropriate preparation and ensures that the result xml file is available for transmission to FIS.
The Race Secretary also ensures the duplication and publication of the official results after the Results are

2nd Section   Rules Common to Alpine Events 第二部分    高山滑雪竞赛通则


- 计时长
- 助理计时员
- 终点监督员
- 计算长及其助理
计时及计算长负责监督比赛后以电子文件方式传输 给国际雪联的《计时与数据技术报告（TDTR）》和 可扩展标记语言文件（XML）的编制工作。在传输 可扩展标记语言文件（XML）之前，可以打印一份《计 时与数据技术报告》的副本（仅当技术代表无法查 阅该报告时）以供审查。《计时与数据技术报告》的 填报软件可在国际雪联官网上找到。
601.3.7      竞赛秘书
竞赛秘书负责整个比赛的竞赛技术方面的所有秘书 工作，如做好抽签准备等 ；确保比赛正式结果包含 本规则第 617.3.4 条要求的信息 ；负责技术官员、仲 裁委员会和领队会议的会议记录。



竞赛秘书负责精心准备确保将起点、终点、计时、 计算及旗门裁判员需要的所有表格，并按照正确顺  序在恰当的时间送交有关官员。
竞赛秘书通过适当的准备促进比赛成绩的计算，确 保包含比赛成绩的可扩展标记语言文件（XML）准 备就绪以便传输给国际雪联。
竞赛秘书确保在比赛成绩被认定为“对国际雪联积 分系统有效”后，复制并公布正式成绩。可扩展标

COMPETITION RULES (ICR)


considered“Valid for FIS points”. In the case that the transmission of the electronic xml result file is delayed, results may be duplicated and published with the permis- sion of the TD.

601.3.8             The Chief of Medical and Rescue Services
The Chief of Medical and Rescue Services is responsible for organising adequate first aid and medical coverage during the official training periods and the actual competition.
The Chief of Medical and Rescue Services must arrange an appropriate facility to which injured competitors should be taken and treated.
The Chief of Medical and Rescue Services coordinates plans with the team doctors before the start of the official training or the start of any competition.
During training and the races The Chief of Medical and Rescue Services must be in telephone or radio commu- nication with the assistants and must co-ordinate plans with the Chief of Race before the start of the official training, or start of any competition.
A doctor, who should be a good skier, should be ready at the start to deal with any eventuality and must stay in contact with the Jury and the members of the rescue ser- vice. This task can be delegated to a team doctor. Details of the Medical Support Requirements are given in chap- ter 1 of the FIS Medical Guide.

The following officials may also be appointed:

记语言文件（XML）的传输延迟的，经技术代表允许， 可以复制并公布成绩。



601.3.8       医疗与救援主管
医疗与救援主管负责 ：
在场地适应训练和正式比赛期间组织充分的现场急 救和医疗服务工作 ；
安排好适当的设备以接纳并救治受伤运动员 ;


在场地适应训练或任何比赛开始前与随队医生协调 工作计划 ；
在训练和比赛期间，必须与助手保持电话或无线电 对讲通信 ；
在场地适应训练或任何比赛开始前与竞赛长协调工 作计划 ；
在起点处安排一位滑雪技术过硬的医生负责随时准  备处理任何意外，该医生必须与仲裁委员会及救护  人员持续保持联系。此项任务可指派给一位随队医  生。详细的医疗支持服务要求见《国际雪联医疗指南》 第一章。

601.3.9.1     The Chief of Finish Area
The Finish Area Coordinator is responsible for coor- dinating the various requirements in the finish area to deal with any request the demanding, pre, during and post-competition activities. Responsibilities include con- struction and coordination of the mixed-zone, television and press interviews, winner ceremonies, doping control facility and the coordination with security for these areas.     The collaboration is between the LOC’s Finish Area Co- ordinator and persons managing the above areas, togeth- er with the FIS personnel handling equipment control, teams, accreditation and access, media, ceremonies and doping controls, from the planning stages through to im- plementation during the event.

601.3.9.2     The Chief of Course Equipment and Technical Equipment   The Chief of Course Equipment is responsible for the provision of equipment and tools needed for the prepa- ration and maintenance of the competition courses and the conduct of the race, where these duties have not been assigned to another official.

601.3.9.3     The Chief of Press
The Chief of Press is responsible for all briefing and in- formation provided to journalists, photographers, televi- sion and radio reporters, in accordance with the instruc- tions ofthe Organising Committee.

601.3.9.1     终点区域主管
终点区域协调员负责整合对终点区域提出的各种要 求，以处理在赛前、赛中及赛后终点区域的活动产 生的任何需要。终点区域主管的职责包括 ：创建和 协调混合区域、电视和媒体采访、颁奖仪式、兴奋 剂控制设施等，并协调该区域的安全。


终点区域管理合作是建立在组委会委派的终点区域 协调员和管理该区域的工作人员之间的，与国际雪 联工作人员共同协同完成。他们在赛事计划阶段直 至赛事执行过程中要处理竞赛器材检查、运动队管 理、注册与准入、媒体、颁奖仪式和兴奋剂控制等 各方面的工作。
601.3.9.2     赛道长和技术设备主管
赛道长负责提供赛道准备和维护以及维持比赛的运 行所需的设备和工具。上述职责中未指派给其他官 员的，均应由赛道长负责。



601.3.9.3     新闻媒体主管
新闻媒体主管根据组委会的指令，负责向新闻记 者、摄影记者、电视和电台记者通报情况并为其 提供信息。

- the Referee

- the Start Referee (Olympic Winter Games and FIS World Ski Championships)
- the Finish Referee (Olympic Winter Games and FIS World Ski Championships)

601.4.1.1     The FIS Council appoints:

- the Finish Referee

In order to qualify, a proposed member must hold a valid licence as a Technical Delegate of the FIS.

601.4.1.3     The organising National Ski Association submits its pro- posals for the Chief of Race in the Organising Commit- tee to the FIS Council for approval.

601.4.1.4     The Jury of a women race must include at least one woman.

601.4.1.5     All members of the Jury must be able to understand each other in one and the same FIS language.

601.4.1.6     Persons who work for a National Ski Association with responsibility for a ski team must not be members of the Jury.

601.4.1.4     女子比赛的仲裁委员会必须包含至少一位女性成员。

601.4.5             Franchise and Voting (World Cup:  See also World
Cup Rules)
The TD is Chair of the Jury and conducts the meetings. Each of the following has one vote in the Jury:

601.4.5.1     For Olympic Winter Games and FIS World Ski Champi- onships, all Jury members.

601.4.5.2     For International races
The TD, Chief of Race, Referee and in the case of Downhill and Super-G, the Assistant Referee.

601.4.5.3     Decisions are made by simple majority vote of members present and voting (exception art. 646.3).
601.4.5.4     In the case of a tie, the TD has the casting vote (also see World Cup Rules).

601.4.5.5     Minutes must be kept of all meetings and decisions of the Jury and signed by each individual member of the Jury, with each individual vote on decisions recorded, as per art. 601.3.7.

601.4.5.6     The Minutes must be written in at least one of the FIS languages (English, French or German).

提出抗议时，于抗议期限届满时职责结束 ；否则， 其职责需在处理完全部抗议后结束。


601.4.5      特权和表决权（世界杯 ：另见《国际雪联世界杯 规则》）

601.4.5.3      由出席会议的成员按简单多数制投票形成决定（本 规则第 646.3 条规定的除外）。

601.4.5.4     表决出现平局时，技术代表拥有最终决定权（另参 见《国际雪联世界杯规则》）。

601.4.5.5     依照本规则第 601.3.7 条，必须保存由每位仲裁委员 会成员签名的所有会议记录和仲裁委员会决定，并 记录每位成员对决定的投票情况。

COMPETITION RULES (ICR)

2nd Section   Rules Common to Alpine Events 第二部分    高山滑雪竞赛通则






601.4.5.7     In cases where an immediate decision must be made and it is not possible to convene the entire Jury, each member of the Jury has the right, prior to or during the race, to make decisions which according to the rules are reserved to the Jury as a whole; but only provisionally with the obligation to have the decision confirmed by the Jury as soon as possible.

601.4.6             Duties of the Jury
The Jury monitors the adherence to the rules throughout the entire race, including the official training.

601.4.6.1     From a technical standpoint particularly by:
- Checking the competition course and the set courses
- Checking the snow conditions
- Checking the preparation of the course
- Approving the use of snow compactors and other chemicals
- Checking the crowd control systems
- Checking the start, the finish and the run-out from the finish
- Checking the first aid service
- Appointing the course setters
- Fixing the time of course setting
- Overseeing the work of the course setters
- Spot-checking of the gate panels
- Opening or closing competition courses for training after consideration of the technical preparations and the prevailing weather conditions

601.4.5.7     必须立即作出决定但不可能召集仲裁委员会全体成 员开会的，仲裁委员会每一位成员均有权在比赛前 或比赛中行使根据规则本应由仲裁委员会作为一个 整体保留的决定权 ；但只能作出临时性决定，仲裁 委员会必须尽快追认。



601.4.6       仲裁委员会的职责
整个比赛过程中，包括场地适应训练期间，仲裁委 员会始终负责监督比赛规则的遵守情况。
601.4.6.1      在技术方面，仲裁委员会主要负责 ：
- 检查赛道和旗门设计 ；
- 检查雪况 ；
- 检查赛道的准备工作 ；
- 批准使用压雪机及融雪剂等化学品 ；

- 检查观众管理系统 ；
- 检查出发区、终点区域和终点坡道延伸部分 ；

- 检查急救服务体系 ；
- 任命旗门设计员 ；
- 确定旗门设计时间 ；
- 监督旗门设计员的工作 ；
- 对旗门布进行抽检 ；
- 根据技术准备状况和当前天气情况，决定开放或关 闭用于训练的赛道 ；





THE INTERNATIONAL SKI
COMPETITION RULES (ICR)


- Determining the method of the competitor’s course in- spection
- Inspection of the course before the race
- Determining the number of forerunners for each run and setting the start order of the forerunners
- Debriefing the forerunners as necessary
- Changing the start order after consideration of course conditions and in extraordinary conditions
- Changing the start intervals
- Giving instructions to and obtaining information from the gate judges
For Downhill:
- Arrangement of an additional competitor’s inspection in unusual weather conditions
- Shortening the official training
- Positioning of yellow ﬂag
- Checking on the setting of gates
- Changing the position and distance of the gates or add- ing extra gates as indicated by the experience gained in the training runs. Following significant changes, the competitors must be allowed at least one more training run on the course.
601.4.6.2     From an organisational viewpoint particularly by:
- Ranking of the competitors for the draw
- Division of the competitors without points into groups according to some determined basis
- Granting of re-runs
- Cancellation of the race (beforehand)

2nd Section   Rules Common to Alpine Events 第二部分    高山滑雪竞赛通则


- 决定运动员视察线路的方式 ；

- 赛前视察线路 ；
- 决定每轮滑行的试滑员人数及出发顺序 ；

- 必要时要求试滑员汇报试滑情况 ；
- 根据赛道情况及特殊情况，改变出发顺序 ；

- 改变出发时间间隔 ；
- 指挥并听取旗门裁判员的汇报。

对于滑降比赛 ：
- 天气条件异常的，额外安排一次运动员视察线路 ；

- 缩短场地适应训练的时间 ；
- 确定黄旗的位置 ；
- 检查旗门设置情况 ；
- 根据在场地适应训练中获得的体验，调整旗门位置 和间距，或者增加旗门数量。如调整较大，必须允 许运动员再进行 1 次场地适应训练。



601.4.6.2     在组织方面，仲裁委员会主要负责 ：
- 安排运动员抽签顺序 ；
- 根据某些客观标准，对没有积分的运动员分组 ；

- 批准重滑 ；
-（基于如下情况，事先决定）取消比赛 ：





THE INTERNATIONAL SKI
COMPETITION RULES (ICR)


- if snow conditions are unsuitable
- the recommendations of the Technical Advisor’s report have not been carried out
- the first aid and medical service are inadequate or missing
- the crowd control is insufficient
- Shortening the course, if snow or weather conditions make this appear necessary
- Interruption of the race if the prerequisites of art. 624 are present
- Termination of the race if the prerequisites of art. 625 are present

601.4.6.3     From a disciplinary viewpoint particularly by:
- Decision on a proposal of the Technical Delegate or a Jury member to exclude a competitor for lack of physi- cal and technical ability
- Enforcement of the checks on regulations concerning ad- vertising on equipment and clothing in the competition area
- Decisions on limitation of quotas for officials, techni- cians and medical personnel for admission to the race-
course
- Imposition of sanctions
- Decisions on protests
- Issue of particular directives throughout the entire event

601.4.7             Questions not Covered by Rules
In general, the Jury makes decisions on all questions not clarified by the Rules.

2nd Section   Rules Common to Alpine Events 第二部分    高山滑雪竞赛通则


- 雪况不适宜比赛 ；
- 未落实技术顾问报告中的建议 ；

- 急救和医疗服务不足或缺失 ；
- 观众管理工作不到位 ；
- 缩短赛道，如果雪况或天气条件表明这样做明显必 要时 ；
- 暂停比赛，如果出现本规则第 624 条中的情况 ；

- 终止比赛，如果出现本规则第 625 条中的情况。


601.4.6.3      在纪律方面仲裁委员会主要负责 ：
- 根据技术代表或仲裁委员会成员的建议，勒令身体 条件和技能不足的运动员退出比赛 ；

- 在比赛场地实施对器材和服装上的广告是否合规 的检查 ；
- 决定压缩进入赛道的官员、技术人员和医务人员的 配额 ；

- 实施制裁 ；
- 裁断抗议 ；
- 在整个比赛期间发布特别指令。


601.4.7      《国际雪联滑雪竞赛规则》未涉及的问题
一般情况下，对于《国际雪联滑雪竞赛规则》未明 确的问题，仲裁委员会有权作出决定。

COMPETITION RULES (ICR)

2nd Section   Rules Common to Alpine Events 第二部分    高山滑雪竞赛通则






601.4.8             Radios
At all competitions published in the FIS Calendar, the Jury members plus Start and Finish Referee must be equipped with radios. These must function on a single reserved frequency and be free of interference.

601.4.9             Duties of the TD for all Events
For FIS World Cup, FIS World Ski Championships and Olympic Winter Games the duties of the TDs are defined in the World Cup rules.

601.4.9.1     Before the race The TD
- Reviews the homologation file and consults the organ- iser regarding the existence of a special authorisation.
- If it is established that no homologation exists, the Jury must cancel the race (see art. 650).
- Reads the TD reports concerning previous events at the site and checks whether any improvements proposed in these reports have been carried out.
- Inspects the liability insurance certificate as required by art. 212.2 and reports where necessary to the FIS.
- Inspects the competition courses.
- Supervises the compliance with art. 704 concerning the official training.
- Spot checks the gate panels.
- Collaborates in the administrative and technical prepa- rations.
- Checks the official entry lists, including FIS points.

601.4.8      对讲机
在《国际雪联竞赛日历》中公布的所有比赛中，仲 裁委员会成员以及起点和终点裁判长均需配备使用 专属频率且不受干扰的对讲机。


601.4.9      技术代表在所有比赛中肩负的职责
技术代表在国际雪联世界杯、国际雪联世界锦标赛 和冬季奥林匹克运动会的职责，参见世界杯规则。


601.4.9.1      赛前职责
技术代表负责 ：
- 复审赛道认证文件，询问组织方赛道是否获得专门 授权。
- 如果技术代表认为赛道未经认证，仲裁委员会必须 取消该比赛（见本规则第 650 条）。
- 查阅该赛场以往赛事的技术代表报告，检查报告中 提出的改进建议是否已经落实。

- 检查已经投保本规则第 212.2 条要求的责任保险的 确认证明，必要时报告国际雪联。
- 视察赛道。
- 监督对本规则第 704 条关于场地适应训练之规定的 遵守情况。
- 抽检旗门布。
- 协调赛事组织和技术准备工作。

- 检查正式报名表，特别是其中填报的国际雪联积分。






THE INTERNATIONAL SKI
COMPETITION RULES (ICR)

2nd Section   Rules Common to Alpine Events 第二部分    高山滑雪竞赛通则






- Checks on the presence of sufficient radios for all members of the Jury (with separate frequencies).
- Takes note of the accreditation and the authorisation for entry to the competition course.
- Checks over the competition courses with regard to preparation, marking, crowd control, as well as the lay- out of start and finish areas.
- Supervises the course setting together with the Jury.
- Checks on the location of the television towers and sees that they are adequately protected if necessary.
- Checks the locations of the first aid service along the course as well as the organisation of the medical care.
- Checks on all technical installations such as timekeeping, hand timing, communications, transport of people, etc.
- Is present in the race area during all official trainings.
- Takes part in all meetings of the Jury and of the team captains.
- Works closely together with the officials of the Organ- ising Committee and the FIS technical advisor.
- Is Chair of the Jury with a casting vote in case of a tie.
- If necessary, appoints members to the Jury.
- Has the right, if a Slalom or Giant Slalom cannot be carried out on the homologated competition course ow- ing“force majeure”, to move the race to a“substitute competition course”proposed by the organiser.
This is on the explicit condition that the necessary ho- mologation 38 measures can be fulfilled. For Downhill and Super-G there is only the possibility of shortening

- 检查是否为仲裁委员会所有成员准备了足够的对 讲机（具备不同的频率）。
- 记录进入赛道的注册与授权情况。

- 检查赛道的准备、标识、观众管理以及起点、终点 区的布置等情况。

- 会同仲裁委员会一起监督旗门的设计。
- 检查 电视塔 的位置，确保其在必要时得到妥善 保护。
- 检查赛道沿线各急救站的位置和医疗服务的组织 情况。
- 检查所有技术装置，如计时、手动计时、通讯、人 员转运等。
- 所有场地适应训练期间应亲临比赛区域。
- 参加所有仲裁委员会会议和领队会议。

- 与组委会官员和国际雪联技术顾问在工作中密切 合作。
- 担任仲裁委员会主任，并在表决出现平局时拥有最 终决定权。
- 如有必要，任命仲裁委员会成员。
- 因“不可抗力”因素导致回转和大回转比赛不能在 获得认证的赛道上进行时，有权根据组织者的建议， 把比赛移到替补赛道上举行。这样做必须满足的明  确条件是，替补赛道满足必要的认证措施。
在滑降和超级大回转比赛中，只可以在批准的赛道 上缩短比赛距离。但在任何情况下，均需确保达到 规定的最小的垂直落差。

the run on a homologated competition course.The min- imum prescribed vertical drops must, however, be ob- served in every case.

601.4.9.2     During the race The TD
- Must be present in the competition area.
- Works closely with the Jury, the team captains and the coaches.
- Observes that the valid rules and directives with regard to advertising, on clothing and race equipment are obeyed.
- Supervises the technical and organisational conduct of the event.
- Advises the organisation concerning the observance of the FIS Rules and regulations, and directives ofthe Jury.

601.4.9.3     After the race The TD
- Helps with the compilation of the Referee’s report.
- Calculates the race and penalty points for the individ- ual races. If these points are calculated by computer, it is the TD’s duty to re-check the points and to confirm their accuracy with a personal signature. Above all, it is important to check the correct use of the corresponding F value for each event.
- Presents properly submitted protests to the Jury for de- cision.
- Signs the official result lists provided by the race secre- tary and give the authorisation for the award ceremony.






601.4.9.2      比赛期间职责
在比赛期间，技术代表 ：
- 必须亲临比赛场地。
- 与仲裁委员会、领队和教练员在工作中密切合作。

- 确保关于比赛服装和竞赛器材上广告标识的有效 规则和指令得到遵守。
- 监督比赛的技术与组织实施工作。

- 就遵守《国际雪联滑雪竞赛规则》及相关规定与仲 裁委员会的指令向组织方建言献策。

601.4.9.3     赛后职责
比赛结束后，技术代表应当 ：
- 协助撰写裁判长报告。
- 计算比赛积分和判罚分。如果积分由电脑计算，技 术代表的职责是复核积分，并在确认其准确性后签 名。最重要的是检查本次比赛对应的 F 值是否运 用正确。


- 将适当提出的抗议转交仲裁委员会裁决。

- 在竞赛秘书提供的正式成绩列表上签名，批准举行 颁奖仪式。

COMPETITION RULES (ICR)

2nd Section   Rules Common to Alpine Events 第二部分    高山滑雪竞赛通则






- Oversees the electronic transmission of the Timing Report (TDTR) xml files and completes the TD Report online immediately after the event and must also check that the results are correct on the FIS website. For more information see Rules of the FIS points.
- Presents to the FIS proposals for changes in the com- petition rules on the basis of practical experience at the event in question.

601.4.9.4     In general The TD
- Decides on questions which are not covered or are in- sufficiently covered by the FIS Rules, in so far as these have not already been decided by the Jury and do not fall within the scope of other authorities.
- Works very closely with the Referee and Assistant Referee.
- Has the right to propose to the Jury the exclusion of competitors from participating in the race.
- Has the right to obtain support from the Organising Com- mittee and all officials under its jurisdiction in all matters necessary for the fulfilment of the TD’S duties.

601.4.9.5     Olympic Winter Games, FIS World Ski Championships
and FIS Junior World Ski Championships
The TD prepares a detailed final report to be sent to the FIS and the Organising Committee.

601.4.10           Duties and Rights of the Referee
- The Referee supervises the draw.

- 监督《计时报告》（TDTR）及可扩展标记语言文 件（XML）的电子传输工作，在赛事结束后立即 在线完成《技术代表报告》，检对国际雪联网站上 的成绩是否正确。详见《国际雪联积分规则》。

- 以本次比赛的实际经验为基础，向国际雪联提出修 改比赛规则的建议。


601.4.9.4     一般职责
技术代表负责 ：
- 对于《国际雪联滑雪竞赛规则》没有涉及或涵盖不 足的问题，若尚未由仲裁委员会作出决定，也不属 于其他部门的职权范围，由技术代表作出决定。

- 与裁判长和副裁判长在工作中密切合作。
- 有权向仲裁委员会提议勒令运动员退出比赛。

- 在履行职责时，有权获得组委会和所有在组委会管 辖权限范围内的官员就履行技术代表的职责所必 需的支持。

601.4.9.5     冬季奥林匹克运动会、国际雪联世界滑雪锦标赛和 国际雪联世界青少年锦标赛
技术代表准备详细的最终报告，提交国际雪联和组 委会。
601.4.10      裁判长的职责与权利
- 裁判长监督抽签。

COMPETITION RULES (ICR)

2nd Section   Rules Common to Alpine Events 第二部分    高山滑雪竞赛通则






- At the end of the first run, and again at the end of the race, the Referee will receive the Start and Finish Ref- erees’reports, and any other official reports regarding breach of rules and disqualifications.
- Checks, signs and posts the Referee’s Report on the official notice board at the end of each run, and at the end of the race, including a list of disqualified compet- itors, the gate numbers where the faults occurred, the name of the relevant gate judge or judges, and the exact time of the posting.
- Sends a report to the FIS should unusual circumstances arise or in the event of a serious difference of opinion among the Jury members or in the case of severe injury to a competitor.

601.4.10.1    Collaboration with the TD
The Referee and the Assistant Referee work very closely with the TD.

601.4.11           The Technical Adviser
To support the Jury, the Alpine Committee can appoint technical advisers for all categories of races.
The technical adviser has the right to express an opinion within the Jury without the right to vote.

601.5           The FIS can impose sanctions against a Jury or individu- al Jury members.

- 在第一轮滑行结束后和比赛结束后，裁判长负责接 收起点、终点裁判长的报告及其他关于违反规则和 取消资格的官方报告。

- 在每一轮滑行结束后和比赛结束后，裁判长要检 查、签署裁判长报告单并张贴在官方公告板上。丧 失资格运动员名单、发生失误的旗门号码、相关旗 门裁判员的姓名及张贴的准确时间，均应在该报告 单中体现出来。

- 出现特殊情况、仲裁委员会成员意见严重分歧或运 动员受重伤时，应向国际雪联递交报告。



601.4.10.1    与技术代表合作
裁判长和副裁判长应与技术代表在工作中保持非常 密切的合作。
601.4.11     技术顾问
为支持仲裁委员会的工作，高山滑雪委员会可以为 各种比赛任命技术顾问。
技术顾问在仲裁委员会中有权发表意见，但无权 表决。
601.5       国际雪联可以对仲裁委员会或其成员进行处罚。

602           The Technical Delegate (TD)

602.1          Definition

602.1.1             The primary duties of the TD
- to make sure that the rules and directions ofthe FIS are followed
- to see that the event runs smoothly
- to advise the organisers about the scope of their duties
- to be the official representative of the FIS

602.1.2             Responsibility
The TD structure comes under the responsibility of the Alpine Committee.The Sub-Committee for Alpine Tech- nical Delegates exercises this authority.

602.1.3              Prerequisites
The TD must hold a valid TD licence (exception see art.
602.3).

602.1.4             Development

602.1.4.1     The development of a TD is:
- Applicant
- Observer at National Level FIS races
- Oral entrance examination
- Written entrance examination
- Candidate
- Practical examination ( Downhill Event acting as the

602       技术代表（TD）
602.1       定义
602.1.1       技术代表的主要职责
- 确保国际雪联的规则和指示得到遵守 ；

- 确保比赛顺利进行 ；
- 就组织方的职责范围向其提出建议 ；
- 担任国际雪联的正式代表。

602.1.2      责任
技术代表的组织结构由高山滑雪委员会负责。高山 滑雪技术代表分委员会行使该权力。


602.1.3      前提条件
技术代表须持有效的技术代表许可（例外情况参见 本规则第 602.3 条）。
602.1.4      选拔

602.1.4.1     技术代表选拔过程如下 ：
- 申请 ；
- 成为国家级国际雪联比赛观察员 ；
- 口试 ；
- 笔试 ；
- 成为候选人 ；
- 实践考核（在滑降比赛中担任副裁判长）；

Assistant Referee)
- Practical examination (Giant Slalom or Slalom acting as TD)
- TD
The FIS recommends that the National Ski Associations apply a maximum age limit of 40 for applicants and 65 years for TD’s (qualifying date: 1st July).
602.1.4.2     Each National Ski Association should nominate capable
persons to train as a TD. The Sub-Committee for Alpine Technical Delegates has the final decision as to their ac- ceptance.

602.1.5             Training

602.1.5.1     The basic training of the applicant is the responsibility of each National Ski Association.
602.1.5.2     Applicants must be nominated by their respective NSA. First Year
- The applicants must attend the annual TD update course held be the NSA (June-July Southern Hemi- sphere, October-November Northern Hemisphere).
- Attend two FIS races held in their country in order to gain experience under the supervision of the TD Com- missioner or an appointed representative.
- Complete official reports for these assignments and send them to their TD Commissioner, with copies to the FIS (in an official language).

- 实践考核（在大回转或回转比赛中担任技术代表）；

- 成为技术代表。
国际雪联建议，国家滑雪协会对申请人的最高年龄 限制为40岁，对技术代表的最高年龄限制为65岁（有 效日期 ：7 月 1 日）。
602.1.4.2     各国家滑雪协会应选拔本协会有能力的人员作为技 术代表培养对象，高山滑雪技术代表分委员会有权 最终决定是否接纳他们。
602.1.5      培训

602.1.5.1     申请人的基本培训由各国家滑雪协会负责。



602.1.5.2     申请人必须由其各自所属的国家滑雪协会提名。
第一年
- 申请人必须参加每年由国家滑雪协会举办的技术代 表进修课程（南半球 6 至 7 月，北半球 10 至 11 月）。

- 参加两次在申请者本国举办的国际雪联比赛，以便 在技术代表专员或指定的代表的监督下积累经验。

- 完成有关上述任务的正式报告，并将报告原件送交 其所属的技术代表专员，同时将复印件送交国际雪 联（使用一种国际雪联的官方语言）。

2nd Section   Rules Common to Alpine Events 第二部分    高山滑雪竞赛通则






- At the end of the season the NSA applies to the FIS for official acceptance of the applicant, copy to the TD Commissioner.
Second Year
- The applicant must attend the annual national TD update.
- Must pass the written and oral entrance examination conducted in an official FIS language.
As a Candidate
Is assigned under the supervision of a TD Examiner (from another country) to a:
- Practical examination (Downhill event acting as the Assistant Referee)
- Practical examination (Giant Slalom or Slalom and act- ing as the TD)
- If an event consists of more than one competition the examination starts with the arrival according to 602.4.3 and has to be executed on the first competition day.
- Complete official reports for these assignments and send them to the TD Commissioner, with copies to the FIS (in an official language)
- The FIS Office will verify all the information from the dif- ferent reports from the candidate and examiners and provide such details as necessary to the Sub-Committee for TDs.
- The Sub-Committee may decide not to issue a TD licence if the candidate has not completed all require- ments or is deemed to be unsuitable. In this event the Sub-Committee may decide as to whether the candidate may continue to train as a FIS TD and which parts of the procedure have to be repeated.

- 在赛季末，国家滑雪协会向国际雪联申请正式接纳 申请人，并将复印件发送技术代表专员。

第二年
- 申请人必须参加年度国家技术代表进修培训。
- 必须通过以国际雪联官方语言之一进行的笔试和 口试。
身为候选人
被指派在技术代表审查员（来自另一国家）的监督 下参加 ：
- 实践考核（滑降比赛中担任副裁判长）；

- 实践考核（在大回转或回转比赛中担任技术代表）；

- 如果一项赛事由多场比赛组成，则考核将从 602.4.3 规定的到达开始，且必须在第一个比赛日进行 ；

- 完成有关上述任务的正式报告，将报告原件送交 其技术代表专员，同时将复印件送交国际雪联（使 用一种官方语言）；
- 国际雪联办公室将对来自候选人和审查员的不同 报告中的全部信息进行审查，并将必要的详细信息 送交技术代表分委员会 ；
- 候选人未符合所有要求或被判定不符合资格的，分 委员会有权决定不颁发技术代表许可。随后，分委 员会有权决定候选人是否可以继续作为国际雪联 技术代表的培养对象，以及哪些程序应该重来。

COMPETITION RULES (ICR)


- If the candidates are considered to be suitable they will become official FIS Alpine Technical Delegates after the next TD update course.

602.1.5.3     At any event only one TD candidate may serve with a TD. Exceptions can be authorised by the FIS.

602.1.5.4     The assignment of the TD candidates is conducted, on proposal of the national responsible officials for TD questions, by the FIS, which also checks the perfor- mances ofthe individual candidates.
602.1.5.5     The TD candidate has no right to reimbursement of costs

602.1.5.6     TDs are responsible for training the candidate assigned to them.

602.1.6             Licence
The licence is a numbered identification document val- id for 12 months. It must be renewed each year and is obligatory for every TD.

602.1.7             Further Training and Expiration of Licence
Every licensed TD must take part annually in a further training course supervised by FIS. TDs will lose their licence if they miss two consecutive TD updates or miss two years’assignments and can show no good reason for their absence. To regain their licence they must once again undergo the TD Candidate procedures.

2nd Section   Rules Common to Alpine Events 第二部分    高山滑雪竞赛通则


- 被认定合格的候选人参加完下一次技术代表进修 课程后，成为正式的国际雪联高山滑雪技术代表。


602.1.5.3     每一赛事只能有 1 名技术代表候选人与 1 名技术代 表一起工作。但国际雪联有权准予例外。

602.1.5.4     根据成员国家滑雪协会负责技术代表事务官员的建 议，国际雪联实施技术代表候选人的配置工作，并 检查各候选人的实际表现。


602.1.5.5      技术代表候选人无权要求报销费用。

602.1.5.6     技术代表负责培训分配给他的技术代表候选人。


602.1.6      证书
技术代表许可证书是一份编号的身份证明文件，有  效期 12个月。每位技术代表有义务每年更新其许可。


602.1.7       继续培训与证书有效期
每位持证的技术代表必须参加每年由国际雪联督办 的培训课程。如果连续 2 次未参加培训或 2 年未被 委任工作，且无缺席的正当理由，技术代表将失去 其许可。若想重新获得许可，须按技术代表候选人 的选拔程序重新申请。

COMPETITION RULES (ICR)

2nd Section   Rules Common to Alpine Events 第二部分    高山滑雪竞赛通则






602.2          Appointment

602.2.1             For Olympic Winter Games, FIS World  Ski Champi- onships and FIS Junior World Ski Championships the appointment is made by the FIS Council on recommen- dation of the Alpine Committee.

602.2.2             For all other competitions, the appointment is made by the Sub-Committee for Alpine Technical Delegates.

602.2.3             An exception is made for Youth, CIT, Masters, World Cup DAR, DAR, CISM, Customs and UNI races, for which the TD’s are proposed by the Sub-Committee in question and confirmed by the Sub-Committee for Al- pine Technical Delegates.

602.2.4      A TD cannot be member of the organising association.     In exceptional cases the Sub-Committee for Alpine Technical Delegates may appoint a TD from the same country. The TD must, however, not be a member of the organising club or of the regional association.

602.3           TD Replacement

602.3.1             If the TD for Olympic Winter Games, FIS World  Ski Championships or FIS Junior World Ski Championships is unable to serve, the FIS Council as well as the National Ski Association to which the TD belongs must be notified. The FIS Council must appoint another TD immediately.

602.2       技术代表的任命
602.2.1             冬季奥林匹克运动会、国际雪联世界锦标赛和国际 雪联世界青少年锦标赛的技术代表由高山滑雪委员 会推荐，国际雪联理事会任命。


602.2.2             所有其他比赛的技术代表由高山滑雪技术代表分委 员会任命。

602.2.3             作为例外，青少年赛、公民赛、大师赛、残疾人世 界杯赛、残疾人赛、国际军人运动理事会的赛事和 大学生赛等比赛的技术代表，由上述有关分委员会 提名，由高山滑雪技术代表分委员会确认。


602.2.4       技术代表不能是赛事组织方国家滑雪协会会员。
特殊情况下，高山滑雪技术代表分委员会可以从赛  事组织方国家滑雪协会会员中任命 1 名技术代表。 但该技术代表不得是作为赛事组织方的俱乐部或地 区滑雪协会的会员。
602.3       技术代表的更换
602.3.1             冬季奥林匹克运动会、国际雪联世界锦标赛或国际 雪联世界青少年滑雪锦标赛的技术代表不能履职的， 应通知国际雪联理事会以及该技术代表所属国家 滑雪协会。国际雪联理事会须立即另任命一名技 术代表。






THE INTERNATIONAL SKI
COMPETITION RULES (ICR)

2nd Section   Rules Common to Alpine Events 第二部分    高山滑雪竞赛通则






602.3.2             For all other races the National Ski Association to which the TD belongs is responsible for the immediate appoint- ment of a replacement. The Organising Committee in question and the FIS are to be informed immediately.

602.3.3             If for unforeseen reasons, a TD for the Olympic Winter Games or FIS World Ski Championships does not arrive or arrives too late at a competition and is thereby part- ly or completely unable to fulfil his/her function at the competition, a deputy is to be named by the FIS Council from amongst the members of the Jury present at the competition site.

602.3.4             At all other international races, a deputy for the absent TD is to be named on the spot by the Jury. The re- placement must likewise meet the requirements of art. 602.1.6.
In an emergency, a TD can also be named who does not meet these requirements, but is competent to ensure the conduct (or continuation) of the race. Stringent criteria must be applied when choosing this person.

602.3.5             The replacement TD has the same rights and duties as the TD originally appointed.

602.4          Organisation of the Assignments

602.4.1              The TD must establish early contact with the Organiser.

602.3.2             在所有其他比赛中，不能履职的技术代表所属国家 滑雪协会负责立即指派一名接替者，并应立即通知 相关组委会和国际雪联。


602.3.3             因无法预料的原因，冬季奥林匹克运动会和国际雪 联世界锦标赛的技术代表未能或很晚抵达比赛赛场， 以致不能完成其在比赛中的部分或全部工作任务的， 国际雪联理事会可以从已抵达比赛现场的仲裁委员 会成员中指派一位代理技术代表。



602.3.4             在所有其他国际比赛中技术代表缺席的，仲裁委员 会可以当场任命代理技术代表。代理技术代表须符 合本规则第 602.1.6 条要求。
在紧急情况下，也可以任命一位不符合上述条件但 有能力保证比赛进行（或继续）的技术代表。选择 这样的人选时应采用严格的标准。


602.3.5             代理技术代表具有与原技术代表同样的权利与义务。


602.4       赛事组织工作的安排
602.4.1             技术代表必须尽早与组织方建立联系。

COMPETITION RULES (ICR)

2nd Section   Rules Common to Alpine Events 第二部分    高山滑雪竞赛通则






602.4.2             Cancellations or postponements of events must be an- nounced to the TD and to the FIS immediately, taking into account any applicable deadlines.

602.4.3             For Downhill and  Super-G, the TD must arrive at the competition site at least 48 hours before the draw for the first training. In all other events this must be at least 24 hours before the draw for the event concerned.

602.5           Expense Accounts
The TD2) has a right to reimbursement for travel expens- es up to a maximum of CHF 600.--1) (highway taxes included), as well as free accommodation and meals during the assignment. This rule also applies to agreed inspections as well as the trip to the competition (train, first class; for longer distances air fare, tourist class; or payment of a per kilometre fee of CHF 0.70 or equiva- lent).
In addition a fixed daily rate of CHF 100. -- is added for the travel days to and from, as well as each day of the assignment, which includes postage charges for mailing reports, etc. Double charges (e.g. travelling home on the same day as the last race) are not permitted. If overnight accommodation during the journey to and from the as- signment is necessary, this must be justified and reim- bursed separately.
1) The maximum payment ofCHF 600. -- is valid for all races except Olympic Winter Games, World Cup and Continental Cup.

602.4.2             如需取消或延期比赛，必须立即通报技术代表和国
际雪联，同时要考虑到可适用的期限。


602.4.3             在滑降和超级大回转比赛中，技术代表必须至少在 第一次训练的抽签前 48 小时到达比赛场地。在所有 其他比赛项目中，必须至少在相关比赛抽签前 24 小 时到达比赛场地。
602.5       费用帐目
技术代表2 ）有权报销交通费，最高为 600瑞士法郎 1 ） （含高速公路费），履职期间的食宿免费。这项规则
也适用于经双方同意的视察及相应的到比赛场地的 旅行（火车头等车厢 ；长途飞行经济舱 ；或付给每 公里 0.70 瑞士法郎或等值货币）。



另外还须支付固定的每日（包括履职的每一天以及 往返旅行日） 100 瑞士法郎的履职补助费，其中包 括邮寄工作报告的邮费等。不得重复支付费用（如 在比赛最后一天就回到了家）。往返旅途中的过夜住 宿费必须正当合理，并单独报销。



1) 最高支付 600 瑞士法郎。适用于除冬季奥林匹克 运动会、世界杯和洲际杯外的所有比赛。

603           Course Setter

603.1           Prerequisites

603.1.1             For Olympic Winter Games, FIS World Ski Champion- ships and World Cup:
- nomination by the National Ski Association team cap- tain to the Coaches Working Group and
- proof of appropriate experience in the setting of cours- es for World Cup events, Olympic Winter Games or FIS World Ski Championships

603.1.2             For all other competitions entered in the FIS Calendar:
- Continental Cup: Nomination from National Ski Asso- ciations to Cup Coordinators or Working Group.
- All other events in the FIS Calendar: Nomination through the Jury or Organising Committee

603.1.3             For Downhill’s, the course setter must be familiar with
the particular competition course.

603.2          Appointment

603.2.1             For Olympic Winter Games, FIS World Ski Champion- ships and World Cups, the appointment is made after examination by the Chief Race Director.

- 由国家滑雪协会领队向赛会竞赛组提名 ；
- 证明有在世界杯、冬季奥林匹克运动会和国际雪联 世界锦标赛旗门设计的实践经验。



603.1.2             对于纳入《国际雪联竞赛日历》中的所有其他比赛：

603.2.2             For European Cup, the EC Coordinator appoints the course setters.

603.2.3             For all other competitions included in the FIS Calendar, the appointment is made by the Jury. For competitions consisting of two runs, each run is to be set by a differ- ent course setter. One of the two course setters may be named by the organiser.

603.3           Supervision of the Course Setters

603.3.1             The work of the course setters is supervised by the Jury.

603.4          Organisation of the Assignment
For Olympic Winter Games, FIS World Ski Champion- ships and World Cup races the course setter assignment is managed by the Chief Race Director. For European Cup races the course setter assignment is managed by the EC Coordinator. For all remaining races the assign- ment is managed by the Jury.

603.5           Replacement of Course Setters

603.5.1             For Olympic Winter Games and FIS World Ski Cham- pionships, the Chief Race Director names a replacement course setter immediately, details of which are published by the FIS Office.

603.5.2             For all other competitions entered in the FIS Calendar,

603.2.2             欧洲杯，由其杯赛协调员任命。


603.2.3              《国际雪联竞赛日历》其他所有国际比赛，由仲裁 委员会任命。比赛包括两轮滑行的，每轮滑行的线 路应由不同的旗门设计员设计，其中的一名可由组 织方任命。


603.3       对旗门设计员的监督
603.3.1             旗门设计员的工作由仲裁委员会监督。
603.4       责任分工的安排
冬季奥林匹克运动会、国际雪联世界滑雪锦标赛和  世界杯的旗门设计员的职责分工由竞赛总主任负责。 欧洲杯的旗门设计员的职责分工由欧洲杯协调员负 责。其余所有比赛由仲裁委员会负责。



603.5       旗门设计员的递补
603.5.1            在冬季奥林匹克运动会和国际雪联世界锦标赛中， 递补旗门设计员由竞赛主任立即任命，具体内容由 国际雪联办公室发布。


603.5.2             对于其他纳入《国际雪联竞赛日历》中的所有比赛，

the Jury names a replacement course setter.

603.5.3             The replacement course setter should have the same
qualifications as the original course setter

603.6          Rights of the Course Setter

603.6.1             To recommend the introduction of changes in the com- petition terrain and in the safety measures.

603.6.2             Availability of a sufficient number of helpers for the set- ting of the course,  so that the course setter can concen- trate solely on the course setting.

603.6.3            Provision of all necessary materials by the chief of course equipment.

603.6.4             Immediate completion of the finishing touches to the
race course.

603.7           Duties of the Course Setter

603.7.1             In order to set the course appropriately, respecting the terrain, the snow cover and the ability of the participat- ing competitors, the course setter conducts a pre-inspec- tion of the race terrain in the presence of the TD, the Referee, the Chief of Race, and the Chief of Course.

603.7.2             The course setter sets the course respecting the existing safety measures and course preparation. The course setter

2nd Section   Rules Common to Alpine Events 第二部分    高山滑雪竞赛通则


由仲裁委员会任命递补旗门设计员。

603.5.3             递补旗门设计员应具备与原旗门设计员相同的资质。


603.6      旗门设计员的权利
603.6.1             有权建议对旗门的地形和安全设施进行调整。


603.6.2       为使旗门设计员集中精力只进行旗门设计，必须为 其提供足够多的助手来具体落实旗门设计。


603.6.3       设备长应提供所有必需品。


603.6.4             及时完成旗门设计的收尾工作。


603.7       旗门设计员的职责
603.7.1       为合理设计比赛线路，要考虑到地形、积雪、参赛  运动员的滑雪技能等情况，旗门设计员应和技术代  表、裁判长、竞赛长、赛道长一起预视察赛道的地形。



603.7.2       旗门设计员设计比赛线路应考虑现有的安全措施和
赛道的前期准备工作，必须考虑速度控制。

COMPETITION RULES (ICR)

must take speed control into consideration.

603.7.3             All courses must be set according to the ICR


603.7.4             The courses must be set and ready in time, so that the competitors are not disturbed during course inspection.

603.7.5             The course setters should take care that the difference between the winning times of each run of Slalom and Giant Slalom will not be too great.

603.7.6             The course setting is a task of the course setter alone, who is responsible for adhering to the rules of the ICR and may be advised by members of the Jury, and by the technical advisor in Downhill and Super-G, if present.

603.7.7             The course setters must participate in all team captains ’ meetings at which a report is to be made about the course.

603.8          Arrival at the Race Site

603.8.1             For Downhill and Super-G races, this should be no later     than the morning of the day of the first team captains ’ meeting, so that if required any additional course prepa-     ration or safety measures can be implemented.

603.8.2            For  Slalom  and Giant  Slalom races if possible this should be the day before, but always before the first team captains’meeting.



603.7.3       所有比赛线路的设计必须按照《国际雪联滑雪竞赛 规则》进行设计。

603.7.4       比赛线路要按时完成设计并准备就绪，以免干扰运 动员视察线路。

603.7.5             旗门设计员应该注意，回转和大回转每一轮滑行中 获胜者用时的差别不宜太大。


603.7.6       旗门设计是旗门设计员本人的任务，必须遵守《国 际雪联滑雪竞赛规则》，仲裁委员会成员、滑降和超 级大回转技术顾问如果在场，可以向旗门设计员提 出建议。

603.7.7       旗门设计员须参加每次领队会议，并在会上报告比 赛线路的设计情况。

603.8       到达比赛场所
603.8.1            对于滑降和超级大回转比赛，旗门设计员应不迟于 召开第一次领队会议的当天早晨到达比赛场地，以 便在需要时进行额外的赛道准备或安全措施调整等 工作。

603.8.2       对于回转和大回转比赛，如有可能，旗门设计员应 再提前一天到达比赛场地，但必须早于第一次领队 会议。

604           Accreditation / Rights and Duties of Team Officials

604.1           Officials, Medical* and Technical Personnel
Quotas for the right of access to the closed race course:
- up to 3 competitors: 3 trainers 2 doctors* 2 technicians

- 4 or 5 competitors: 4 trainers 2 doctors* 3 technicians

- 6 to 10 competitors: 5 trainers 2 doctors* 4 technicians  As well as representatives of the FIS in an official capacity.  These quotas include the national team officials (team captains, etc.).
These persons must be identified by armband or another clearly visible accreditation. If necessary, the Jury can re- duce these quotas, Cup Rules can determine special quotas.  The persons accredited according to art. 220.3 and 220.5, as well as the official technicians and medical personnel must comply with the directions of the officials charged by the organisers with responsibility for overall security (e.g.: stewards, police, etc.).
The instructions given by the Jury to accredited journal- ists, coaches and team captains have priority in all cases. *) Medical personnel includes doctors, physiotherapists, first aid people etc.

604.2           Team Captains and Trainers
The team captains and trainers must be accredited by the organisers according to quota. The accreditation gives

604       随队官员的注册及其权利与职责


604.1            官员、医务人员 * 和技术人员
有权进入封闭赛道的人员配额 ：
- 不足 3 名参赛运动员的 ：3 名教练员 2 名医生 * 2 名技术人员
- 4 到 5 名参赛运动员 ：4 名教练员 2 名医生 * 3 名 技术人员
- 6 到 10 名参赛运动员 ：5 名教练员 2 名医生 * 4 名 技术人员
以及具备官方身份的国际雪联代表。
上述配额包括国家队官员（领队等）。
所有获得配额的人员须佩戴袖章或其他显著的用于 识别的注册证件。如有必要，仲裁委员会可以减少 上述配额，国际雪联的杯赛规则可设定特别配额。
依照本规则第 220.3 条和 220.5 条注册的人员以及官 方技术人员和医务人员，须服从组织方委任的负责 整体安全的官员（管理人员、警察等）的指挥。


仲裁委员会给注册记者、教练员及领队下达的指令 在任何情况下都应当优先遵守。
*) 医务人员包括医生、理疗师、急救人员等。

In accordance with ICR 213.4 and 216 the time and loca- tion of the first team captain’s meeting and of the draw must be shown in the program.
An actual meeting, attended in person or held online, by team captains, jury, and race officials is an inseparable part of the competition and is important for communica- tion of jury instructions, support of the OC, OC requests and information as well as a critical element for risk management and liability related matters. 由领队、仲裁委员会委员和竞赛官员本人实际参加 的会议，是比赛不可分割的一部分，对传达仲裁委 员会的指令、支持组委会、通报组委会的要求和信 息等都具有重要的意义，也是风险管理和有关责任 事项的关键因素。本规则第 216 条和第 217 条规定 适用于所有情况。

604.4           Entries and Draw

604.4.1             The Organiser must determine the final date of entry (art.
213.8) between 48 h and 24 h (art. 215. 1) before the first Team Captains’Meeting.
604.4.2              A Team Captain may only make substitutions before the Draw.

604.4.3             The event programme as determined in art. 213 must be published on the FIS website alpine competition calendar.

605           Forerunners
605.1           The organiser is obliged to provide at least three forerun- ners who have signed the FIS Athletes Declaration. The forerunner is a member of the Organising Committee. In Downhill, the forerunners should participate in 46 all training runs. In extraordinary conditions, the Jury may increase the number of forerunners.
The Jury may designate different forerunners for each run.

605.2           The forerunners must wear forerunners’start numbers (bibs).
605.3           The nominated forerunners should have the skiing abili- ty to ski the course in a racing manner.

605.4           Forerunners are not permitted to start in the competition.
605.5           The Jury determines the forerunners and their start order. After an interruption of the race additional  forerunners

604.4       报名与抽签
604.4.1             组织方必须在首次领队会议前 24 至 48 小时（本
规则第 215.1 条）确定报名截止日期（本规则第 213.8 条）。
604.4.2              替换领队只能在抽签前进行。

604.4.3             本规则第 213 条确定的比赛项目秩序册必须在国际 雪联官网高山滑雪竞赛日历中公布。

605       试滑员
605.1      组织者有义务提供至少 3 名已签署国际雪联《运动 员宣言》的试滑员。试滑员是组委会的成员。在滑 降比赛中，试滑员须参加所有轮次的滑行训练。在 特殊情况下，仲裁委员会可以增加试滑员的人数。


仲裁委员会可以为每轮滑行指定不同的试滑员。

605.2      试滑员必须佩戴试滑员出发号码（号码布）。
605.3      被任命的试滑员应具备以比赛方式滑完全程的滑雪 能力。

605.4      试滑员不得再参加相应比赛。
605.5      仲裁委员会确定每轮滑行的试滑员及其出发顺序。 比赛暂停后，如果需要可额外增加试滑员。

607.1           The FIS competition year is July  1st - June 30th of the following year.
In order to compete in international competitions (ex- cept U 16 - U 14 competitions) a competitor must be no younger than age group U 18.

607.2           International junior competitions are restricted to U 18 and U21 age group. (Exception National Junior Champi- onship)

608.4           Quota regulations

608.4.1             The quota per nation is max. 4 (four) U 14 and 6 (six) U 16 resulting in the total number of max. 10 competing athletes per nation. No more than 4 (four) athletes of the same gender may be registered within each category. The organising nation is entitled to a double quota that is maximum 20 competing athletes. In case of events with- in multiple races the quota is for the event and not for the race.
608.4.2             Under normal circumstances, the max. number of com- peting athletes must not exceed 140 per category and gender.

608.4.3             Pursuant to Rules of the FIS Alpine Points, the organ- ising nation may register more than the double quota of participants other nations may also register more than the double quota, by invitation.

608.4.4            If the organising nation is unable to fill their legiti- mate quota other nations may be invited to participate with a double quota, at the invitation of the organising nation.

608.4       配额规定
608.4.1             各国配额最多 4 名 U14 和 6 名U16，即每个国家最 多 10 名运动员参赛。每一组别的注册人数中，性别 相同的运动员不得超过 4 名。主办国有权获得最多
20 名参赛运动员的双倍配额。如果赛事包括多个比 赛项目（小项），配额是针对比赛项目（小项），而 不是针对该赛事。



608.4.2             通常情况下，参加每个比赛项目的每个组别和性别 的运动员不能超过 140 人。


608.4.3       根据《国际雪联高山滑雪积分规则》，比赛组织国可 以注册多于 2 倍配额的参赛运动员 ；通过邀请，其 他国家也可以注册多于 2 倍配额的参赛运动员。


608.4.4       比赛组织国参赛运动员未能凑满配额的，其他国家 应比赛组织国的邀请，可以 2 倍配额的运动员参赛。

608.5          Allotment into groups and start order

608.5.1             In each group each participating nation is allotted one starting place max.

608.5.2             If more than  15 nations have registered, the following principles apply:
> Group 1: The first group will contain one athlete from each nation registered. Each nation is allotted one start place only.
> Group 2 - 3 - 4: Same as group 1.
> Last group: The last group consists of athletes from the or- ganising nation, with its double quota. If the total number of competing athletes is thereby exceeded, a separate last group will be formed, using the same procedure as in Group 1.
608.5.3             In U 16 - U 14 races with few participants (see art.
608.5.4), the draw follows the principles described for the double quota of organising nations.

608.5.4             The team leaders are responsible for the identification of participants in each group.

608.5.5             Each group is drawn separately

608.5.6              Start order 2nd runs - The best 30 of the 1st run start in the reversed order.
608.5.7             Specific starting orders approved by the Yout h  and

608.5     分组和出发顺序
608.5.1             每组每个参赛国最多分得 1 个出发位置。


608.5.2             注册参赛国家超过 15 个的，适用如下原则 ：

> 第 1 组 ：包含每个注册参赛国家的 1 名运动员。
每个国家只能分得 1 个出发位置。

> 第 2-3-4 组 ：同第 1 组。
> 最后 1 组 ：由拥有 2 倍配额的组织方国家的运动 员组成。参赛运动员的总数因此超额的，采用与 第 1 组相同的程序另外建立一个最后 1 组。


608.5.3       在参赛人数较少的 U16-U14 比赛中（参见本规则第
608.5.4 条），抽签遵循组织方国家拥有双倍配额的 原则。

608.5.4              队伍管理者负责每一组别运动员的身份确认工作。

608.5.5             各组单独抽签。


608.5.6       第 2 轮滑行出发顺序 ：第 1 轮滑行成绩前 30 名选手 倒序出发。

608.5.7             经青少年和儿童分委员会批准的特别出发顺序，可

608.6           U16 - U14 Events
608.6.1             U 16 - U 14 events may include  Slalom, Giant  Slalom, Super-G, Parallel, Kombi events, team competition (e.g. Mixed Team Parallel).

608.6.2             Except where noted in ICR 608 for Youth the Alpine Rules in ICR are to be followed.
608.6.3             Team competitions may be conducted for U 14 and U 16. Such team competitions should be described as“Specifi- cations for Youth Team Competitions”.
608.6.3.1     For the team evaluation, only the team declared at the first team captains meeting as“A”will be considered.

608.7           Equipment

608.7.1             All equipment used by Youth is governed by the FIS Specifications for Competition Equipment.

608.7.2             Youth are required to wear a crash helmet that conforms to the FIS Specifications for Competition Equipment.

608.8           Parallel Events
The FIS ICR for the running of Parallel (art.  1220) applies.

608.6       U16 - U14 赛事
608.6.1              U 16-U14 比赛项目可包括回转、大回转、超级大回转、 平行式比赛、组合赛、团体赛（如混合队式平行式  比赛）。

608.6.2             应当遵守《国际雪联竞赛规则》第 608 条有关青少 年高山滑雪的例外规定。

608.6.3             U14 和 U16 可以组织团体比赛。这种团体赛应称为 “青年团体赛具体规定”。


608.6.3.1     团队评估只考虑在第一次团队领队会议上宣布为 “A”的团队。
608.7       竞赛器材

608.7.2             青少年运动员必须穿戴符合《国际雪联竞赛器材具 体规定》防护头盔。

608.8       平行式比赛
适用《国际雪联竞赛规则有关举办平行式比赛的规 则（本规则第 1220 条）。






THE INTERNATIONAL SKI
COMPETITION RULES (ICR)

2nd Section   Rules Common to Alpine Events 第二部分    高山滑雪竞赛通则






608.9           Kombi
The U 16 - U 14 Kombi is an internationally recognized event that consists of a mixture of standard turns and gates. The event meets developmental needs for this age group, creating a tactical awareness by blending sections of different gates in a flowing, rhythmical, constantly changing pattern. Results may be determined by com- bined times of each run, or each run may be classified separately. The OC must indicate the method in advance.

608.9.1             Course Setting

608.9.1.2     The Course Setter and Jury are to provide an interesting and controlled course.
608.9.1.3     The competitor’s speed must be controlled when tran- sitioning from one section to a different section and the course setting should allow skiers a smooth transition from jumps or waves back into the course.

608.9.2             Kombi Design
There can be 2 different forms of the Kombi:
SL / GS Format (technical orientation) Setting with stubbies, SL gates and GS gates or coloured ground in- dicators and GS / SG Format (speed orientation). Setting with GS and SG gates or coloured ground indicators.
The selected race style must be announced on the race notice prior to the race and again at the first team cap- tains meeting.

608.9       组合赛
U 16-U14 组合赛是一项国际承认的比赛，由一系列 不同标准弯道和旗门组合而成。这项比赛满足了这 一年龄段的发展需要，通过将包括多个旗门的不同 旗门组以一种流畅的、有节奏的、不断变化的模式 混合在一起，创造一种战术意识。比赛成绩可以根 据各轮滑行的总时间确定，或者每轮滑行单独决胜 负。组委会必须提前说明竞赛模式。


608.9.1      旗门设计
608.9.1.2     旗门设计员和仲裁委员会应提供一条有趣且安全的 线路。

608.9.1.3      当选手从一个旗门组切换到另一个旗门组时必须能 够控制速度，且比赛线路的设计必须能让选手从跳 跃或波浪部分流畅地切换回比赛线路。


608.9.2      组合赛设计
组合赛可以有两种不同的模式 ：
回转 / 大回转组合模式（技术偏好）：旗门设置用短 杆，回转和大回转旗门或彩色地面指示标。大回转 / 超级大回转模式（速度偏好）：旗门设置用大回转和 超级大回转旗门或彩色地面指示标。
必须在赛前的竞赛公告中公布拟采用的竞赛组合模 式，第一次领队会议时应再次通告。






THE INTERNATIONAL SKI
COMPETITION RULES (ICR)

2nd Section   Rules Common to Alpine Events 第二部分    高山滑雪竞赛通则






608.9.3             SL / GS Kombi: Technical Data
Slalom Skis are recommended to be used for SL/GS Kombi and the OC must announce in advance the type of Kombi in order to enable correct ski selection.
608.9.3.1     Terrain and Vertical drop.
Use U 16 - U 14 GS slope, vertical drop between 140 -
200 meters
608.9.3.2     Gates
Gates consist of two poles. The outside gate must be the same type as the turning gate (stubby gate with stubby gate, SL gate with SL gate, GS panel with GS panel)
- Consecutive gates must alternate in red and blue.
- SL gates must have a minimum distance of 4m and max. 6m.
- GS gates must have a minimum distance of 4m and a max. 8m.
- SL Minimum distance between turning gate to turning gate 0.75m.
- SL Maximum distance turning gate to turning gate 12m.
- GS Minimum distance turning gate to turning gate. No minimum restriction
- GS Maximum distance turning gate to turning gate 20m.
608.9.3.3     Course characteristics and recommendations:
- Minimum of 30 turns

608.9.3       回转 / 大回转组合赛 ：技术数据
回转 / 大回转组合赛建议使用回转滑雪板，组委 会必须提前宣布组合赛的模式，以便选择正确的 滑雪板。
608.9.3.1     地形和垂直落差
采用 U 16 - U14 大回转坡道，垂直落差在 140 米至 200 米之间。
608.9.3.2     旗门
旗门由 2 根旗杆组成。外侧旗门和转弯旗门必须规 格相同（短杆旗门布搭配短杆旗门，回转旗门布搭 配回转旗门，大回转旗门布搭配大回转旗门）。
- 连续的旗门必须红蓝交替。
- 回转旗门间距最少 4 米，最多 6 米。

- 大回转旗门间距最少 4 米，最多 8 米。

- 回转转弯旗门之间最小间距为 0.75 米。

- 回转转弯旗门之间最大间距为 12 米。

- 大回转转弯旗门之间没有最小距离限制。

- 大回转转弯旗门之间最大间距为 20 米。


608.9.3.3     比赛线路特点与建议 ：
- 最少 30 个转弯。





THE INTERNATIONAL SKI
COMPETITION RULES (ICR)


- Recommended to have a minimum of 5 different sections.
- Slalom skis recommended
- The course should test the skier’s ability to react and adapt to an ever changing rhythm and radius, but allow the competitors smooth transition between the various sections of gates.
- Building terrain is optional but not necessary as the course itself should apply enough demand. Use creativ- ity with available terrain.
- Include a minimum of one jump
- Avoid gates that cause sudden braking and deceleration.
- Use the entire slope and natural terrain and skiing across the fall line as often as possible
- It is recommended to use only a single pole for vertical combinations
- The first and last gates should give the competitor the general direction.
- There should be at least one section of stubby gates.
- Forerunners or course testers should be available for course setting.

608.9.4             GS / SG Kombi: Technical Data
Giant Slalom Skis are recommended to be used for GS/ SG Kombi and the OC must announce in advance the type of Kombi in order to enable correct ski selection.

608.9.4.1     Terrain and Vertical drop.
Use homologated GS course, 250 meters maximum ver- tical drop.

2nd Section   Rules Common to Alpine Events 第二部分    高山滑雪竞赛通则


- 建议最少设 5 个不同的旗门组。
- 建议使用回转滑雪板。
- 比赛线路应该检测滑雪者对不断变化的节奏和转 弯半径的反应和适应能力，但要能让选手在不同旗 门组的旗门之间流畅转换。

- 可以改造赛道地形，但不是必需的，赛道本身应充 分满足需要。要创造性地利用现有的可用地形。

- 至少包含一处跳跃。
- 应避免造成急停和减速的旗门。
- 利用整个坡道和自然地形，引导运动员尽可能连续 地穿越滚落线。
- 在设计垂直组合时建议仅使用单旗门杆。

- 第一组旗门和最后一组旗门应给参赛运动员指明 基本的方向。
- 应至少有一个旗门组用短杆旗门。
- 试滑员或线路检验员应随时待命、保障旗门设计。


608.9.4              大回转 / 超级大回转组合赛 ：技术数据
大回转 / 超级大回转组合赛建议选用大回转滑雪板， 组委会必须提前宣布组合赛的模式，以便准备适宜 的滑雪板。
608.9.4.1     地势和垂直落差
使用经认证的大回转赛道，垂直落差最大 250 米。






THE INTERNATIONAL SKI
COMPETITION RULES (ICR)

2nd Section   Rules Common to Alpine Events 第二部分    高山滑雪竞赛通则






608.9.4.2     Gates
- Gates consist of two poles. Outside gate must be the same as turning gate.
- Consecutive gates must alternate in red and blue.
- GS gates must have a minimum distance of 4m and a max. 8m.
- SG gates must have a minimum distance of 6m and a max 8m.
- GS turning gate to turning gate minimum 10m maxi- mum 20m
- SG turning gate to turning gate minimum 15m maxi- mum 28m
608.9.4.3     Course characteristics and recommendations:
- Number of Direction changes 10% to 12% of Vertical drop.
- Recommended to have 3-5 different sections.
- Giant Slalom skis recommended.
- The course should test the skier’s ability to react and adapt to an ever changing rhythm and radius, but allow the competitors smooth transition between the various sections of gates.
- Building terrain is optional but must allow course to ﬂow smoothly.
- Include a minimum of one jump
- Avoid gates that cause sudden braking and deceleration.
- The first and last gates should give the competitor the general direction.
- Forerunners or course testers should be available for course setting.

608.9.4.2     旗门
- 旗门由 2 根旗杆组成。外侧旗门和转弯旗门必须 相同。
- 连续的旗门必须红蓝交替。
- 大回转旗门间距须最少 4 米，最多 8 米。

- 超级大回转旗门间距须最少 6 米，最多 8 米。

- 大回转转弯旗门之间距离为最少 10 米，最多 20 米。

- 超级大回转转弯旗门之间距离为最少 15 米，最多 28 米。

608.9.4.3      比赛线路特点与建议 ：
- 换向次数在垂直落差的 10% 到 12% 之间。
- 建议设 3 到 5 个不同旗门组。
- 建议使用大回转滑雪板。
- 比赛线路应该检验滑雪者对不断变化的节奏和转 弯半径的反应和适应能力，但要能让选手在不同旗 门组的旗门之间流畅转换。

- 可以改造地形，但必须使线路保持流畅。

- 至少包含一处跳跃。
- 应避免造成急停和减速的旗门。
- 第一组旗门和最后一组旗门应给参赛运动员指明 基本的方向。
- 试滑员或线路检验员应随时待命、保障旗门设计。






THE INTERNATIONAL SKI
COMPETITION RULES (ICR)

2nd Section   Rules Common to Alpine Events 第二部分    高山滑雪竞赛通则






608.9.5             Kombi Inspection
A normal competitor’s inspection and with a time limit established by the Jury is suggested. The concept is to test reaction and adaptability from the normal amount of inspection time.

608.9.6             Number of runs
The OC and Jury should decide on the number of runs by the first team captains meeting. Depending on weath- er and course conditions it is recommended that entries up to 140 competitors should be 2 runs and entries over
140 competitors should be one run.

608.9.7              Rules
The ICR Slalom and Giant Slalom rules apply for run- ning of the Kombi race except as modified in art. 608.

608.9.8             Starting order
By team seeding.

608.9.9             Gate judging
A sufficient number of gate judges should be present. For the Stubby sections it is recommended to have one gate judge for every two gates. It is also recommended to spray a blue line on the inside of the gate to help to identify straddles.

608.9.5       组合赛线路视察
建议安排常规的运动员视察线路活动，时限由仲裁 委员会确定。目的是检测运动员在常规视察线路时 限内所作的反应和适应能力。


608.9.6      滑行轮次数
组委会和仲裁委员会应在第一次领队会议前决定滑 行轮次数。根据天气情况和赛道条件，建议在报名 参赛运动员不到 140 名时采取 2 轮滑行，超过 140 名时采取 1 轮滑行。


608.9.7       规则
本规则有关回转和大回转的规则可用于组合赛，但 本规则第 608 条特别调整的内容除外。
608.9.8       出发顺序
依据代表队排名确定。

608.9.9      旗门裁判
应当配备足够数量的旗门裁判员。建议在短杆旗门 组每 2 个旗门设置 1 个旗门裁判员，在旗门内侧喷 涂蓝线以便选手确认是否正确越过旗门。

610            Start, Finish, Timing and Calculations

611            Technical Installations

611.1          Communications & Cabling
In all international competitions, it is highly recom- mended that there is multiple communications (telephone or radios, etc.) between the Start and Finish. Voice com- munication between Start and Finish must be assured by fixed wire connection or radio. In case of radio, this must be on a separate channel from that used by any oth- er function of the OC.
In Olympic Winter Games and FIS World Champion- ships all communications and timing connections be- tween Start and Finish must be assured by fixed wiring.

611.2         Timing Equipment
For all events in the FIS Calendar, electronic timers, start gates and photocells homologated by the FIS must be used. A list of these approved devices will be published. Races using timing equipment other than those on the homologated FIS list will not be considered for FIS points.
Specifications and procedures for timing are more fully described in a separate FIS Timing Booklet.

611.2.1             Electric Timing
For all international competitions, FIS World Cup, FIS Continental Cups and FIS competitions, two synchronised

610       起点、终点、计时与计算
611       技术设备
611.1            通讯联系与布线
在所有的国际比赛中，起点与终点之间须有多种通 讯联系（电话或对讲机等）。起点和终点的语音联系  须使用固定的有线连接或对讲机。若使用对讲机， 必须使用单独的频率，以免被组委会其他通讯内容 干扰。


在冬季奥林匹克运动会和国际雪联世界锦标赛中， 起点和终点之间所有通讯和计时连接都必须使用固 定电缆。
611.2            计时设备
所有《国际雪联竞赛日历》中的比赛，均须使用经 国际雪联认证的电子计时器、出发门及切光器。被 认证的计时设备名单应公布。参加未使用列入国 际雪联认证清单的此类计时设备比赛没有国际雪 联积分。
《国际雪联计时手册》专门对计时具体要求和程序有 更全面的说明。
611.2.1      电子计时
包括国际雪联世界杯赛、国际雪联洲际杯赛、国际 雪联比赛的所有国际比赛，应使用两套彼此独立运

COMPETITION RULES (ICR)

2nd Section   Rules Common to Alpine Events 第二部分    高山滑雪竞赛通则






electronically isolated timing systems operating in time- of-day must be used. One system will be designated system A (main system), the other system B (back-up system) prior to the beginning of the race. Only excep- tion for Parallel competitions, on Level 2, 3 and 4 where no system B is required.
Time of day times must be immediately and automati- cally sequentially recorded on printed strips at the max- imum precision of the timing device according to the requirements for homologation. The final result is cal- culated by subtracting the start time from the finish time
for each skier’s run and is then expressed to 1/100th (0.01) precision by truncating the calculated net time on course.
All times used for the final result must be from system
A. If there is a failure of system A, a calculated net time from system B must be used following the same pro- cedure as set out in art. 611.3.2.1. It is not permitted to substitute time-of-day times from system B for use with system A for the purpose of net time calculations.
For all events, system A must be connected to its re- spective start gate contact. System B must be separately connected to another electronically isolated start gate contact.
Refer to the FIS Timing Booklet for more details regard- ing cabling and complete wiring descriptions, diagrams and start gate installations.
All timing equipment and technical installation should be set up or protected in such a way that danger to the

行且电控同步的电子计时系统。赛前确定其中一套 系统为 A 系统（主系统），另一套为 B 系统（备份 系统）。仅平行式比赛为例外，第 2、3、4 级比赛不 要求有备份系统。


比赛中需要记录的时间信息，必须按照计时装置认 证所要求的最高精度、立即自动地按顺序记录并打 印。每名运动员的最终成绩是通过其结束时间减去 出发时间计算出每次滑行的赛道净用时，再四舍五 入以 1/100（0.01）秒的精度表示。



用于计算最终成绩的所有基础时间数据都必须来自 A 系统。如果 A 系统出现故障，则必须按照本规则 第 611.3.2. 1 条规定的同一程序使用 B 系统计算得出 的净时间。不允许不按本规则第 611.3.2. 1 条规定的 程序、简单地用 B 系统的时间数据代替 A 系统的时 间数据来计算净用时。
对于所有赛事，A 系统必须与各出发门相连接，B 系统也必须同样地与各出发门相连接，但必须与 A 系统电子隔离。

有关布线和完整接线说明、图表和出发门安装的更 详细信息，参见《国际雪联计时手册》。
所有计时设备和技术装置都应妥善安装并做好绝缘 等保护，避免对运动员构成危险。

competitors is avoided where possible.
Synchronisation of the timing systems must occur as close as possible to the scheduled start for the first run of the day. Synchronisation of all systems must be main- tained throughout each run. Timers must not be resyn- chronised during any run.

611.2.1.1     Start Gate
The start gate must have separate electronically isolated switch contacts for triggering the start inputs of both sys- temA & B.
If a start gate or start wand requires replacement during a run, it must be replaced with identical equipment in the same position

611.2.1.2     Photocells
For all events, there must be two photocell system(s) homologated by the FIS installed at the finish line. One is connected to systemA. The other is connected to system B. Procedures and regulations for start gates and photocells are found in the FIS Timing Booklet.

611.2.1.3     Start Clock
For DH, SG and GS, the use of a start clock that pro- vides at least an acoustic countdown signal on the fixed start interval as prescribed by the Jury should be used as an aid to race management. This is mandatory for all Level 0, 1 and 2 races.


计时系统的时间同步操作，必须尽可能邻近秩序册 中每天第一轮滑行的出发时间。在每一轮滑行过程 中都必须保持所有系统自始至终时间同步。计时器 在任何一轮滑行期间均不得重新同步。


611.2.1.1     出发门
出发门必须具有两套相互电子隔离的电子开关触点， 以触发 A 系统和 B 系统的出发时间信号输入。

如果在某轮滑行中要更换出发门或起滑杆，必须确 保在同一位置的 AB 系统更换完全相同的设备。


611.2.1.2      切光器
所有比赛的终点线上都必须安装两套经国际雪联认 证的切光系统。其中一套连接到 A 系统，另一套连 接到 B 系统。
出发门和切光器的程序和规定参见《国际雪联计时 手册》。
611.2.1.3      出发钟
在滑降、超级大回转和大回转比赛中，应至少装备 一套按仲裁委员会确定的固定出发时间间隔自动发 出倒计时信号的出发钟，用作比赛管理的辅助工具。 这是所有 0 级、1 级和 2 级比赛的强制性要求。
