COMPETITION RULES (ICR)

2nd Section   Rules Common to Alpine Events 第二部分    高山滑雪竞赛通则






611.2.2             Hand Timing
Manual (hand) timing, completely separate and indepen- dent of the electronic timing, must be used for all com- petitions listed in the FIS Calendar. Stopwatches or hand operated battery powered timers that are installed at both the Start and the Finish and capable of expressing the time of day to at least 1/100th (0.01) precision qualify as proper hand timing devices. They must be synchronised prior to the start of the first run, with the same time-of- day as system A and system B (see art. 611.2. 1). Printed records, either automatic or hand-written, of recorded hand times must be immediately available at the start and at the finish.

611.2.3              Presentation of times
Organisers should provide appropriate facilities for con- tinuous presentation of all registered times of all com- petitors.

611.2.4              Timing without Cable
For FIS Level 3 events only, it is permitted to use ho- mologated timing equipment in such a way that hill ca- ble connection between start and finish is not required. Refer to the FIS Timing Booklet for a detailed discussion of how this is possible.

611.3           Timing

611.3.1              With electronic timing, the time is taken when a competitor

611.2.2      手动计时
手动计时完全独立于电子计时，必须用于《国际雪  联竞赛日历》中的所有比赛。起点、终点处安装的  秒表或手动操作电池驱动的计时器，必须同适格的  手动计时工具一样，计时精度能够达到 1/100（0.01） 秒。手动计时器必须在第一轮滑行开始前进行同步， 与 A 系统和 B 系统运行在同一当前时间。自动或手  写的手动计时的打印记录，必须能够在出发区和终  点区立即提供。






611.2.3      时间显示
组织者应提供适当的设施，可连续显示所有运动员 已记录的滑行时间。


611.2.4      无线计时
允许在起点终点间无高山电缆连接的情况下使用经 认证的计时设备，这一规定仅适用于第 3 级别的比 赛。具体操作的详细说明见《国际雪联计时手册》。



611.3       计时
611.3.1      使用电子计时设备时，当运动员通过终点线并因切





THE INTERNATIONAL SKI
COMPETITION RULES (ICR)


crosses the finish line and triggers the beam between the photo cells.
In case of a fall at the finish where the competitor does not come to a full stop, the time can be taken without both of the competitor’s feet having crossed the finish line.
For the registered time to become valid, the competitor must immediately completely cross the finish line with or without skis. With hand timing the time will be taken when any part of the competitor crosses the finish line.     The finish controller determines the correctness of pas- sage across the finish line.

611.3.2             In the case of a failure of the main electronic timing sys- tem (system A), the results of the electronic back-up sys- tem (system B) will be valid as per art. 611.2.1. For the Olympic Winter Games, FIS World Ski Championships and FIS World Cup, a synchronised electronic timing system with printers, connected to the starting gate and to the photocells at the finish is obligatory.
In case of a failure in the lines of the timing system be- tween start and finish, this back-up system will allow the calculation of the times to 1/100ths of a second.
In the case that time of day from either system A or sys- tem B are not available for a competitor, the calculated time of day as per art. 611.3.2.1 will be considered valid.


611.3.2.1     Utilisation of times taken by hand
Hand times may be used in the official results after a

2nd Section   Rules Common to Alpine Events 第二部分    高山滑雪竞赛通则


入切光器间的光束而触发切光器时，该时间即被 记录。
运动员在终点摔倒（没有完全抵达终点）的，即 使其双腿还未完全越过终点线，其触线时间也应 被记录。
为使记录时间生效，运动员必须立即完全越过终点 线，不管有没有穿滑雪板。采用手动计时时，应记 录运动员身体的任何一部分越过终点线的时间。
终点监督员决定运动员越过终点线的正确性。



611.3.2       电子计时主系统 A 系统失灵的，根据本规则第
611.2. 1 条，备份电子计时系统 B 系统的成绩将有效。 冬季奥林匹克运动会、国际雪联世界锦标赛和国际  雪联世界杯上，必须配备一套带打印机的同步电 子计时系统与起点门和终点的切光器相连是强制 性义务。

计时系统连接起点、终点的导线失灵的，上述备份 系统可用于计算时间，精确到 1/100 秒。

计时系统中的 A 系统和 B 系统中记录的时间数据对 某个运动员而言，均无法用于计算其比赛净用时的， 则根据本规则第 611.3.2. 1 条利用手动计时系统的时 间数据的计算结果视为有效。
611.3.2.1     手动计时的使用
在算出时间修正值后，正式成绩可采用手动计时时间。






THE INTERNATIONAL SKI
COMPETITION RULES (ICR)

2nd Section   Rules Common to Alpine Events 第二部分    高山滑雪竞赛通则






correction has been calculated.
Calculation of the correction:
Subtract the electronic time from the time taken by hand for the 10 competitors starting before the missing time. If there are not 10 times before, complete the calculation with the remaining times after the missed time.
The sum of the 10 time differences is divided by 10 and rounded up or down (0.044 -> 0.04, 0.045 -> 0.05) to give the correction which must be applied to the hand time of the competitor without an electronic time.

611.3.2.2     Photo Finish
A Photo Finish System may be used to determine a com- petitor’s finish time. In case of a failure of system“A” and“B”, and where the competition has been recorded     by the Photo Finish System, this time must be used in     place of hand-timing without any correction.
The photo finish time is taken when any part of the com- petitor’s body first crosses the Finish line. The photo fin- ish result is to be provided to the Jury only.

611.3.3              The official timing strips from the printer will be given to the Technical Delegate for review. They will be kept by the OC until the official approval of the race or after any appeal dealing with timing or race results.
A technical timing report form as prescribed by the FIS must accompany the race results and must be reviewed and sent by the chief of timing and reviewed and con- firmed by the TD as approval of the race.


修正值的计算方法如下 ：
计算缺失时间的运动员之前出发的 10 名运动员手动 计时时间减去电子计时时间的差。如果在缺失时间 的运动员之前出发的运动员不足 10 名，则用其后出 发的运动员的记录时间数据完成上述计算。
10 个时间差之和除以 10，四舍五入（0.044- ＞ 0.04,0.045- ＞ 0.05）后得出的即为修正值，该修正 值必须从缺失电子计时时间的运动员的手动计时中 减去，以得到其最终成绩。
611.3.2.2     终点录像
终点录像系统用来确定运动员的完赛时间。 A 系统 和 B 系统同时故障，并且比赛已由终点录像系统记 录下来的，必须使用终点录像系统记录的时间代替 手动计时，不需要任何修正。
运动员身体的任何部位首先切入终点线的时间，即 为终点录像计时时间。终点录像成绩只提供给仲裁 委员会。


611.3.3       打印的正式时间列表应交给技术代表检查，并由组 委会一直保存到比赛成绩获正式核准，或任何有关 计时或比赛成绩的申诉终结后。

国际雪联规定的计时技术报告表必须与比赛成绩一 并提交，并由计时长审查并发送，再由技术代表审 查并确认，作为对比赛成绩的核准。

COMPETITION RULES (ICR)


All printed records from system A, system B and hand timing must be retained by the OC for a period of three
(3) months after the competition or after any appeal dealing with timing or race results.

611.3.4              When the official printing timer allows manual input or correction of a time, some type of indication (star, as- terisk or other) concerning any effected change must be printed on all timing documentation.

611.3.5              Computer software calculating net times must use the pre- cision of the time ofthe day as used in the timing device.

611.4          Private timing and speed measurement
equipment of the Teams
Any request to install such equipment has to be made to the Jury by the team captain concerned, and the Jury decides concerning approval of the installation. At Olympic Winter Games, FIS World Ski Championships and FIS World Cup only the organisers timing equipment is permitted.

612           Start and Finish Officials

612.1           The Starter
The starter must synchronise a watch with those of the assistant starter and by telephone or radio with the chief timekeeper within ten minutes of the start. The starter is responsible for the warning signal and the start comman- das well as for the accuracy of the intervals between these

2nd Section   Rules Common to Alpine Events 第二部分    高山滑雪竞赛通则


所有 A 系统和 B 系统的打印记录和手动计时记录要 由组委会保留，至到比赛结束后或任何关于计时和 比赛结果的申诉终结后 3 个月。


611.3.4             正式打印计时器允许手工输入或修正其计时的，要 在所有的时间记录文件中的任何有效改变处打印某 种标记（星号等）。


611.3.5             用电脑软件计算净用时的，必须使用与计时设备一 样精度的时间。
611.4            各队自用计时和测速设备

任何安装计时设备的请求均须由有关领队向仲裁委 员会提出，由仲裁委员会裁定是否同意安装。在冬 季奥林匹克运动会、国际雪联世界锦标赛和国际雪 联世界杯上，仅可使用组织方的计时设备。


612       起点与终点官员
612.1       发令员
出发时间前 10 分钟内，发令员须用某一计时表与其 助理发令员的计时表同步，并用电话或对讲机与计 时长进行时间同步。发令员负责发出准备信号和出 发命令，并准确控制这些信号之间的间隔。发令员 向助理发令员指派监督运动员的任务。

COMPETITION RULES (ICR)

2nd Section   Rules Common to Alpine Events 第二部分    高山滑雪竞赛通则






signals and assigns the supervision of the competitors to the assistant starter.

612.2           The Assistant Starter
The assistant starter is responsible for calling the com- petitors to the start in their correct order.

612.3           The Start Recorder
The start recorder is responsible for recording the actual start times of all competitors.

612.4          The Chief Timekeeper
The chief timekeeper is responsible for the accuracy of the timing and synchronises the watches with the starter as shortly before and after the race as is possible. The chief timekeeper must publish unofficial times as quick- ly as possible (on the score-board, etc.). If the electric timing fails, the chief timekeeper must communicate im- mediately with the start referee and the TD.

612.5          The Assistant Timekeeper
Two assistant timekeepers operate stop watches according to art. 611.2.2. One assistant timekeeper maintains a com- plete record with the registered times of all competitors.

612.6          The Finish Controller
The finish controller has the following duties:
- Supervision of the section between the last gate and the finish




612.2       助理发令员
助理发令员负责严格按出发顺序召集运动员到起 点区。
612.3       出发记录员
出发记录员负责记录运动员的实际出发时间。


612.4       计时长
计时长负责计时的准确性。在比赛前后，要与发令 员在尽可能接近比赛开始的时间内对计时表进行时 间同步，尽快公布非正式成绩（在成绩板上）。如果 电子计时装置失灵，计时长须立即与起点裁判员和 技术代表联系。



612.5       助理计时员
2 名助理计时员按本规则第 611.2.2 条操作秒表。1 名助理计时员保留所有运动员登记时间的完整记录。


612.6       终点监督员
终点监督员负有以下职责 ：
- 监督最后 1 道旗门至终点的区域 ；

COMPETITION RULES (ICR)

2nd Section   Rules Common to Alpine Events 第二部分    高山滑雪竞赛通则






- Supervision of the proper crossing of the finish line
- Recording of the order of finishing of all competitors who complete the course

612.7          The Chief of Calculations
The chief of calculations is responsible for quick and accurate calculation of results and supervises the imme- diate duplication of unofficial results and the publication of official results after expiration of the protest interval, or after any protests have been dealt with.

613            The Start

613.1           The Start Area
The start area must be closed off to everyone except the starting competitor, accompanied by only one trainer and the start officials.
The start area must be protected appropriately against inclement weather.
A special roped off area must be provided for trainers, team captains, service personnel etc., in which they may take care of the waiting competitors without being inter- rupted by the public. An adequate shelter must be pre- pared for the competitors waiting for the call to start.
The competitor enters the defined start hut with both skis attached without any covers on them.

613.2           The Start Ramp
The start ramp should be prepared in such a way that the

- 监督运动员是否正确越过终点线 ；
- 记录所有完赛运动员到达终点的顺序。


612.7       计算长
计算长负责迅速准确地计算比赛成绩，监督非正式 成绩的立即备份，在抗议期限届满或所有抗议处理 完毕后公布正式成绩。



613       出发
613.1       出发区
出发区必须清空所有人，但将要出发的运动员及陪 同的 1 名教练和起点官员除外。
出发区必须加以适当防护以抵御恶劣天气。

必须用安全网为教练、领队、服务人员等围出一块 特别隔离区（紧邻出发区），以便他们在此照顾等待 出场的运动员而免受观众的打扰。必须为等待叫号 出发的运动员准备适用的遮庇棚。

运动员进入指定的出发棚，携带滑雪板，滑雪板上 没有任何覆盖物。
613.2       出发台
出发台应准备得使运动员能够放松地站立在起点线





THE INTERNATIONAL SKI
COMPETITION RULES (ICR)


competitors can stand relaxed on the starting line and can quickly reach full speed after leaving the start.

613.3           Start Procedure
No official or attendant who could possibly give an ad- vantage to or disturb the starting competitors can be be- hind them. All outside help is forbidden.
By order of the starter, competitors must plant their poles in front of the start line, or where indicated. The Starter must not touch the competitor at the start. Pushing off from the start posts or other aids is for- bidden and competitors must start only with the help of their ski poles.

613.4           Start Signals
10 seconds before the start, the starter will tell each competitor“10 seconds”. Five seconds before the start, the starter should count“5, 4, 3, 2, 1”and then give the start command“Go - Partez - Los”.(For Slalom see art. 805.3).
If possible, an automatic audible signal is to be used (art. 611.2.1.3). The starter will let the competitor see the start clock.

613.5           Start Timing
The start timing must measure the exact time when the competitors cross the start line with their leg below the knee.

2nd Section   Rules Common to Alpine Events 第二部分    高山滑雪竞赛通则


上，且出发后能很快达到全速。


613.3       出发程序
出发运动员身后不得有任何可能帮助或妨碍的官员 或陪同人员。任何外部帮助均在禁止之列。
按发令员的命令，运动员必须把雪杖插在出发线前 或指定位置。出发时，发令员不能接触运动员，运 动员出发时仅可凭借其雪杖，不得借助蹬推出发杆 或其他辅助。



613.4       出发信号
出发前 10 秒，发令员提示即将出发的运动员 ：“10 秒”。出发前 5 秒时，发令员开始倒计数“5、4、3、 2、1”，然后发出出发命令 ：“出发（发音为 ：Go-  Partez-Los ）” ( 回转赛参见本规则第 805.3 条 )。
如果可能，可使用自动语音信号（本规则第 611.2.1.3 条）。发令员应指引运动员看到出发钟。


613.5       出发计时
出发时间必须测量到运动员膝盖以下切入出发线的 准确时间。






THE INTERNATIONAL SKI
COMPETITION RULES (ICR)

2nd Section   Rules Common to Alpine Events 第二部分    高山滑雪竞赛通则






613.6           Delayed Start
A competitor who is not ready to start on time will be sanctioned. The Start Referee may however excuse such a delay if, in the start referee’s opinion the delay is due to“force majeure”.
For example, breakdown of a competitor’s personal equipment or minor sickness of a competitor does not constitute“force majeure”.
In case of doubt, the Jury may allow the start provisionally.

613.6.1             The start referee makes the decisions after consultation with the Jury (according to art. 613.6.2 and 613.6.3) and must record the start numbers and names of com- petitors who were not allowed to start because of late appearance, or who were allowed to start in spite of late appearance, or who were allowed to start provisionally.

613.6.2             In the case of fixed start intervals, delayed competitors may start at the fixed interval after they have reported to the start referee, in accordance with the decision of the Jury. The Start Referee informs the Jury as to when (after which start number) a delayed competitor is starting.

613.6.3             In the case of irregular start intervals, the delayed com- petitor will start according to art. 805.3. The start referee informs the Jury as to when (after which start number) a delayed competitor is starting.

613.6       出发延迟
不能按时出发的运动员要受到制裁。起点裁判长认 定因“不可抗力”耽搁出发的，可以放行。


但是，运动员的轻微病症或者自用竞赛器材故障， 不构成“不可抗力”因素。

如有疑问，仲裁委员会可允许运动员临时出发。

613.6.1             起点裁判长在同仲裁委员会协商后作出决定（根据 本规则第 613.6.2 条和 613.6.3 条）并相应记录以下 内容 ：因迟到而决定禁止出发、尽管迟到仍允许出 发或获准临时出发的运动员的出发号码和姓名。



613.6.2             采用固定出发间隔的比赛，迟到运动员向起点裁判 长报告后，根据仲裁委员会的决定，可以在该固定 间隔时间出发。迟到运动员出发前，起点裁判长通 知仲裁委员会（在哪个出发号码运动员后出发）。


613.6.3       非固定时间间隔出发时，迟到运动员可按本规则第
805.3 条规定出发。起点裁判长通知仲裁委员会迟到 运动员何时出发（在哪个出发号码之后）。






THE INTERNATIONAL SKI
COMPETITION RULES (ICR)

2nd Section   Rules Common to Alpine Events 第二部分    高山滑雪竞赛通则






613.7           Valid and False Starts
In competitions with a fixed start interval the competitor must start on the start signal. The start time is valid if it occurs within the following limits: 5 seconds before and 5 seconds after the official start time. A competitor who does not start within that space of time will be disqualified.
The start referee must inform the Referee of the start numbers and names of the competitors who made a false start or have contravened the starting rules.

614          Competition Course, Competition and Inspection

614.1           Competition Course

614.1.1             Competition Course and Technical Parts
A competition course is a designated area on a specific ski-slope, described by the respective FIS homologation. Start and Finish installations, television towers, mea- suring equipment, sponsor advertising equipment etc. are necessary items for a competition and are part of the competition course.

614.1.2        Course Setting

614.1.2.1     Assistance
Assistance must be provided at a time to be fixed by the Jury, so that the course setter can concentrate on the actual course setting and not be distracted by fetching poles, etc.

613.7       有效出发和错误出发
在固定出发间隔的比赛中，运动员须按出发信号出  发。运动员的实际出发时间在以下时限内的，为有 效出发 ：出发信号指示的正式出发时间前后 5 秒。 运动员未在此时限内出发的，取消资格。

起点裁判长须将错误出发或违反出发规则的运动员 姓名和出发号码通知裁判长。


614       赛道、比赛和视察线路

614.1       赛道
614.1.1       赛道及技术部分
赛道是从某一特定雪道中围出的区域，并（其技术 参数等）由各自的国际雪联认定证书具体描述。起 点和终点设备、电视塔、测量器材、赞助者广告器 材等，是比赛必需的物品，并成为赛道的组成部分。



614.1.2      旗门设计
614.1.2.1     协助
在仲裁委员会指定的时间内，必须为旗门设计员提 供协助，以便其全神贯注于旗门设计事务，不致因 取旗门杆等事务分神。

COMPETITION RULES (ICR)

2nd Section   Rules Common to Alpine Events 第二部分    高山滑雪竞赛通则






The Chief of Course equipment must provide enough of the following:
- enough blue and red slalom poles
- a corresponding number of gate panels, divided by co- lours
- hammers, drills, gate-keys, wedges etc.
- enough gate numbers
- colouring substance for marking the position of the poles.

614.1.2.2     Marking of the gates
The positions of the gate poles may be marked with an easily recognisable colouring substance which remains visible throughout the entire race.

614.1.2.3     Numbering the gates
The gates must be numbered from top to bottom of the course. Start and Finish are not counted.
614.1.2.4     Marking of the course and terrain
In Downhill and in Super-G the course should be marked using:
- on the inside and/or outside of the racing line before and after the gate
- small pine needles or similar material spread on the
course
and/or
- coloured dye used vertically from gate to gate as well as horizontally across the course or the inside and/or

赛道长必须足量提供下列设备 ：

- 足够的蓝色和红色回转旗杆 ；
- 有相应数量以颜色区分的旗门布 ；

- 大锤、电钻、旗门扳子、楔子等 ；
- 足够的旗门号码 ；
- 标记旗门杆位置的彩色涂料。


614.1.2.2      标示旗门
旗门杆的位置可以用易于辨认的彩色涂料标明，并 在整个比赛期间都清晰可见。


614.1.2.3     对旗门进行编号
旗门必须自线路起点至终点用数字编号。起点和终 点不计在内。
614.1.2.4     标示比赛线路和地形
在滑降和超级大回转项目中，比赛线路应进行如下 标示 ：
- 在进入旗门前和出旗门后的比赛线路内侧或者 外侧 ；
- 将小松针或类似材料撒在赛道上 ；

或者
- 用染料明显标示下列区域 ：旗门间沿赛道的垂直或 者水平方向，在进入旗门前和出旗门后的线路内侧

COMPETITION RULES (ICR)

2nd Section   Rules Common to Alpine Events 第二部分    高山滑雪竞赛通则






outside of the racing line before and after the gate no- tably on the approaches indicating changes in terrain, jumps, etc.

614.1.2.5     Spare Poles
The Chief of Course equipment is responsible for the availability and correct placing of enough spare poles. The poles are to be placed so that the competitors are not mislead by them.

614.1.3              Training on Competition Courses and Warm up Slopes
Official training in Downhill is part of the competition and governed in art.704.
For other types of Alpine events, the Jury may approve special training with or without gates (free ski) which can take place on the competition course. In that case, the training has to be controlled by the Jury and the Race Organisation.
Warm up slopes outside the competition course should be made available to the participating teams under spe- cific guidelines by the Organiser.
Warm up slopes are not under the control of the Jury and are not governed by the ICR.

614.1.4             Closing and Modification of the Course
A competition course is closed from the time the course setting begins.Nobody except for the Jury is permitted to change gates, gate panels, markings, etc. or modify the course structure (jumps, bumps, etc.) on a closed course.

和 / 或外侧雪道上，尤其要明显标示通往地形变化 及跳跃赛段的路段。


614.1.2.5     备用旗门杆
设备长负责准备随时可用并便于准确布置的数量充 足的备用旗门杆并妥善存放以免误导运动员。



614.1.3     在赛道和热身雪道上训练
场地适应训练是滑降比赛项目的组成部分并受本规 则 704 条规制。
对于滑降以外的其他高山滑雪比赛项目，仲裁委员 会可以批准在赛道上进行带旗门或者不带旗门（即 自由滑）的专门训练。此时，这类训练必须在仲裁 委员会及竞赛组织机构的监督下进行。
赛道之外的热身雪道应提前备妥以供各参赛队在组 织方的特别指引下使用。

热身雪道不受仲裁委员会管控，也不受《国际雪联 滑雪竞赛规则》规制。
614.1.4       赛道的关闭与修整
从旗门设计开始封闭赛道。除仲裁委员会外，任何 人不得在关闭赛道内改动旗门、旗门布、旗门标志等， 或修改旗门组合结构（跳跃、起伏处等）。





THE INTERNATIONAL SKI
COMPETITION RULES (ICR)


Competitors are not permitted to enter a closed competi- tion course.
Trainers, servicemen etc., who are allowed on a closed competition course are to be decided by the Jury.
Photographers and camera teams are allowed into the closed course area for the necessary documentation of the competition. Their total number can be limited by the Jury. They will be located by the Jury where possible and must remain only in this area.
The Jury or the Organising Committee may close a competition course or sections of a course to competi- tors, trainers, media and service personnel outside of the actual competition or training times for preparation and maintenance purposes.

614.1.5             Course changes
In case of necessary changes on the course, such as small relocation of gates, an additional inspection or training run is not necessary.
Details must be communicated to all team captains and com- petitors must be informed by the Start Referee at the start.

614.1.6             Downhill and Super-G at FIS World Ski Champion-
ships and Olympic Winter Games
Alpine men’s and women’s Downhill and Super-G com- petitions should be carried out on independent competi- tion courses, but start and finish installations and short sections of the courses can be used for both genders.

2nd Section   Rules Common to Alpine Events 第二部分    高山滑雪竞赛通则


运动员不得进入关闭赛道。

可以进入关闭赛道的教练员、服务人员由仲裁委员 会决定。
为留存必要的比赛音像资料的摄影师与摄制组可以 进入封闭的赛道区域，其总人数由仲裁委员会限定， 其活动区域也由仲裁委员会限定且只能在指定区域 活动。

为了准备或维护赛场的需要，仲裁委员会或者组委 会可以在实际比赛或训练时间以外对运动员、教练 员、媒体及服务人员关闭赛道或其部分赛段。



614.1.5      线路调整
如需要对线路进行必要调整，例如略微移动旗门位 置等，则无需额外的线路视察或试滑训练。

所有变更细节必须通报领队并由起点裁判长在起点 处告知参赛运动员。
614.1.6      国际雪联世界锦标赛和冬季奥林匹克运动会中的 滑降和超级大回转
高山滑雪男女滑降和超级大回转比赛应在彼此独立 的赛道上进行，但是赛道起点和终点的装置和赛道 中的部分赛段可以共享。






THE INTERNATIONAL SKI
COMPETITION RULES (ICR)

2nd Section   Rules Common to Alpine Events
第二部分    高山滑雪竞赛通则






614.2           Competition

614.2.1              Passage of the Gates
A gate must be passed according to art. 661.4.1.

614.2.2              Interdiction to Continue after a Gate Fault
If competitors miss a gate, they must no longer continue through further gates.

614.2.3              Interdiction to Continue after a competitor stops
If competitors come to a complete stop (e.g. after a fall), they must no longer continue through previous or further gates. This interdiction is valid in all events with a fixed start interval (Downhill, Super-G, Giant Slalom, Paral- lel). Only exception is for Slalom (art. 661.4. 1), as long as the competitor:
- does not interfere with the run of the next competitor or, - have not been passed by the next competitor.

614.2.4             Loss of one ski
If competitors lose a ski without having committed a gate fault or without coming to a complete stop, they may continue, as long as they
- does not interfere with the run of the next competitor or,
- have not been passed by the next competitor.
See also details in art. 615.3, 661.4.1, 804.3, 904.3.

614.2            比赛

614.2.1      通过旗门
运动员必须按照本规则第 661.4.1 条的规定通过旗门。

614.2.2       旗门失误后禁止继续比赛
运动员漏过 1 个旗门，不得继续通过后续旗门。


614.2.3       运动员停止后禁止继续比赛
运动员完全停止（如摔倒之后）后，不能继续通过 之前或后续旗门。此项规定适用于所有固定出发间  隔的比赛（滑降、超级大回转、大回转、平行式比 赛）。只有回转比赛有例外（见本规则第 661.4. 1 条）， 即只要运动员尚未出现下列情形仍可继续比赛 ：

- 没有干扰下一名运动员的滑行，或者
- 未被下一名运动员超越。

614.2.4       一只滑雪板脱落
运动员一只滑雪板脱落但没有出现旗门犯规也没有 完全停止的，可以继续比赛，但是必须 ：
- 没有干扰下一名运动员的滑行，或者
- 未被下一名运动员超越。
另详见本规则第 615.3 条、第 661.4. 1 条、第 804.3 条、 第 904.3 条。






THE INTERNATIONAL SKI
COMPETITION RULES (ICR)

2nd Section   Rules Common to Alpine Events 第二部分    高山滑雪竞赛通则






614.3           Inspection

614.3.1             Jury inspection
On race day, the Jury inspects the course and has to con- firm the FIS programme for the day. Team Captains may accompany the Jury.

614.3.2             Competitor inspection
The competitor inspection is held after Jury inspection and after the Jury has opened the competition course and is normally inspected, from top to bottom of the course. The course must be in racing condition from the time the competitor’s inspection starts and the competitors must not be disturbed during the inspection by workers on the course or similar. The competitors are authorised to study the final setting of the course by either skiing down at the side of the course at low speed, or side slip- ping through the gates (inspection). Skiing through gates or making practice turns parallel to those required by gates on the course is not allowed.
Competitors must carry their start numbers. Fenced, roped or blocked off sections of the course or gates must be respected. By the end of the inspection time, Compet- itors have to be outside the competition course.
Competitors are not permitted to enter the competition course on foot without skis.

614.3.3             Jury decisions
The time and duration of the Competitors Inspection is

614.3       视察
614.3.1       仲裁委员会视察赛道
仲裁委员会在每个比赛当日视察赛道，同时还要确 认当天的国际雪联竞赛秩序册。领队可陪同仲裁委 员会视察。
614.3.2       运动员视察线路
仲裁委员会视察线路完毕并决定开放线路后，运动 员可从线路的起点到终点对线路进行常规视察。从 运动员开始视察线路时起，赛道必须进入竞赛状态， 在赛道上或者其他区域的工作人员不得打扰视察线 路的运动员。允许运动员研究完成最后设计的线路， 他们有权从旗门一侧低速滑行或以横板滑降（平整 赛道滑行）通过旗门的方式来视察旗门。禁止滑行 穿过旗门或在旗门旁的平行赛段上模拟练习如何按 要求转弯通过该旗门。



运动员必须携带其出发号码布。运动员必须远离赛  道上用防护网、安全绳隔离或封闭的赛段或者旗门。 视察线路时间结束后，运动员必须退出赛道。
禁止运动员不穿滑雪板徒步进入赛道。


614.3.3      仲裁委员会决定
运动员视察赛道的开始和持续时间由仲裁委员会决





THE INTERNATIONAL SKI
COMPETITION RULES (ICR)


determined by the Jury and scheduled at the team cap- tains meeting. If necessary (e.g. because of special weather conditions), the Jury may decide on special- methods of competitors inspection.

615            The Finish

615.1           The Finish Area

615.1.1             The finish area should be plainly visible to competitors approaching the finish. It must be wide with a gently sloped smooth run-out.

615.1.2             In setting the course with gates particular attention should be paid to directing

615.1.3             The finish area is to be fenced in. Any unauthorised en- try is not allowed.

615.1.4              Finish installations and closures should be set up or se- cured through suitable protection measures.

615.1.5             For competitors who have finished their runs, a special area separated from the actual finish, is to be provided. In this area or corridor, it should be possible to make contact with the press (print, radio, TV and film) located in the media corridors.
615.1.6             The competitor must leave the finish area through the

2nd Section   Rules Common to Alpine Events 第二部分    高山滑雪竞赛通则


定并在领队会议上发出通知。必要时（如特殊天气 原因），仲裁委员会可决定采用特殊方式让运动员视 察线路。


615       终点
615.1       终点区
615.1.1       终点区应让接近终点的运动员清晰可见。终点区要
开阔，终点线后须有一段逆坡缓冲区。


615.1.2             在用旗门设计比赛线路时，尤其要注意引导运动员 按地形的自然线形通过终点。

615.1.3       整个终点区须完全用防护网围起，任何人未经授权 不得入内。

615.1.4       终点区应建终点设施和关闭装置或通过适当的措施 予以保护。

615.1.5             应为已经结束其滑行轮次的运动员提供一处与实际  终点分离的特别区域，在该区域或者走廊内运动员  可与位于媒体走廊的媒体（文字、电台、电视和电影） 接触。


615.1.6       运动员必须携带所有在比赛中使用的竞赛器材，从





THE INTERNATIONAL SKI
COMPETITION RULES (ICR)


official exit with all the competition equipment used in the race.

615.2          The Finish and its Markings
The Finish is marked by two poles or vertical banners which may be connected by a horizontal banner. In Downhill and Super-G races, the finish must be no less than 15 metres wide and in Slalom and Giant Slalom no less than 10 metres wide. In exceptional cases, the Jury may decrease this distance on the spot for technical reasons or because of the terrain. The width of the finish is considered to be the distance between the two finish poles or banners. The supports used to mount the timing devices must also be at least this far apart.
The timing supports can usually be placed behind the finish poles or banners, on the downhill side. The finish line between the timing cells must be clearly marked horizontally with colouring substance.

615.3          Crossing of the Finish Line and Record-
ing of the Times
The finish line must be crossed:
- on both skis or
- on one ski or
- with both feet in case of a fall between the last gate and the finish line.In this case the time is taken when any part of the competitor’s body stops the timekeeping system.

2nd Section   Rules Common to Alpine Events 第二部分    高山滑雪竞赛通则


正式的出口离开终点区。


615.2       终点及其标识
终点由 2 个标杆或中间由 1 个横幅连接的 2 根竖直 旗标标示。在滑降和超级大回转比赛中，终点宽度 不得少于 15 米 ；在回转和大回转比赛中，终点宽度 应不少于 10 米。在特殊情况下，因技术原因或地形 原因，仲裁委员会可以在现场缩短终点宽度。终点 宽度应视为 2 个标杆或旗标之间的距离。用于安装 计时装置的立柱至少也要相隔同等宽度。



计时装置的支柱通常安置在终点标杆或旗标的山下 一侧的后面。位于计时切光器之间的终点线须沿水 平方向用彩色涂料清楚地标明。


615.3       越过终点线和记录时间

必须以如下方式之一通过终点线 ：
- 穿着两只滑雪板 ；
- 穿着一只滑雪板 ；
- 双脚未穿滑雪板通过，限于在终点线与最后一个旗 门之间摔倒的。在这种情况下，计取运动员身体的 任何一部分触发计时系统停止计时的时间。

COMPETITION RULES (ICR)

2nd Section   Rules Common to Alpine Events 第二部分    高山滑雪竞赛通则






615.4           Report
The Finish Referee must make a report to the Referee immediately after the race or the official training.

616           Microphones and Special Electronic Devices
616.1           Within the areas of Start and Finish as well as in the area of the closed competition course, the use of microphones installed without the agreement of the organiser and the Jury (“roving”and so-called“gallows”, microphones set into cameras or other technical instruments) is for- bidden in training as well as in the race.

616.2           Unmanned and anchorless aerial vehicles (UAV) such as Drones or Quadrocopters etc., are strictly prohibited over the Race Course area during inspection, training or competition, unless approved by the Jury and the organ- iser in writing subject to any prohibitions imposed by local laws or the property owners. The Race Course area is defined by the Jury.
Violators will be subject to sanctions by the Jury in ac- cordance with ICR art. 223.

617           Calculation and Announcement of Results

617.1          Unofficial Times
Times taken by the timekeepers must be considered

615.4       报告
终点裁判长应在比赛或场地适应训练后立即向裁判 长报告。
616       话筒和特殊电子设备

616.1      在训练和比赛期间，在终点和起点区域以及封闭的 赛道区域，不得使用未经组织方和仲裁委员会允许 而安装的各种话筒（包括移动话筒和安装在三脚架 上的话筒，照相机及其他技术设备的内置话筒）。



616.2      在视察赛道、训练或比赛期间，严禁在比赛用赛道 区域上空使用无人驾驶和无锚定飞行器 (UAV)，如 无人机或四轴飞行器等设备，除非在不违反当地法 律或者业主设定的禁止性条件的情况下，经仲裁委 员会会同组织方以书面形式批准才能够使用。赛道 区域的范围由仲裁委员会界定。

违规者由仲裁委员会根据本规则第 223 条进行处罚。


617       计算与公布成绩

617.1       非正式成绩
计时员所计的时间应视为非正式成绩。这样的成绩






THE INTERNATIONAL SKI
COMPETITION RULES (ICR)

2nd Section   Rules Common to Alpine Events 第二部分    高山滑雪竞赛通则






unofficial times. They should be posted on a score-board which should be readily visible from the area provided for the competitors who have finished, and from the press area. Whenever possible, unofficial times should be announced to the public over loud-speakers.

617.2          Announcement of Unofficial Times and Disqualifications
617.2.1             As soon as possible after completion of the race, unoffi- cial times and disqualifications must be published on the official notice board at the finish.
The time limit for protest is counted from the moment of this announcement. (art. 643.4, 643.5)

617.2.2             Oral announcement of disqualifications may replace the
publication on the official notice board.
It can be decided that protests can be delivered verbally to the Referee at the Finish within 15 minutes after the announcement of the disqualification. Protests submitted after this are considered null and void.
The team captains must be informed beforehand of the announcement and protest procedure.

617.3           Official Results

617.3.1             Results are determined from the official times of those competitors who have been officially classified

应张帖在成绩板上，在专门为到达终点的运动员特 设的区域和采访区内都清晰可见。如有可能，非正 式成绩应通过扩音器向观众公布。



617.2       非正式成绩和取消资格的公布


617.2. 1      比赛结束后，必须尽快在设立于终点区的正式告示
板上公布非正式成绩和取消资格情况。

抗议期限自公告之时起计算（另见本规则第 643.4条、 第 643.5 条）。
617.2.2       可以口头宣布取消资格的方式代替正式告示板上的 公告。
可以决定在宣布取消比赛资格后 15 分钟内，在终点 区口头向终点裁判长提出抗议。在此之后提交的抗 议被视为无效。

领队必须在宣布取消资格和抗议程序之前先得到 通知。
617.3       正式成绩
617.3.1             比赛成绩取决于正式分组的运动员的正式比赛时间。






THE INTERNATIONAL SKI
COMPETITION RULES (ICR)

2nd Section   Rules Common to Alpine Events 第二部分    高山滑雪竞赛通则






617.3.2             Combined results are calculated by adding together the race times obtained in each event of the combined event. (or by adding the race points)

617.3.3             If two or more competitors have the same time or the same number of points, the competitor with the higher start number must be listed first on the official list of re- sults (ex aequo).

617.3.4             The official result list must contain:
- the name of the organising club or association
- the name of the competition, the site, event, category and gender
- the date of the race
- all technical data such as the name of the competition course, altitude at start and finish, vertical drop, FIS homologation number and, for Downhill and Super-G, the length of the course
- the names and nations of the members of the Jury
- for each run, the names and nations of the course setter and the forerunners, the number of gates (Slalom, Gi- ant Slalom and Super-G between brackets number of direction changes) and the start time
- the weather, the snow conditions on the course and the air temperature at race start and finish recorded at time of race start.
- all details concerning the competitors, ranking, start number, code number, name and first name, nation (and possibly club), time and race points

617.3.2             全能比赛成绩，就是将全能比赛中每项比赛的时间 相加（或将比赛积分相加）。


617.3.3       如果有两名或更多的运动员所用的时间相等或积分 相同，在正式成绩公告中出发号码大的运动员要排 在前面（公平原则）。


617.3.4             正式成绩列表应当包含 ：
- 作为组织方的俱乐部或协会的名称 ；
- 比赛名称、地点、比赛项目、组别和性别 ；

- 比赛日期 ；
- 所有技术数据，如赛道名称、起点终点的海拔高度、 垂直落差、国际雪联的认证号码以及滑降和超级大 回转比赛线路长度 ；

- 仲裁委员会成员的姓名和国籍 ；
- 每一轮滑行中旗门设计员和试滑员的姓名和国籍、 旗门数量（回转、大回转和超级大回转换向次数） 和出发时间 ；

- 比赛开始时在比赛起点和终点记录的天气、赛道上 的雪况和气温 ；

- 有关运动员、排名、出发号码、注册代码、姓名、 国家（也可能是俱乐部）、时间和比赛积分等所有  详细信息 ；

- the start number, code number, name, first name and nation of those competitors who were not at the start, did not finish or were disqualified in each run
- the names of the official service companies, e.g. timing company, computer service etc.

619            Award Ceremony
The official award ceremony must not be held before the completion of the race and not before the Technical Del- egate has authorised it.
The organiser has the right to present the probable win- ners before this time. This presentation is unofficial and is organised at a place different from that of the official award ceremony.

620            Start Order
For the Olympic Winter Games, FIS World Ski Champi- onships, FIS World Cup and the FIS Continental Cups

- 每轮未到出发区、没有完成比赛、取消资格的运动 员的出发号码、注册代码、姓名和国籍 ；

- 比赛代码和 F值 ；
- 判罚计算表 ；
- 技术代表的签名。

617.3.5             各国均须以指定的 3 个大写字母组成的国际雪联代
码指代（参见国际雪联公告或其官网）。

618       国际雪联积分与参加国际雪联比赛

619       颁奖仪式
比赛结束前以及技术代表尚未授权前，不得举行正 式颁奖仪式。
组织方有权在正式颁奖仪式前向准获胜者提前颁奖， 但这样的颁奖是非正式的，并且是在不同于正式颁 奖仪式的地点进行。


620       出发顺序
对于冬季奥林匹克运动会、国际雪联世界滑雪锦标 赛、国际雪联世界杯和国际雪联洲际杯， 可 以颁布





THE INTERNATIONAL SKI
COMPETITION RULES (ICR)


special regulations may be issued.

621           Group Draw and Start Order
621.1          The classification of competitors who are present is made by the Jury.

621.2           The FIS Points List worked out by FIS must be used for the classification of competitors. If competitors do not appear in the last valid FIS points list, they will be assigned to that group of competitors without FIS points.

621.3           The starting order of the competitors in all alpine com- petitions is determined by their FIS points (Downhill, Slalom, Giant Slalom, Super-G and Alpine Combined). A first group of a maximum of the  15 best competitors present regardless of nationality will be drawn.The group may be increased if two or more competitors share the 15th rank.
All remaining competitors start in order of their FIS points. All competitors without FIS points will be drawn in the last group.
If in the first 15 competitors present, the points differ- ence between one and the next competitor is too great; the Jury will decide the number of competitors in the first group. The rest will start in the order of their FIS points.

2nd Section   Rules Common to Alpine Events 第二部分    高山滑雪竞赛通则


特别规定。

621       分组抽签和出发顺序
621.1      仲裁委员会负责参赛运动员的分组。


621.2      运动员分组时应使用由国际雪联制定的国际雪联积 分榜。如果某运动员未被纳入最新的国际雪联积分 榜，应被分入无国际雪联积分的运动员组。



621.3      所有高山滑雪比赛中参赛运动员的出发顺序由其国 际雪联积分（滑降、回转、大回转、超级大回转和 全能赛）决定。第一组运动员最多 15 名，从参赛的 积分最高的运动员中抽出，不分国籍。如果有两名 或以上的参赛运动员并列第 15 名，则该组人数可以 增加。

其余运动员将按其国际雪联积分顺序出发。没有国  际雪联积分的所有参赛运动员都会被抽到最后一组。

如果参赛的前 15 名运动员中，紧挨着的两人积分相 差太大，由仲裁委员会决定第一组的人数。其余运 动员按其国际雪联积分排名出发。






THE INTERNATIONAL SKI
COMPETITION RULES (ICR)

2nd Section   Rules Common to Alpine Events 第二部分    高山滑雪竞赛通则






621.3.1             Youth Competition (see art. 608.6)

621.3.2             Starting Order at National Championships (NC)
As an alternative to art. 621.3 for National Champion- ships the Jury may permit the draw/choice of start num- bers to be as follows:
For Slalom and Giant Slalom the first 15 ranked compet- itors according to current FIS points will be divided into two groups (1 to 7 and 8 to 15) Start numbers will then be drawn within the groups by double draw.
For Downhill, Super-G and Alpine Combined the first 15 ranked competitors according to current FIS points, in ranked order, may choose a start number between 1 and
30. The remaining start numbers between 1 and 30 will then be drawn amongst the competitors ranked 16 to 30 according to current FIS points. All other competitors start in the order of their FIS points.

621.3.3              Starting order Alpine Combined
If the Slalom run takes place before the Downhill or Su- per-G, competitors who are shown as DNS, NPS, DNF or DSQ will start in the Downhill or Super-G with their original bib after the last qualified competitor in the Sla- lom Run, with the exception of Olympic Winter Games, FIS World Ski Championships, World Cup and European Cup competitions. The starting order of AC competitions is determined by AC FIS points. Exception: AC compe- titions at NC and NJC may be seeded by DH or SG FIS points.

621.3.1       青少年比赛（参见本规则第 608.6 条）。
621.3.2       国内锦标赛（NC）中的出发顺序
作为国内锦标赛针对本规则第 621.3 条的替代方 案，仲裁委员会可允许采取如下方式抽签或选择 出发号码 ：
在回转和大回转比赛中，第一组的 15 名运动员根据 国际雪联的积分分成 2 组（1 至 7 号及 8 至 15 号）。 然后在组内通过双重抽签抽取出发号码。
在滑降、超级大回转和全能赛比赛中，根据现有国 际雪联积分排名前 15 的运动员，可以按排名顺序选 择 1 到 30 之间的出发号码。 1 到 30 号中剩余的号 码将根据现有国际雪联积分，在排名 16 到 30 的运 动员中抽签决定。所有其他运动员按照其国际雪联 积分排名出发。


621.3.3       高山全能出发顺序
如果回转项目在滑降和超级大回转之前举行，被判罚  未出发（DNS）、禁止出发（NPS）、未完成（DNF） 或取消资格（DSQ）的运动员在参加滑降和超级大回  转比赛时仍佩戴最初的出发号码布，其顺序应安排在  有资格参加回转比赛的最后 1 名运动员之后。以上规  定不适用于冬季奥林匹克运动会、国际雪联世界锦标  赛、世界杯和欧洲杯的比赛。高山全能比赛的出发顺  序由高山全能国际雪联积分决定。例外情况 ：国内锦  标赛和国内青少年锦标赛中的高山全能比赛可由滑  降或超级大回转国际雪联积分确定种子选手。

621.4           If the number without FIS points is too great, the Jury must divide them into several groups. In this case, each nation announces the groups to which it wishes its com- petitors to belong. Each group is then drawn separately. The Jury should whenever possible, take into account the observations made during the official downhill train- ing and must divide the competitors from several nations fairly between the groups without FIS points. As a rule, each nation who has entered competitors without FIS points puts one competitor into the first group of com- petitors without FIS points.

621.5          The Jury has the right to change the starting order if they consider the condition of the course warrants it.
621.6           The draw must take place on the day before the race. For night races, the draw must take place at the latest before noon on the race day.

621.7           The first group and the groups without FIS Points in downhill training must be drawn every day.

621.8           The draw (first group and groups without FIS points) must be held in a team captains’meeting.
A double draw is recommended with a simultaneous draw of the start number and the name of the competitor.

621.9          The Jury may allow a computer-assisted draw. A repre- sentative of each nation is required to sign the team entry

621.4      无国际雪联积分的人数过多的，仲裁委员会必须将 其分成若干组。此时，每个国家都宣布希望其运动 员归属的分组，然后每组单独抽签。如有可能，仲 裁委员会应在考虑滑降适应场地训练期间观察到的 运动员表现的基础上，将来自不同国家的运动员公 平分配到没有国际雪联积分的各组中。原则上，每 个派出无国际雪联积分选手参赛的国家都要有一名 选手放入由没有国际雪联积分选手组成的第一组中。




621.5      仲裁委员会有权根据赛道条件需要更改出发顺序。


621.6      抽签须在比赛的前一天进行。如果比赛在夜间进行， 抽签最迟在比赛日的午前进行。


621.7      第一组和滑降训练中无国际雪联积分的各训练组， 每天都必须抽签。

621.8       抽签（第一组和无国际雪联积分各组）必须在领队 会议上进行。
建议采用双重抽签法，即同时抽出出发顺序号码和 运动员的姓名。
621.9      仲裁委员会可以允许计算机辅助抽签。在采用计算 机抽签之前，每个国家的代表都必须在领队会议上

at the team captains’meeting before the draw is con- ducted by computer.

621.10        Starting Order in Extraordinary Condi-
tions (Snow Seed)
In extraordinary conditions, the Jury may change the start- ing order of a Downhill race, a Giant Slalom or a Super-G (when snowing, etc.). A group of at least 6 competitors, nominated in advance, start before start number one.
These 6 competitors are drawn from among the last 20% of the start list.They will start in reverse order of their start numbers.

621.11         Starting Order for the 2nd Run

621.11.1           In competitions with two runs, the starting order for the second run is determined by the result list of the first run except for the first 30 places.
621.11.2           For the first 30 places the starting order is as follows:
- the 30th in the result list starts 1st
- the 29th in the result list starts 2nd
- the 28th in the result list starts 3rd
- the 27th in the result list starts 4th
- the 1st in the result list starts 30th
- from the 31st onward according to the result list of the first run.
If more than one competitor is ranked 30th, the competi- tor with the lowest start number will start first.

的参赛队签到表中签名。


621.10      特殊情况下的出发顺序（下雪）

在特殊情况下（如下雪等），仲裁委员会可以改变滑 降、大回转和超级大回转的出发顺序。事先提名的 由至少 6 名运动员组成的小组，在第一出发顺序之 前出发。
这 6 名运动员从出发顺序表最后 20% 的运动员中抽 签选出。按他们的出发顺序号倒序出发。


621.11      第二轮滑行出发顺序
621.11.1           有两轮滑行的比赛项目，第二轮滑行的出发顺序由 第一轮滑行成绩列表决定，前 30 名除外。


621.11.2           成绩列表中位居前 30 名的运动员出发顺序如下 ：
- 第 30 名第 1 出发 ；
- 第 29 名第 2 出发 ；
- 第 28 名第 3 出发 ；
- 第 27 名第 4 出发 ；
- 第 1 名第 30 出发。
- 从第 31 名起，按第一轮滑行成绩列表顺序出发。

如果有不止一名运动员排在第 30 名，出发号码小的 先出发。

COMPETITION RULES (ICR)

2nd Section   Rules Common to Alpine Events 第二部分    高山滑雪竞赛通则






621.11.3            Starting Order for the 2nd Run at FIS Races（all levels ） The Jury has the right to decide no later than one hour   before the start of the first run; whether the reversed   order shall be reduced to the first fifteen placed competi-   tors from the first run.
621.11.4           A start list for the second run must be published in good time and made available to teams and officials at the start for the second run.

621.12         Double Entries
If competitors have started in a competition they cannot appear as DNS 1 in another competition on the same day, except for a DH training. If competitors are entered into and drawn for a DH competition and subsequently leaves this competition in order to participate in another DH competition, they will not be permitted to return to the first DH competition.
The FIS Office will refer all double entries to the FIS Council for appropriate action.

622            Start Intervals

622.1          Regular Intervals
In Downhill, Giant Slalom and Super-G, competitors will normally start at regular intervals of 60 seconds; for Slalom see art. 805.1. The Jury may fix different inter- vals.

621.11.3      国际雪联比赛中第二轮滑行的出发顺序（所有等级） 仲裁委员会有权在第一轮滑行开始 1 个小时前决定， 是否将倒序出发的运动员减到第一轮滑行的前  15 名。


621.11.4      必须及时发布第二轮滑行的出发顺序，并在第二轮
滑行的出发区提供给代表队和其随队官员。


621.12      双重报名
除滑降训练外，已经在比赛中出发的运动员不能以  未出发 1（DNS 1）的身份在同一天参加其他比赛。 如果运动员报名参加滑降比赛并已抽签，然后为参  加另一项滑降比赛而离开了该次比赛，则不能再返  回参加该次滑降比赛。


国际雪联办公室将向国际雪联理事会报告所有双重 报名的情况以采取适当措施。
622       出发间隔
622.1       正常出发间隔
在滑降、大回转和超级大回转比赛中，运动员通常 按 60 秒的正常间隔出发 ；回转比赛参见本规则第 805. 1 条。仲裁委员会可以确定不同的间隔时间。






THE INTERNATIONAL SKI
COMPETITION RULES (ICR)

2nd Section   Rules Common to Alpine Events 第二部分    高山滑雪竞赛通则






622.2          Special Start Intervals
The start intervals in Downhill, Super-G and if neces- sary, Giant Slalom may be changed under the following conditions:
622.2.1             The time extension must be used for sensible TV trans- mission of interesting sections of the entire course.

622.2.2             The start interval is determined by the Jury.

622.2.3             The start interval must not be less than 40 seconds in Downhill and Super-G and 30 seconds in Giant Slalom.
622.2.4             Further exceptions to art. 622.2.2 and 622.2.3 can be made only by the FIS Council (World Cup: According to World Cup Rules).

623           Re-runs

623.1           Prerequisites

623.1.1             Competitors who are obstructed while racing must stop immediately after the incident takes place and report this to the nearest gate judge. They may apply to any mem- ber of the Jury for a re-run. This claim can also be made by the team captain of the obstructed competitor. Com- petitors should make their way to the Finish along the side of the course.

622.2       特殊出发间隔
在滑降、超级大回转比赛中，以及必要时在大回转 比赛中，如遇下列情况可改变出发间隔 ：


622.2.1              电视合理转播整个比赛中最精彩的旗门组时，必须 延长出发间隔。

622.2.2              出发间隔由仲裁委员会决定。

622.2.3             滑降和超级大回转的出发间隔不得少于 40 秒，大回 转的出发间隔不得少于 30 秒。

622.2.4            只有国际雪联理事会方可进一步作出本规则第
622.2.2 条和第 622.2.3 条以外的规定（世界杯赛 ： 参照《世界杯规则》）。

623       重滑
623.1       先决条件
623.1.1             运动员在比赛中受到阻碍，应在事故发生后立即停 下来并向距离最近的旗门裁判员报告。受阻运动员 或由其领队可以向仲裁委员会的任何成员提出重滑 要求。运动员应设法沿着赛道边缘抵达终点。






THE INTERNATIONAL SKI
COMPETITION RULES (ICR)

2nd Section   Rules Common to Alpine Events 第二部分    高山滑雪竞赛通则






623.1.2              In special situations (e.g. failure of the timekeeping system or other technical failures), the Jury may grant a re-run.

623.1.3             When competitors are waved down by a yellow flag, they must stop immediately. They have the right to a re- run, provided that the Jury considers this possible from an organisational point of view. The Jury should ensure that the competitor’s re-run takes place before the last competitor on the start list of the race, or training run in the case of Downhill (see art. 705.2 and 705.3).

623.2          Grounds for Interference

623.2.1             Blocking of the course by an official, a spectator, an ani- mal or other Obstruction.
623.2.2             Blocking of the course by a fallen competitor who does not clear the course quickly enough.

623.2.3             Objects in the course such as a lost ski pole or the ski of a previous competitor.

623.2.4             Activities of the first aid service which obstruct the com- petitor.

623.2.5             Absence of a gate that has not been promptly replaced.

623.2.6             Other similar incidents beyond the will and control of the competitor, which cause significant loss of speed or

623.1.2             在特殊情况下（如计时系统失灵或其他技术性故障）， 仲裁委员会可下令重滑。

623.1.3       运动员看到挥舞黄旗必须立即停止滑行。若仲裁委  员会从赛事组织的角度认为可行，运动员有权重滑。 仲裁委员会应确保其在出发顺序表最后 1 名运动员 出发前或在滑降中的训练前重滑（参见本规则第
705.2 条、第 705.3 条）。



623.2       干扰的情形
623.2.1             在赛道上受到官员、观众、动物或其他障碍物的 阻碍。

623.2.2             在赛道上受到滑倒而又没有及时离开线路的运动员 的阻碍。

623.2.3             受到赛道上物品的阻碍，如前面运动员丢落的滑雪 杖、滑雪板。

623.2.4             受到急救活动的阻碍。


623.2.5             旗门缺失并且没有及时重新安放好。

623.2.6             其他类似的超出运动员意志力和控制范围的事故， 造成其速度明显减慢或比赛线路的实际延长，进而





THE INTERNATIONAL SKI
COMPETITION RULES (ICR)


a lengthening of the racing line and consequently affect the competitor’s time.

623.2.7             Interruption by an official with a Yellow Flag (see art. 623.1.3).

623.3           Validity of a Re-run

623.3.1             If the Referee or another Jury member is unable to question the appropriate officials immediately or to judge the justification for the re-run they may grant a provisional re-run, to avoid delay for the competitor. This re-run will be valid only if it is subsequently confirmed by the Jury.

623.3.2             If competitors were already disqualified before the inci- dent entitling them to a re-run, the re-run is not valid.

623.3.3             The provisional or subsequently approved run remains valid even if it proves slower than the obstructed one.

623.4          Start Time of the Re-run

623.4.1              In the case of fixed start intervals, competitors must start at the fixed interval, after they have reported to the start refer- ee, in accordance with the decision of the start referee.

623.4.2             With non-fixed start intervals, the procedure is in accor- dance with the provisions of art. 805.3.

2nd Section   Rules Common to Alpine Events 第二部分    高山滑雪竞赛通则


影响运动员的用时。


623.2.7             受到手持黄旗的官员的干扰而暂停滑行（见本规则 第 623.1.3 条）。
623.3       重滑的有效性
623.3.1             如果裁判长或者其他仲裁委员会成员不能马上询问 有关官员或无法判定重滑的正当理由，为避免耽误 运动员，可批准临时重滑一次。临时重滑只有随后 经仲裁委员会确认后方为有效。



623.3.2             运动员在赋予其重滑权利的事故发生前已被取消资 格的，重滑无效。

623.3.3             临时获准或随后正式获批的重滑，即便比受到阻碍 的第一次滑行还慢，重滑成绩仍然有效。

623.4            重滑的出发时间

623.4.1             在采用固定出发间隔的比赛中，重新出发的运动员 向起点裁判长报告后，根据其决定在固定的出发间 隔时间出发。

623.4.2             在采用非固定出发间隔的比赛中，出发程序按本规 则第 805.3 条执行。

624           Interruption of the Run or Training
If an interrupted run cannot be finished on the same day, it is to be treated as a terminated run.

624.1          By the Jury

624.1.1             to allow course maintenance

624.1.2             for unfavourable or inconsistent weather and snow con- ditions
624.1.2.1     The race is to be restarted as soon as the work on the course has finished and if the weather and snow con- ditions have changed so that a fair competition can be assured.
624.1.2.2     A repeated interruption of the race ordered for the same reason should lead to a termination. A Downhill, a Su- per-G, as well as one run of Slalom or Giant Slalom may not last longer than four hours.

624.2           Brief Interruption
Each member of the Jury is entitled to order a brief inter- ruption of the run, including at the request of a gate judge.

625           Termination of a Competition

625.1           by the Jury
- if the competitors are significantly affected by outside

624       比赛或训练的暂停
如果被暂停的比赛不能在当天结束，应视为被终止 的比赛。
624.1       仲裁委员会决定
624.1.1              因需平整赛道 ；

624.1.2              因恶劣或不稳定的天气及雪况。


624.1.2.1     一旦赛道平整完毕，如果天气和雪况发生变化，比
赛继续进行，以确保公平竞争。



624.1.2.2     因相同原因致使比赛赛序反复被打断的，应终止比 赛。滑降、超级大回转及回转或大回转任何一轮滑 行时间不得超过 4 小时。


624.2       短时暂停比赛
仲裁委员会的每—位成员都有权命令比赛短时暂停， 包括应旗门裁判员请求的情形。
625       终止比赛
625.1       由仲裁委员会决定
- 参赛运动员明显受到外界干扰影响 ；

COMPETITION RULES (ICR)

2nd Section   Rules Common to Alpine Events 第二部分    高山滑雪竞赛通则






disturbing inﬂuences.
- if conditions arise that interfere with the fairness of the race or if the proper conduct of the race may no longer be guaranteed.

626           Report
For all interrupted or terminated competitions (art. 624 and 625), a full and detailed report is to be made by the TD to the FIS and the organising National Ski Associa- tion. The report must contain a well-founded recommen- dation, as to whether the terminated competition is to be taken into consideration for FIS points or not.

627            Not Permitted to Start (NPS)
A competitor will not be permitted to start (NPS) in any FIS International Ski competition who:

627.1          wears obscene names and/or symbols on clothing and equipment (art.207. 1) or behaves in an unsportsmanlike manner in the start area (art.205.5, 223.1. 1)

627.2           violates the FIS rules in regard to the FIS Specifications for Alpine Competition Equipment and Commercial Markings on Equipment (art. 222 and 207). (Exception art. 606.2 Competition Suits)

627.3          refuses to undertake a FIS required medical examination (art. 221.2)


- 发生妨碍比赛公平或不能保证比赛正常进行的情况。



626       报告
对于所有暂停或终止的比赛（本规则第 624 和第 625 条），应由技术代表向国际雪联和组织比赛的国 家滑雪协会提交一份完整详细的报告。报告必须包 含有理有据的建议，内容涉及是否考虑将被终止的 比赛算入国际雪联积分。


627       禁止出发（NPS）
有如下违规行为的运动员在任何国际雪联国际比赛 中均禁止出发 ：
627.1      比赛服装或竞赛器材上带有淫秽名称或者标识的（本 规则第 207. 1 条），或在出发区行为举止缺乏运动员 风范（本规则第 205.5 条，第 223.1. 1 条）。
627.2      违反《国际雪联高山滑雪竞赛器材与竞赛器材上的  商业标识的具体规定》（本规则第 222 条和 207 条）。 （本规则第 606.2 条比赛服装除外）


627.3      拒绝接受国际雪联要求执行的医学检查（本规则第
221.2 条）。






THE INTERNATIONAL SKI
COMPETITION RULES (ICR)

2nd Section   Rules Common to Alpine Events 第二部分    高山滑雪竞赛通则






627.4           trains on a course closed for competitors (art. 614.1.4)
627.5           in training for Downhill has not participated in at least one timed training run (art. 704.8.3)

627.6           does not wear a crash helmet that conforms to the Speci- fications for Alpine Competition Equipment (art. 606.4), or does not have ski brakes on their skis (art. 606.3), does not wear or carry an official start number according to the rules. (art. 606. 1)

627.7           was disqualified, (DSQ) did not start (DNS), not permit- ted to start (NPS) or did not finish (DNF) in the first run. Alpine Combined FIS races are exempt from this rule. A competitor who was DSQ, DNS, NPS or DNF in the slalom run can start the speed event. If the speed event precedes the slalom run the exemption does not apply. (art. 621.3.3)

628            Penalties
A penalty will be assessed by the Jury especially where the competitor:

628.1           violate the rules governing advertising on equipment (art. 207.)

628.2           alters the start number (Bib) in a way which is not per- mitted (art. 606. 1)

627.4       在不对运动员开放的赛道上训练（本规则第 614.1.4 条）。
627.5      在滑降训练中，没有参加至少一轮的计时训练（本 规则第 704.8.3 条）。

627.6                不穿戴符合《高山滑雪竞赛器材具体规定》的防护 头盔（本规则第 606.4条），或滑雪板上没有制动器（本 规则第 606.3 条），不按照规定佩戴或携带正式出发 号码（本规则第 606. 1 条）。


627.7      在第一轮滑行中被裁定取消资格（DSQ）、未出发 （DNS）、禁止出发（NPS）或者未完成（DNF）。国
际雪联高山滑雪全能赛不受此规则的限制。在回转 比赛中被判取消资格、未出发、禁止出发或没有完 成比赛的运动员可以参加竞速项目。如果竞速项目 安排在回转比赛之前，则不适用例外（本规则第 621.3.3 条）。
628       处罚
仲裁委员会将对是否给予处罚进行评估，特别是运 动员有如下行为的 ：
628.1      违反在竞赛器材上作广告的规则（本规则第 207 条）；


628.2         以未经允许手段改变出发号码（号码布）（本规则第
606. 1 条）；






THE INTERNATIONAL SKI
COMPETITION RULES (ICR)

2nd Section   Rules Common to Alpine Events 第二部分    高山滑雪竞赛通则






628.3           does not wear or carry the official start number accord- ing to the rules. (art.606.1, 614.3)

628.4           skis through set gates or practices turns parallel to the course or violates in any way rules of competitors’in- spection (art. 614.3)

628.5           is not ready to start on time or makes a false start (art.
613.6, 613.7, 805.3.1, 805.4, 1226.3)

628.6           violates rules of the start or starts in a manner that is not permitted by the rules (art. 613.3)

628.7          requests  a re-run which proves not to be valid (art. 623.3.2)

628.8           continues to race after committing a gate fault or after a complete stop or violates the rule Loss of one Ski (art.
614.2.2, 614.2.3, 614.2.4)

628.9          fails to cross the finish line correctly (art. 615.3)

628.10         does not leave the finish area through the official exit with all the competition equipment used in the race (art. 615.1.6).

628.11         takes skis to the official ceremonies (art. 206.6)
628.12           receives outside help during a competition (art. 661.3)

628.3      未按规则佩戴或携带正式 出发号码（本规则第
606. 1、第 614.3 条）；
628.4      滑行穿过旗门或在旗门旁的平行赛段练习转弯， 或违反有关运动员视察线路的规定（本规则第
614.3 条）；
628.5      未能按时出发，或违反出发规定（本规则第 613.6 条、 第 613.7 条、第 805.3. 1 条、第 805.4 条和 1226.3 条）；
628.6      违反了出发规则，或以其他规则不允许的方式出发 （本规则第 613.3 条）；
628.7      要求重滑但重滑后未获得有效确认（本规则第 623.3.2 条）；
628.8      导致旗门失误、完全停止或者违反失去一只滑雪板 的规定（本规则第 614.2.2、614.2.3、614.2.4 条）继 续滑行的 ；

628.9       未正确通过终点线（本规则第 615.3 条）；


628.10     未携带比赛中使用的所有竞赛器材从正式出口离开 终点区（本规则第 615.1.7 条）；


628.11     携带滑雪板参加正式颁奖仪式（本规则第 206.6 条）；
628.12     比赛中得到外界帮助（本规则第 661.3 条）；

628.13        wears obscene names and/or symbols on clothing and equipment (art.207. 1) or behaves in an unsportsmanlike manner in the competition area(art. 205.5, 223.1. 1)

628.14         has actually started in a competition and is later determined by the Jury to have been in violation of art. 627 rules.

629           Disqualifications
Competitors will be disqualified if they:

629.1           participate in the race under false pretences
629.2          jeopardise the security of persons or property or causes actual injury or damage

629.3           do not pass through a gate correctly (art. 661.4) or does not start within the time limits defined by art. 613.7.

640            Protests
640.1          A Jury must only accept a protest if it is based upon physical evidence.

640.2           A Jury is only permitted to re-evaluate its previous deci- sion where new evidence exists that relates to the origi- nal Jury decision.

640.3          All Jury decisions are final except those that may be protested under art.641. Appeals can be made as per art. 647.1.1.

628.13     比赛服装或竞赛器材上带有淫秽名称或者标识的（本 规则第 207. 1 条），或在比赛场地的行为举止缺乏运 动员风范（本规则第 205.5 条、第 223.1. 1 条）；
628.14     实际上已经在比赛中出发，但随后被仲裁委员会认 定为违反本规则第 627 条。

629       取消资格
运动员有如下行为将被取消资格 ：

629.1      弄虚作假参加比赛 ；
629.2      危及人身、财产安全或者造成实际伤害、损害 ；


629.3      未正确通过旗门（本规则第 661.4 条），或没有按本 规则第 613.7 条在限定时间内出发。

640       抗议
640.1      仲裁委员会仅接受以实质性证据为基础的抗议。


640.2      仲裁委员会只有发现与其原决定有关的新证据时， 才可以重审先前的决定。


640.3      除根据本规则第 641 条提出抗议外，仲裁委员会的 所有决定均为最终决定。可根据本规则第 647.1. 1 条 提出申诉。

COMPETITION RULES (ICR)

641            Types of Protests
641.1           Against admittance of competitors or their competition equipment,

641.2           Against the course or its condition,

641.3           Against a competitor or against an official during the race, 641.4          Against disqualifications,

641.5          Against timekeeping,

641.6          Against instructions of the Jury.

642           Place of Submittal
The various protests are to be submitted as follows:

642.1           Protests according to the art. 641.1 - 641.6 at the loca- tion designated on the official notice board or at a place announced at a team captains’meeting.

643           Deadlines for Submittal

643.1          Against the admittance of a competitor:
- before the Draw.

643.2          Against the course or its condition:
- not later than 60 minutes before the beginning of the race.

641       抗议的类型
641.1      对授予运动员参赛资格或者认可竞赛器材方面的决 定的抗议 ；

641.2      对赛道或其状况的抗议 ；
641.3      比赛期间对某位运动员或官员的抗议 ；
641.4      对取消资格的抗议 ；
641.5      对计时的抗议 ；
641.6      对仲裁委员会指令的抗议。
642       提交地点
各类抗议应提交至如下地点 ：

642.1      根据本规则第 641. 1 条至第 641.6 条提出的抗议，提 交至官方公告牌所标示的地点，或领队会议上宣布 的地点。
643       提交期限
643.1       运动员参赛资格方面的 ：
- 抽签前。

643.2       赛道及其状况方面的 ：
- 不迟于比赛开始前 60 分钟。






THE INTERNATIONAL SKI
COMPETITION RULES (ICR)

2nd Section   Rules Common to Alpine Events 第二部分    高山滑雪竞赛通则






643.3          Against  a  competitor or competitor’s equipment  or against an official because of irregular behaviour during the competition:
- within 15 minutes after the last competitor has passed the finish.

643.4          Against disqualification:
- within 15 minutes after the posting or announcement of the disqualification.

643.5          Against the timekeeping:
- within 15 minutes after the posting of the unofficial re- sult list.

643.6          Against all instructions of the Jury:
- immediately and no later than the deadlines for submit- tal of protest according to the art. 643.4.

644            Form of Protests
644.1           Protests are to be submitted in writing.

644.2           As exceptions, protests according to the art. 641.3, 641.4 and 641.5 can be made verbally (art. 617.2.2).

644.3          Protests must be substantiated in detail. Proof must be submitted and any evidence must be included.

644.4          CHF 100. -- or the equivalent in another valid currency

643.3      对某运动员、其竞赛器材或某官员比赛期间的不合 常规行为 ：

- 最后一位参赛运动员通过终点后 15 分钟内。


643.4       对取消资格的抗议 ：
- 取消资格公告或宣布后 15 分钟内。


643.5       对计时的抗议 ：
- 公告非正式成绩列表后 15 分钟内。


643.6       针对仲裁委员会指令的 ：
- 立即提出，且不晚于本规则第 643.4 条规定的最后 提交期限。
644       抗议的形式
644.1      抗议应采用书面形式提交。
644.2      根据本规则第 641.3 条、第 641.4 条和第 641.5 条所提 抗议，作为例外，可以口头提出（本规则第 617.2.2 条）。
644.3      抗议必须依据详细事实，并提交证明抗议成立的所 有证据。

644.4      提交抗议时，须随附 100 瑞士法郎或其他等值有效

must accompany the protest. This deposit will be re- turned if the protest is upheld, otherwise it goes to the account of the FIS.
644.5           A protest may be withdrawn by the protesting party be-
fore the publication of a decision by the Jury.
In this case, the money deposit must be returned. A with- drawal of the protest is not possible when the Jury or a member of the Jury takes, an intermediate decision for reasons of time, e.g. a decision“with reserve”.

644.6          Protests not submitted on time in the correct manner or submitted without the protest fee will not be considered.

645           Authorisation
The following are authorised to submit protests:
- National Ski Associations
- Trainers
- Team Captains.

646            Settlement of Protests by the Jury
646.1          The Jury meets to deal with the protests at a predeter- mined place and time fixed and announced by it.

646.2           In dealing with a protest against disqualification (art.
661.4), the gate judge and, if needed, the gate judge of the adjacent gate combinations or other involved offi- cials, the competitor in question and the protesting team

货币作为押金。如果抗议成立，该押金退回 ；否则 转入国际雪联账户。


644.5        仲裁委员会的决定公布前，提出抗议方可以撤回 抗议。
此时，押金须退回。但仲裁委员会或其成员因时间  原因已作出了居中决定（例如“有保留意见”的决定） 的，不能再撤回抗议。


644.6        未按正确方式及时提交或未随附押金的抗议不予 受理。
645       抗议权
有权提交抗议者包括 ：
- 国家滑雪协会 ；
- 教练员 ；
- 领队。

646       仲裁委员会对抗议的处理
646.1      仲裁委员会在其事先确定和宣布的地点和时间举行 会议，处理抗议问题。

646.2      处理针对取消资格（本规则第 661.4 条）提出的抗 议时，技术代表或裁判长必须邀请旗门裁判员参加； 如果需要的话，还要邀请临近旗门区的旗门裁判员  或其他涉及此事的官员、当事运动员、以及提出抗

captain or trainer must be invited to attend by the TD or Referee.
In addition any other requested evidence such as video- tape, photos, and films should be checked.

646.3           At the vote on the protest, only the Jury members are to be present. The TD chairs the proceedings. Minutes of the proceedings are to be kept and signed by all voting members of the Jury. The decision requires a majority of all voting members of the Jury, not just of those present. In case of a tie, the TD’s vote is decisive.
The principle of a free evaluation of the evidence is maintained. The rules on which the decision is to be based must be applied and interpreted in such a way that fair proceedings are guaranteed.

646.4           The decision is to be made public immediately after the proceedings by posting on the official notice board with the publication time stated.

647           Right of Appeals

647.1          The Appeal

647.1.1             Can be made:
- against the decisions of the Jury regarding monetary fines as per art.224.11
- against the decision of the Jury to terminate a race (art. 625)

议的领队或教练员参加会议。

此外，还应检查其他任何需要的证据，如录像带、 照片、电影胶片等。
646.3      投票表决关于抗议的处理决定时，只有仲裁委员会  成员可以在场。技术代表主持投票程序。投票过程  记录经所有有表决权的仲裁委员成员签名后留存。 决定根据有表决权的仲裁委员会成员的简单多数作 出，而不仅仅是根据出席会议人员的多数。如果投  票出现平局，技术代表拥有最终决定权。
在证据的采信上要坚持自由心证原则。在法律适用 上要以保证程序公平的方式适用和解释作出决定所 依据的规则。


646.4      在投票程序结束后，决定要立即公布，并在官方公 告板上张贴，注明发布时间。


647       申诉的权利
647.1       申诉
647.1.1              申诉可以针对以下事由 ：
- 根据本规则第 224. 11 条，不服仲裁委员会有关罚 款的决定 ；
- 不服仲裁委员会终止比赛的决定 （本规则第 625 条）；





THE INTERNATIONAL SKI
COMPETITION RULES (ICR)


- against the recommendation of the Jury that a terminat- ed race should count for FIS points
- against the official result. This appeal has to be directed exclusively against an obvious and proved calculation mistake.
647.1.2             Appeals must be submitted to the FIS Office only by the National Ski Association.

647.1.3             Time Limits

647.1.3.1     Appeals against Jury decisions must be submitted to the Appeals Commission within 48 hours of their announce- ment.

647.1.3.2     The official results may be appealed to the Council via the FIS Office within 30 days for matters that are outside the competence of the jury.

647.1.4             Decisions concerning appeals are taken by:
- the Appeals Commission
- the FIS Court.

647.2          Postponing Effect
Evidence submitted (protest, appeal) will not cause a postponement of the sanction.

647.3          Submission
All appeals must be in writing. Proof and evidence are to

647.1.4       下列组织对申诉作出处理决定 ：

be included.Appeals submitted after the deadlines (art.

650           Rules regarding the Homologation of Competition Courses

650.1           General
All competitions must take place on FIS-approved (ho- mologated) competition courses.

650.1.1            The competition courses proposed for homologation must comply with the technical requirements of the arts.
701, 801, 901 and 1001.

650.1.2             Exceptions
Exceptions may be granted on request.
Only the FIS Council can grant exceptions or deviations from the prescribed technical data.
The National  Ski Association in question and the Sub-Committee for Alpine Courses submit the proposals for exceptions. If exceptions are granted the exception is valid from date of approval until revoked.

650.2           Request
The request for the homologation of a competition course is to be directed to the Sub-Committee for Alpine Courses through the appropriate National Ski Associ- ation and accompanied by the documents as per art. 650.3.

由和证据。最后期限（本规则第 647.1.3. 1 条和第 647.1.3.2 条）之后提交的，国际雪联拒绝受理。
650       赛道认证相关规则

650.1       一般原则
所有比赛都必须在国际雪联批准（认证）的赛道上 举行。
650.1.1              申请认证的赛道必须达到本规则第701条、第801条、 第 901 条及第 1001 条规定的技术要求。


650.1.2             例外
依申请可以准予例外。
只有国际雪联理事会能够准予例外或者技术数据上 与规定的偏差。
相关的国家滑雪协会和国际雪联高山滑雪场地分委 员会可以共同提出请求批准例外的建议。经批准的 特例自批准之日起生效，直到撤消批准为止。


650.2       请求
赛道认证的请求应通过相关的国家滑雪协会直接提 交给高山滑雪场地分委员会，并随附本规则第 650.3 条规定的文件。






THE INTERNATIONAL SKI
COMPETITION RULES (ICR)

2nd Section   Rules Common to Alpine Events 第二部分    高山滑雪竞赛通则






650.3           Documents
The request for the homologation of a competition course must be accompanied by the following six elements:

650.3.1             A description of the competition course, containing:
- contact address with telephone number and e-mail
- the name of the competition course
- the location of the competition course
- the type of alpine event(s) for which the homologation is requested (see art.201.6.2)
- in case of re-homologation, the old homologation num- ber and the name of the inspector that approved it
- the start point expressed in meters above sea level
- the finish point expressed in meters above sea level
- the vertical drop expressed in meters
- the surface length of the competition course expressed in meters (real developed length)
- the average gradient, the maximum gradient, the mini- mum gradient (in percentages)
- emergency evacuation arrangements for injured com- petitors
- possible helicopter landing sites evacuation distance to the nearest hospital in kilometres and time, in winter conditions, and medical facilities available on site
- possible water supply for the competition course
- artificial snow-making installations
- a description of the access facilities to the start and finish areas, and of the uphill transport with the turn- around time (time necessary from Finish to Start)

650.3       文件
赛道认证请求必须随附以下 6 份要素文件 ：


650.3.1       对赛道的说明，包括 ：
- 联系地址及电话号码、电子邮箱 ；
- 赛道名称 ；
- 赛道位置 ；
- 认证拟举办的比赛项目的类别 （另见本规则第
201.6.2 条）；
- 属于重新认证的，原认证号码及批准该认证的认证 官的姓名 ；
- 用米表示的起点海拔高度 ；
- 用米表示的终点海拔高度 ；
- 用米表示的垂直落差 ；
- 用米表示的赛道表面长度（实际展开长度）；

- 平均坡度、最大坡度、最小坡度（用百分比表示）；

- 受伤运动员的紧急转运安排 ；

- 可能的直升机停靠点，在冬季以公里数和时间计的 转运至最近医院的距离，场地现有医疗设施 ；

- 赛道的可用水源 ；
- 人工造雪设备 ；
- 前往起点和终点区域的运输设施的说明，上山运输 以及周转时间（从终点到起点时间）的说明 ；





THE INTERNATIONAL SKI
COMPETITION RULES (ICR)


- a description of the start and finish areas including de- tails of the terrain, aspect and facilities for spectators, and description of the shelters for the competitors at the start and finish
- a description of the communication system and the available number of lines for Timing (pairs) showing type and number of underground/ permanent or tempo- rary cables including number of outlets along the com- petition course
- details about available radio apparatus

650.3.2             A map with the competition course  shown on it: this document should show the course’s location within the rest of the ski resort, lifts, other courses, parking lots, etc.

650.3.3            A profile indicating the vertical drop and the lengths (horizontal and actual (slope) measured on site) of the competition course (contours at the same scale) includ- ing gradients.

650.3.4             A large and comprehensive image on which the competi- tion course is marked. The size shall be at least 900x900 pixels. The image should be taken preferably from an opposite slope. If that is not possible, then an oblique ae- rial image will be acceptable.

650.3.5             A plan of the entire competition course with all details and data indicated, such as lift towers, groups of trees, snow-making hydrants, snow fences, steep sections,

- 起点终点区域包括地形、地貌以及服务观众的设施 的详细说明，以及起点和终点运动员休息棚的说明；


- 通信系统及其赛道上可供计时系统使用的线路的 数量（多少对）的说明，显示地下或者永久、临时 的电缆的型号及数量，包括沿赛道部署的接线端口 的数量 ；

- 可用对讲机设备的详细说明。

650.3.3       表示垂直落差和赛道（同一比例等高线）长度（水 平长度及实际坡道长度）、坡度的剖面图。



650.3.4       一张上面标出赛道的全景大幅照片，像素至少达到 900x900。照片应从赛道对面的山坡上拍摄。如果无 法做到这一点，那么倾斜的航空照片也可以接受。



650.3.5             整条赛道的草图，标示出所有的细节和数据，如缆  车塔台、树林、造雪机、雪道防护网、陡峭区段、 弯道、雪道交叉口等，以及海拔、段面和滑雪场名

curves, trail intersections, etc. and information on eleva- tions, section and resort names. The purpose of the plan is primarily to provide the inspector with condensed in- formation on the actual state of the competition course, any improvements planned and also the potential loca- tion of permanent safety nets (A nets).

650.3.6             A certification that any development/ improvement work on the ski slopes subject to approval or re-approval has been made in accordance with the existing national laws and with local and national regulations relating to the environment.
The environmental certification shall be provided only in case of:
- a first homologation, except if it is an already existing track or on land that needs no modification.
- a re-approval, only if additional, substantial work has been done.

650.4          The Homologation Inspector

650.4.1             Description
To be proposed to FIS for consideration as International Homologation Inspector, individuals must first be rec- ognised within their National Ski Association as having completed the National Ski Association education and training process (if any) and as having been active and competent as a National Ski Association inspector, for both Speed (DH, SG) and Technical (GS, SL) events.

650.3.6      根据现行的国家法律以及与环境有关的当地和国家 的法规，已经对需要批准或重新批准的滑雪坡道的 全部开发 / 改进工作进行了认证。


环境认证仅在以下情况下应当提供 ：
- 赛道是第一次认证，但既有雪道或位于无需修改的 土地上者除外 ；

- 重新批准，只有在完成了额外的实质性工作的情况 下才需要提供。

650.4       认证官
650.4.1      说明
任何个人被推荐给国际雪联，并由其认证为国际认 证官，必须先完成其所属国家滑雪协会举办的教育 和培训课程，并被所属国家滑雪协会认可，并作为 该国家滑雪协会的认证官在其国内的速度项目（滑 降、超级大回转）和技术项目（回转、大回转）比 赛中积极而称职地工作。





THE INTERNATIONAL SKI
COMPETITION RULES (ICR)


To hold a valid FIS Homologation Inspector licence the inspector must have a solid experience of several years in Alpine Skiing competitions like,as an example, Na- tional Ski Association Homologation Inspector or FIS TD/Referee or Chief of Race/Course or high level Team Coach/Athlete, and should have skills such as engineer- ing, GIS, architecture, forestry, relevant computer skills and to be physically capable.
This experience allows the inspector to assess correctly the suitability of the competition courses with FIS tech- nical requirements of the requested event (vertical drop, gradient, width, etc) and especially assess correctly the risks of a given competition course; the inspector must inform the Homologation Applicant about technical issues and mainly about safety issues for which the in- spector must be able to propose solutions.

650.4.2             Nomination, Education and Development
Candidates must participate in at least 3 inspections with favourable recommendation of experienced Inspec- tors (in agreement with the Sub-Committee Chair) and submit their own documentation and Inspection Report to the Chair. Candidates should also participate at the bi-annual Update and attend the annual Sub-Committee meeting session.
After successful completion of previous necessary steps, candidates obtain a valid Homologation Inspector li- cense and can be assigned to individual missions.
The Sub-Committee may decide not to issue an Inspector

要获得国际雪联的认证官执照，认证官必须有多年 在高山滑雪比赛方面的丰富的经验，例如作为国家 滑雪协会的认证官或者国际雪联的技术代表或者裁 判长、竞赛长或者赛道长，或者优秀代表队的教练 或者运动员，并具备工程、地理、建筑、林业和相 关计算机技能等，并且有良好的身体素质。


上述经验使得认证员得以正确地评估赛道是否具备 国际雪联有关举办相应比赛的技术要求（垂直落差、 坡度、宽度等），特别是要正确评估使用该赛道举办  比赛的风险。认证官必须告知赛道认证申请人有关  的技术问题和主要的安全问题，并能够向其提出解  决方案。



650.4.2       提名、教育与发展
认证官候选人必须参加至少 3 次认证并得到有经验 的认证官的有利的建议（与国际雪联高山滑雪场地 分委员会主任达成一致）并向国际雪联高山滑雪场 地分委员会主任提交其文件材料和认证报告。认证 官候选人还必须参加每 2 年举行一次的进修培训及 认证分委员会的年会。

在成功完成前述必需的步骤后，认证官候选人获得 有效的赛道认证执照并可以受指派独立执行任务了。

认证官候选人未满足起码要求或者被认定还不称职

license if the candidate has not fulfilled all necessary requirements or is deemed to be unsuitable and needs to continue to train.

650.4.3             Appointment
The Chair of the Sub-Committee for Alpine Courses will study the homologation request and appoint an inspec- tor to examine the competition course. The Inspector for Downhill and Super-G courses (including Downhill courses to be used for Entry League races) should not belong to the country requesting a first homologation.
Sufficient space must be provided on Downhill, Giant Slalom and Super-G courses, or on an emergency track or road or on the competition course itself, for the evac- uation of competitors injured during the competition or training.

650.5          Homologation Procedure

650.5.1             The Applicant
The Applicant (ski resort, owner, organiser, club) will send the request for homologation through its National Ski Association to the Chair of the Sub-Committee for Alpine Courses and will deliver copy of the required documents submitted with the request, before the on-site inspection, to the assigned Inspector. In the request the Applicant and the National Ski Association must clearly recognise that the directed improvements of the competi- tion course and the instructions for safety are mandatory for

并需要继续培训的，国际雪联高山滑雪场地分委员 会可以决定不授予认证官执照。


650.4.3       认证官的任命
国际雪联高山滑雪场地分委员会主任初步研究认证 请求后，任命一名认证官前往检查该赛道。滑降或 者超级大回转赛道（包括用于入门级比赛的滑降赛 道）的认证官不应来自首次申请认证的国家。


在滑降、大回转和超级大回转赛道上，或在应急用 的雪道、道路上，必须留有充足的空地以便转运在 比赛或训练中受伤的运动员。

650.5.2             The National Ski Association
The request for homologation prepared by the Applicant must be submitted by its National Ski Association to the Chair of the Sub-Committee for Alpine Courses. The National Ski Association will check if the Applicant has reimbursed the Inspector’s expenses and if not will re- quire the Applicant to meet this obligation.

650.5.3             The Inspector
After the request for homologation has been received by the Chair of the Sub-Committee for Alpine Courses, from the Applicant via the National Ski Association, the Chair will appoint an Inspector. The Inspector im- mediately contacts the Applicant about the time for the inspection and receives a copy of the homologation doc- uments before the inspection.
After the inspection, if no further work is needed, the Inspector writes the Inspection Report. In case im- provements are required on the competition course, the Inspector directs these to the Applicant and makes sure that those works have been carried out before filling the final on-line Inspection Report. After checking all other documents, the Inspector uploads the complete set of documents on the FIS Website through the“Homologa- tion On Line System”.
It is left to the discretion of the Inspector to decide




650.5.2      国家滑雪协会
由申请方准备的认证请求须由其所属的国家滑雪协 会转交国际雪联高山滑雪场地分委员会主任。国家 滑雪协会要检查申请方是否已经报销了认证官的支 出，并责令违者履行此项义务。



650.5.3      认证官
国际雪联高山滑雪场地分委员会主任收到申请方通 过国家滑雪协会提出的认证请求后，即指派认证官。 认证官立即联系申请方确定视察时间，并在视察前  收到认证申请文件的副本。



视察后，赛道不需要作进一步的整改工作的，认证 官撰写《视察报告》。要求对赛道采取改进措施的， 认证官向申请方指出并确保这些改进工作在线上最 终完成《视察报告》时已经切实整改到位。在检查 完所有其他文件后，认证官将已经完成的整套文件 通过“赛道在线认证系统”上传至国际雪联官网。



考虑到冬天情况有所不同，在夏季视察后是否需要

whether, in addition to the summer inspection, a second inspection in winter will be necessary in consideration of different conditions in winter. This applies especially to safety regulations and the placing of nets. In case the competition course is not suitable for international races or for the given event, the Inspector writes the Inspection Report and sends it to the Chair of the Sub Committee for Alpine Courses. The request will then be deleted and the National Ski Association will be informed.

650.5.4              Issue and Publication of the FIS Homologation Certificate
The Chair of the Sub-Committee for Alpine Courses will examine and ratify the documents received via the“Ho- mologation On Line System ”. The Chair may ask the Inspector for further clarifications or amendments as the Chair has the right to refuse the Certificate’s issue if the Chair considers that the race competition course or the documentation are not compliant with FIS rules or FIS standards. If the inspection report is positive then the Homologation Certificate will be issued and immediately published on the FIS website, together with the complete set of documents (Homologation Booklet) that will be visible to the authorised FIS Members (TDs, Inspectors, etc) having a valid FIS Member access.
The FIS System will automatically send a digital copy of the Homologation Certificate and Booklet to the Applicant, to its National Ski Association and to the Inspector, while the original‘paper’copy of the Homologation Certificate will be sent by standard mail only to the Applicant.

国际雪联的信息系统自动将《认证证书》及《认证 文档》的数字文件副本发送给申请方、其所属国家 滑雪协会和认证官。《认证证书》的原始“纸质”文 本以标准邮件形式只发送申请方。
