650.5.4.1     The Homologation Certificate itself sets out the name and event of the competition course and its technical data. The registration number of the certificate indicates the total number of homologated competition courses, the month and year in which the Certificate was issued. The expiration date is indicated.

650.5.4.2     The Applicant’s National  Ski Association will be in- voiced for the relative Homologation Fee (depending on how many competition courses and how many alpine events on the same competition course), to cover the ad- ministrative costs.

650.5.5             Expiration of the Application
If the requested work has not been completed within four years after the inspection is carried out and the ho- mologation cannot be granted, the competition course will be deleted from the list of pending homologation applications. For further consideration a new application is required.

650.5.6             Validity of the FIS Homologation Certificate

650.5.6.1     Downhill and Super-G
The certificate is valid from the date of issue: it will ex- pire on 1st July*, five (5) years later. A re-homologation must be carried out before a new certificate is issued.
*) = For the Southern Hemisphere 1st November.

650.5.4.1    《认证证书》会注明赛道名称、比赛项目类型及技术 数据。证书的注册号显示认证赛道总数、认证证书 的签发年月。失效日期也会注明。




650.5.4.2      申请方的国家滑雪协会会收到认证费的相关发票（取 决于多少条赛道以及同一赛道上有多少项高山滑雪 比赛项目），以支付赛道认证的管理费用。



650.5.5      申请的失效
视察结束后 4 年内要求申请方整改的工作未完成， 且认证请求未获得批准的，该赛道将从待认证申请 名单中删除。希望国际雪联再做考虑的，需要重新 申请。



650.5.6       国际雪联认证证书的有效性

650.5.6.1      滑降和超级大回转
证书自签发之日起生效 ：有效期至 5 年后的 7 月 1 日 *。签发新证书之前必须重新进行认证。
*) = 南半球为 11 月 1 日。






THE INTERNATIONAL SKI
COMPETITION RULES (ICR)

2nd Section   Rules Common to Alpine Events 第二部分    高山滑雪竞赛通则






650.5.6.2     Slalom and Giant Slalom
The certificate is valid from the date of issue: it will ex- pire on 1st July*, ten(10) years later. A re-homologation must be carried out before a new certificate is issued.
*) = For the Southern Hemisphere 1st November.
650.5.6.3     For all Events
Homologation certificates are valid (within periods in art. 650.5.6.1 and 650.5.6.2) as long as no natural or ar- tificial changes or changes in the regulations or technical requirements have occurred.
Natural changes can consist of:
- erosion, land slides or the terrain becoming overgrown. Artificial changes are:
- the construction of buildings, lifts,
- the construction of shelters, parks, roads or tracks etc.
- the installation of snow-making hydrants, snow reten- tion fences or other significant hardware.

650.5.7             Compulsory Report
The National Ski Association which has obtained the homologation of a competition course is responsible to report to the Sub-Committee for Alpine Courses when any natural or artificial changes have occurred (see art. 650.5.6.3). The Chair is then allowed to investigate and if necessary order a new inspection.

650.5.8             Additional TD Report
Technical Delegates may submit Additional Reports

650.5.6.2     回转和大回转
证书自签发之日起生效 ：有效期至 10 年后的 7 月 1 日 *。颁发新证书前必须重新进行认证。
*) = 南半球为 11 月 1 日。

650.5.6.3     针对所有项目
只要没有自然的或人为的变化，在规则或技术要求 上也没有变化的，认证证书持续有效（在本规则第 650.5.6. 1 条和第 650.5.6.2 条规定的期限内）。
自然变化包括 ：
- 侵蚀、滑坡或赛道被植物覆盖。 人为变化包括 ：
- 修建建筑物、缆车 ；
- 兴建屋棚、公园、道路或轨道等 ；
- 安装造雪机、雪道防护栏或其他重要硬件设施。


650.5.7      强制报告义务
获得赛道认证的国家滑雪协会有义务向国际雪联高 山滑雪场地分委员会报告赛道上已发生的任何自然 或者人为的变化 ( 参见本规则第 650.5.6.3 条 )。主 任遂要求调查，必要时可以指令进行视察。



650.5.8       技术代表的附加报告
技术代表无论何时发现与赛道有关的问题或者不遵





THE INTERNATIONAL SKI
COMPETITION RULES (ICR)


to the Chair of the Sub Committee for Alpine Courses whenever experiencing problems related to the compe- tition courses or non-compliance with current FIS Rules and Regulations: it is duty of the Chair to investigate and in appropriate cases suspend the homologation.

650.5.9             Relationship between Homologation, Snow and Weather as well as Special Conditions
An organiser should not depend entirely on the homolo- gation of a competition course by the FIS, but also take note of the prevailing snow and weather conditions e.g. a Downhill course homologated by the FIS may be unsuit- able for holding Downhill races when there is insuffi- cient snow depth, unfavourable surface snow conditions, dense fog, heavy snow fall, storm or rain.

655           Competitions under Artificial Light
655.1          Competitions under artificial lights are permitted.
655.2           Lighting must meet the following specifications:
655.2.1             The light level anywhere on the course must not be less than 80 lux, measured parallel to the surface. The light- ing should be as uniform as Possible.

655.2.2             Floodlights must be placed so that the light does not al- ter the topography of the competition course. The light must enable the competitor to discern the terrain  and

2nd Section   Rules Common to Alpine Events 第二部分    高山滑雪竞赛通则


守现行《国际雪联竞赛规则》及规定的事项，都可 以向国际雪联高山滑雪赛场地分委员会主任提交《附 加报告》。主任有义务安排调查并可以暂停认证证书 的效力。


650.5.9             认证、雪况、天气以及特殊条件之间的关系

组织方不应完全依靠国际雪联对赛道的认证，也应 注意当时的普遍雪况和天气情况，如由国际雪联认 证的滑降赛道，当积雪深度不够、积雪表面的情况 不适合比赛，有浓雾、暴雪、暴风或降雨时，则不 适合举行滑降比赛。



655       人工灯光下的比赛
655.1       允许在人工灯光下进行比赛。
655.2      灯光照明须符合以下具体规定 ：
655.2.1             赛道上任何地方的光亮度在测量平行地面亮度时应 不低于 80 勒克斯。各处灯光亮度应尽可能一致。


655.2.2             必须安装泛光灯，以避免灯光改变赛道的地势形态。 光线必须能让参赛者辨别地形，并且不能改变深度  感知或清晰度。






THE INTERNATIONAL SKI
COMPETITION RULES (ICR)

2nd Section   Rules Common to Alpine Events 第二部分    高山滑雪竞赛通则






must not alter the depth perception or definition.

655.2.3             The lights should not cast the competitor’s shadow into the racing line and should not blind the competitor by glare.

655.3           The TD together with the Jury must check in advance that the lighting conforms to the rules.

655.4           The TD must submit a supplementary report on the qual- ity of the lighting.

660           Gate Judges ’Instructions

661           Control of Passage (Explanation)
661.1                All gate judges must receive a check card, along with weatherproof covering where necessary, for each run that will show:
Name of the gate judge, Number(s) of the gate(s) for which they are responsible and designation of the run (1st or 2nd)

661.2           If a competitor fails to pass through a gate (or a gate marker) correctly according to art. 661.4 the Gate Judge must immediately record the competitor’s bib number and the gate number(s) where the fault occurred.

661.2.1             A drawing of the fault committed is essential.



655.2.3             灯光不应将运动员的身影投射在赛道上，也不应使 运动员感到眩目。


655.3      技术代表会同仲裁委员会须事先检查灯光照明是否 符合规则。

655.4      技术代表必须提交关于照明质量的补充报告。


660       旗门裁判员工作指南
661       旗门监控（解释）
661.1      旗门裁判员必须人手一张检查卡，如有必要需配有
防雨雪封皮，每轮滑行都会载明 ：

旗门裁判员姓名 ；旗门裁判员所负责的旗门号码， 并且注明第几轮滑行（第一轮或第二轮）。


661.2      运动员没有遵照本规则第 661.4 条的规定正确通过 旗门（或旗门标识）的，旗门裁判员必须立即记录 运动员的出发号码和其出现失误的旗门号码。


661.2.1             有必要绘出造成失误的示意图。






THE INTERNATIONAL SKI
COMPETITION RULES (ICR)

2nd Section   Rules Common to Alpine Events 第二部分    高山滑雪竞赛通则






661.3           Should a competitor receive outside help, for instance after a fall, the Gate Judge must record this on the check card. (art. 628. 13)

661.4           Correct Passage

661.4.1             A gate has been passed correctly when both the compet- itor’s ski tips and both feet have crossed the gate line. If a competitor loses a ski, without committing a fault, e.g. not by straddling a pole, then the tip of the remaining ski and both feet must have crossed the gate line. This rule also applies when a competitor has to climb back up to a gate. (art. 614.2.3)
661.4.1.1     The gate line in Downhill, Giant Slalom and Super-G, where a gate consists of two pairs of poles holding gate panels between them, is the shortest imaginary line be- tween the turning pole and the outside gate at snow level (art. 661).
661.4.1.2     The gate line in Slalom is the shortest imaginary line be- tween the turning pole and the outside pole

661.4.1.3     If a competitor removes a pole from its vertical position before both the competitor’s ski tips and both feet have passed the gate line, the ski tips and feet must still pass the original gate line (marks in the snow). This is also valid in the case of a missing turning pole (or gate).

661.3      运动员获得外力帮助的（如摔倒后），旗门裁判员必  须将这类失误记录在检查卡上（本规则第 628. 13条）。


661.4       正确通过旗门
661.4.1             运动员两只滑雪板的尖端和双脚均越过旗门线的视 为正确通过旗门。运动员一只滑雪板脱落但没有产 生骑跨回转杆等失误的，所剩另一只雪板尖端和双 脚必须均越过旗门线。当运动员必须登山回到旗门  位置时，这一规则同样适用（本规则第 614.2.3 条）。



661.4.1.1          滑降、大回转、超级大回转的每个旗门由 2 对上面
有旗门布的旗门杆组成。在雪面上旗门绕行杆和 外侧旗门之间的最短假想线段为旗门线（本规则第 661 条）。


661.4.1.2     回转旗门线是绕行杆和外侧杆之间的最短的假想 线段。

661.4.1.3     运动员的两只滑雪板尖端和双脚未通过旗门线前旗 杆倒斜，运动员的滑雪板尖端和双脚仍必须通过原 旗门线（雪中标识）。本条款在旗门杆（或旗门）缺 失时也同样适用。






THE INTERNATIONAL SKI
COMPETITION RULES (ICR)

2nd Section   Rules Common to Alpine Events 第二部分    高山滑雪竞赛通则






661.4.2             In Parallel, the passage is correct when both ski tips and both feet have passed the turning pole in the direction of the turn (art. 661, fig. B).

662           Importance of the Task of the Gate Judge
662.1          Each gate judge should have a thorough knowledge of the competition rules. Gate judges are required to follow instructions from the Jury.

662.2           The decision handed down by a gate judge must be clear and unbiased.Gate judges must declare a fault only when they are convinced that a fault has been committed.

662.3           Gate judges can consult the adjacent gate judge in or- der to confirm their opinion and can even demand via a member of the Jury that the race is brieﬂy interrupted, so that the tracks on the course may be checked.

662.4           When an adjacent gate judge, a member of the Jury or an official video controller makes a report concerning a competitor which differs from the notes of the gate judge in question, the Jury may freely interpret these notes in view of a possible disqualification of a competitor or of a decision concerning a protest.

661.4.2             在平行式比赛中，两只雪板尖端和双脚在转弯方向 通过转弯杆为正确通过（本规则第 661 条图 B）。


662       旗门裁判员的职责任务

662.1      各旗门裁判员均应对比赛规则有全面了解。规则要
求旗门裁判员遵照仲裁委员会的指令行事。


662.2      旗门裁判员所作判决必须清楚公正，他只有在确信 失误确实发生后才能公布。


662.3      旗门裁判员也可与临近的旗门裁判员协商以确证自 己的判断，甚至可以向仲裁委员会成员提出比赛暂 时中断的要求，以便检查赛道上的痕迹。


662.4      当临近的旗门裁判员、仲裁委员会成员或官方视频 监控员就某运动员作出的报告与当事的旗门裁判员 作出的记录有出入时，仲裁委员会基于运动员有可 能被取消资格或对仲裁委员会的决定提出抗议这两 方面的考虑，自由裁量这些记录。






THE INTERNATIONAL SKI
COMPETITION RULES (ICR)

2nd Section   Rules Common to Alpine Events 第二部分    高山滑雪竞赛通则






663           Giving Information to a Competitor
663.1           In the case of an error or a fall, competitors are permit- ted to ask the gate judge if a fault was committed and the gate judge, if asked, must inform the competitors if they have committed a fault that would lead to disqualifica- tion.
663.2           Competitors are fully responsible for their actions and cannot hold the gate judge responsible.

664          Immediate Announcement of  Dis- qualifying Faults
664.1           The Jury may decide that the gate judge will signal a disqualifying fault immediately by raising a flag of a particular colour, by a sound signal, or by other means as provided by the organisers (art. 670 video control).

664.2          The gate judge must record all infringements on the check card regardless of immediate announcements.

664.3           The gate judge is required to give information to Jury members on request.

665           Duties of the Gate Judge on comple- tion of the 1st and 2nd run
665.1          The chief gate judge (or assistant) is required to collect

663       向运动员提供信息
663.1      运动员发生失误或摔倒的，可以向旗门裁判员询问 是否犯规，如果被问及此事，裁判员必须告知运动 员是否出现了丧失比赛资格的失误。



663.2        运动员要对自己的行为负全部责任，不能要求旗门 裁判员对此负责。

664       及时公布导致取消资格的失误

664.1      仲裁委员会可以决定，旗门裁判员应立即通过升起 特定颜色的旗帜、发出声音信号或通过组织方提供 的其他方式，发出判定取消资格的信号（参照本规 则第 670 条“视频监控”）。

664.2      无论是否立即宣布，旗门裁判员都必须将所有犯规 行为记录在自己的检查卡上。

664.3      旗门裁判员应根据要求向仲裁委员会成员提供信息。


665       在第一轮滑行和第二轮滑行完成时旗门 裁判员的职责
665.1      根据要求，旗门裁判长（或其助手）在每轮滑行结






THE INTERNATIONAL SKI
COMPETITION RULES (ICR)

2nd Section   Rules Common to Alpine Events 第二部分    高山滑雪竞赛通则






all the check cards immediately after each run and to pass them on to the Referee in the finish.

666           Duties of the Gate Judge at the Con- clusion of the Race
666.1           Each gate judge who has recorded a disqualifying fault or who has been witness to an incident leading to a re- run must be available to the Jury until after the settle- ment of any protests.

666.2           It is the responsibility of the Technical Delegate to dis- miss a gate judge who is waiting to be called by the Jury.

667           Supplemental Duties of the Gate Judge
667.1           Gate judges may be asked to perform other duties after they perform their required function, including the re- placement of gate poles, torn or missing panels.

667.2          They should assist in keeping the course clear and re- move any markings made on the course by competitors or third parties.

667.3           Competitors who are obstructed during their run must stop immediately and report this to the nearest gate judge. The gate judge must enter the details of the inci- dent on the check card and have the card available for the Jury at the end of the 1st or 2nd run. The competitor

束后均应立即收集所有的检查卡并转交给终点区的 裁判长。
666       旗门裁判员在比赛结束时的职责

666.1      每位记录了导致取消资格失误，或目睹了导致重滑 事故的旗门裁判员，都必须做到仲裁委员会随叫随 到，直到抗议解决时为止。


666.2      技术代表有责任解除等候仲裁委员会传唤的旗门裁 判员的职务。
667       旗门裁判员的其他职责
667.1      旗门裁判员完成指派任务之余还可能应要求履行其
他职责，包括更换旗门杆或撕脱的旗门布。


667.2      旗门裁判员应当协助保持赛道畅通，协助清除由运
动员或第三方在赛道上留下的任何标记。


667.3      运动员在滑行中受到阻碍时必须立即停止比赛，向 最近的旗门裁判员报告。旗门裁判员必须在检查卡 上记下这一事故的详细情况，并且在第一轮或第二 轮滑行结束时向仲裁委员会提供有关这一情况的记 录。运动员可以向仲裁委员会任一成员申请重滑。

may apply to any member of the Jury for a re-run.

668            Location and support of the Gate Judge
668.1           Gate judge must be so placed that they can safely but properly observe the terrain, gates and course sections for which they are responsible, They should be near enough to be able to take prompt action, but distant enough not to hinder the competitor.

668.2           Organisers are obliged to outfit gate judges so that they are readily identifiable. Identification or clothing should be of a colour that will not be confused with a gate panel.

668.3           Gate judges must be in their location well before the start of the run.Organisers should provide gate judges with protective clothing against adverse weather where necessary and should provide some form of nourishment during the run.

668.4          Any equipment necessary to permit the gate judges to perform their assigned duties should be provided.

669            Number of Gate Judges
669.1           The organiser is responsible for having a sufficient num- ber of competent gate judges available.

669.2           The organiser must inform the Jury of the number of gate



668       旗门裁判员的位置和保障
668.1      旗门裁判员必须配备在安全且能清楚观察到其所负 责的区域的地形、旗门和旗门组的地方。这个地方 要距离赛道足够近以便于其迅速采取行动 ；同时还 应有一定距离，不致妨碍运动员滑行。


668.2      组织方必须为旗门裁判员提供全套服装，使其很容 易识别。识别标志和服装的颜色不能与旗门的颜色 相混淆。

668.3      旗门裁判员必须在比赛开始前各就各位。组织方应 该为旗门裁判员提供抵御不利天气的防护服装，并 且在比赛期间应该为他们提供一定种类的营养品。



668.4      应提供便于旗门裁判员履行其职责所需的任何设备。


669       旗门裁判员的人数
669.1      组织方有责任提供人数足够且称职的旗门裁判员。


669.2      组织方必须告知仲裁委员会，在训练时尤其在 比赛

judges available for training and particularly for the race.

669.3          At Olympic Winter Games, FIS World Ski Champion- ships and FIS World Cup competitions, the number of gate judges will be determined by the Jury.

670            Video control
When the organiser has the equipment for official video control, the Jury will appoint an official video control- ler. The duties of the video controller are to observe the competitors’passage through the course.

680           Poles
All poles used in alpine events are described as slalom poles and are either rigid poles or ﬂex-poles.

680.1          Rigid Poles
Must be round, uniform poles without a bending device and should be of the same material and dimensions as the flex pole. Rigid poles may be used for the outside gate or pole and in exceptional cases (e.g. high wind) as the outside pole of the turning gate (see art 680.2.1.2).

680.2           Flex poles
Flex poles are fitted with a bending device. They must conform to the FIS specifications.

680.2.1             Use of Flex-poles
Flex-poles must be used for all alpine competitions

时能提供多少旗门裁判员。

669.3      在冬季奥林匹克运动会、国际雪联世界锦标赛和国 际雪联世界杯中，旗门裁判员的数量由仲裁委员会 决定。
670       视频监控
组织方备有设备进行官方视频监控的，仲裁委员会 将任命 1 名正式的视频监控员，其职责是在比赛过 程中观察运动员通过赛道的情况。


680       旗门杆
所有用于高山滑雪比赛的旗门杆都称为回转旗门 杆，分为硬直杆和弹力杆两种。
680.1       硬直杆
必须是圆的、样式统一、无弹簧铰链等弯曲装置的  杆，应与弹力杆材料和直径相同。硬直杆可用于外  侧旗门或者外侧杆，在例外的情形下（如大风）可  用做转弯旗门的外侧杆（参见本规则第 680.2.1.2条）


680.2       弹力杆
弹力杆配有弹簧铰链等弯曲装置，必须符合国际雪 联的具体规定。
680.2.1      弹力杆的使用
除滑降比赛外，其他所有已纳入《国际雪联竞赛日

published in the FIS Calendar except Downhill. The use of ﬂex poles may be requested by the Jury for Downhill.

680.2.1.1     Slalom
Slalom poles must be coloured red or blue. The turning pole must be a ﬂex-pole.

680.2.1.2     Giant Slalom and Super-G
In Giant Slalom and Super-G two pairs of slalom poles are used, each pair carrying a gate panel between them. The gate panels should be fixed or tied so they should tear or break away from one pole. The turning pole(s) must be ﬂex-pole(s).

680.2.2             FIS Specifications for Flex Poles
All further details in regard to construction and function- ing of the ﬂex poles are regulated in the valid FIS Speci- fications for ﬂex poles.

690           Gate  Panels for Giant Slalom Su-
per-G and Downhill
Gate panels which conform to the FIS Specifications must be used for all Giant Slalom, Super-G and Down- hill competitions published in the FIS Calendar. A list of homologated panels is published on the FIS Website. Arts. 701.3.2, 901.2.2 and 1001.3.2 remain valid.

680.2.1.1     回转赛
回转旗门杆必须为红色或蓝色，绕行杆必须是弹 力杆。
680.2.1.2      大回转和超级大回转
在大回转和超级大回转赛中，应使用两对回转旗门  杆，每对旗门杆各挂一面旗门布。旗门布应固定、 系好，且能从旗门杆上撕裂或脱解下来。绕行杆必  须采用弹力杆。


680.2.2              国际雪联对弹力杆的具体规定
有关弹力杆结构和功能的更多全面细节信息，请参 见现行有效的国际雪联规范弹力杆的具体规定。


690       大回转、超级大回转和滑降的旗门布
符合国际雪联具体规定的旗门布必须用于所有《国 际雪联竞赛日历》公布的大回转、超级大回转和 滑降比赛项目。经认证的旗门布列表公布在国际雪 联官网上。本规则第 701.3.2 和、第 901.2.2 条和第 1001.3.2 条仍然有效。






THE INTERNATIONAL SKI
COMPETITION RULES (ICR)

2nd Section   Rules Common to Alpine Events 第二部分    高山滑雪竞赛通则






690.1          Release in case of collision

Gate panels should release from the pole when a competitor gets caught by it. The gate panel must meet the test re- quirements for this as defined in the specifications for Gate Panel Homologation.

690.2          No removal during normal collision with
the pole
During normal collisions, the gate panel should not re- lease from the pole.The gate panel must meet the test re- quirements for this defined in the specifications for Gate Panel Homologation.

690.3          Wind permeability
The panel must be made of wind-permeable material.

690.4          Advertising on Panels
Advertising on panels should not reduce wind permea- bility and the release mechanism of the panels.

695           Colours
For Major Events (art. 201.3. 1) and Cups (art. 201.3.2 and 201.3.3) different alternative colours for poles and panels may be used. Orange can be used instead of red at all FIS levels. Poles and panels should be the same colour.

690.1           万一旗门布发生绞缠，应能从旗杆上顺利脱 解下来
运动员被旗门布缠住时，旗门布应能从旗杆上顺利脱 解。旗门布必须达到旗门布认证的具体规定中就此提 出的检测要求。


690.2       旗门布在正常撞击旗杆时不致脱解
运动员正常撞击旗杆时，旗门布不应从旗杆上脱解下 来。旗门布必须达到旗门布认证具体规定中就此提出 的检测要求。



690.3       透风性
旗门布制作材料必须透风性能好。
690.4       旗门布上的广告
旗门布上的广告不应减弱其透风性，亦不得妨碍旗门 布的脱解。
695        颜色
重大比赛（本规则第 201.3.1 条）和杯赛（本规则第 201.3.2 和 201.3.3 条）的旗门杆和旗门布可交替使用 不同颜色。国际雪联所有级别赛事都可以用橙色代替 红色。旗门杆和旗门布应采用相同颜色。

- 450 米至 1100 米（U21 至 U18，700 米） 两轮滑行比赛 ：
- 350 米至 450 米

701.1.2       女子比赛线路 所有比赛 ：
- 450 米至 800 米（U21 至 U18，700 米） 两轮滑行比赛 ：
- 350 米至 450 米

701.1.3      入门级别比赛 (ENL) 女子和男子 ：
一轮滑行比赛 ：
- 400 米至 500 米 两轮滑行比赛 ：
- 300 米至 400 米

COMPETITION RULES (ICR)

3rd Section   Particular Rules for the different Events 第三部分   各比赛项目的特殊规则






The competition course must be homologated for Down- hill with the start and finish positions for ENL indicated.

701.2           Course Length
The course length has to be measured by a measuring tape, wheel or GPS and printed on the start and the re- sults list.

701.3           Gates

701.3.1             A Downhill gate consists of 4 slalom poles and 2 gate panels.

701.3.1.1     Courses are marked with red or blue gates (see art. 701.3.2).
701.3.1.2     If men and women use the same competition course, the additional gates for women must be blue.

701.3.2             For gate panels, rectangular panels are to be used, ap- proximately 0.75 m wide by 0.50 m high. They are to be fastened on the poles, so that they can be recognised as easily as possible by the competitors. In place of red a luminous orange colour may be used. If the safety net- ting is the same colour as the gate panels (usually red or blue), and where the gates cannot be seen properly against the backdrop of the safety netting, an alternative colour for the gate panels (usually blue or red) may be used on those gates.

滑降项目比赛的赛道必须经过认证，并标明入门级 别比赛起点和终点的位置。
701.2       比赛线路长度
比赛线路长度应采用测量尺、轮尺、GPS 等工具测量， 并打印在出发顺序表和成绩列表中。


701.3       旗门
701.3.1             滑降比赛旗门由 4 根回转杆和 2 面旗门布组成。


701.3.1.1      比赛线路用红色或蓝色旗门标明 （参见本规则第
701.3.2 条）。

701.3.1.2     如果男女使用同一条比赛线路，则女子比赛额外的 旗门布必须采用蓝色。
701.3.2             应采用长方形旗门布，宽约 0.75 米、高约 0.50 米。 旗门布应系在旗门杆上，要尽可能便于运动员辨认。 可使用亮橙色代替红色。在赛事中，如果安全网的  颜色与旗门布的颜色（通常为蓝色或红色） 一致。 同色安全网背景下不易区分旗门时，应采用对比颜 色（通常为蓝色或红色）的旗门布。






THE INTERNATIONAL SKI
COMPETITION RULES (ICR)

3rd Section   Particular Rules for the different Events 第三部分   各比赛项目的特殊规则






701.3.3              The width of the gates must be at least 8m.

702            The Courses

702.1          Joint Regulations for Downhill Courses
Downhill courses for Olympic Winter Games, FIS World Ski Championships, and the FIS World Cup must be specifically inspected, in order that they not only comply with the technical requirements, but are also technically demanding.

702.2          General Characteristics of the Courses
A Downhill is characterised by the six components of technique, courage, speed, risk, physical condition and judgement. It must be possible to ski the Downhill course from the start to the finish with different speeds. Athletes adapt speed and performance to their ski techni- cal skills and individual self-responsible judgement.

702.3         Particular Regulations for the Course
Layout
Courses should normally be approx. 30 m wide. The inspector assigned for competition course homologation decides whether this width is sufficient and if necessary, may order widening. The inspector can also permit a width of less than 30 m depending on the line and terrain requirements, as long as the areas of the competition course before and after the narrow part permit this. Fall zones should be planned, where necessary, on the

701.3.3       旗门宽度必须至少 8 米。
702       比赛线路
702.1            滑降比赛线路通则
对冬季奥林匹克运动会、国际雪联世界锦标赛和国  际雪联世界杯的滑降比赛线路必须进行专门视察， 确保比赛线路既符合一般技术要求，又满足技术上 的更高标准。


702.2        比赛线路的一般特征
滑降比赛的特征体现在 6 个方面，即技术、勇气、 速度、冒险、身体状况和判断力。比赛线路必须满  足运动员以不同的速度从起点滑到终点的要求。运  动员根据自己的滑行技术水平和对自我能力负责的 判断来调整滑行速度和动作。


702.3       赛道布置的详细规定

赛道应通常为 30 米宽。受指派负责赛道认证的认证 官有权决定这一宽度是否足够，在其认为必要时可 要求加宽。根据赛道线型和地形的需要，只要赛道 狭窄段前后的区域允许，认证官也可以允许宽度不 足 30 米。必要时应在转弯外侧设置缓冲区。尤其应 在接近赛道的边缘处、下落处和跳跃处做一些能够 协助控制速度的设计。






THE INTERNATIONAL SKI
COMPETITION RULES (ICR)

3rd Section   Particular Rules for the different Events 第三部分   各比赛项目的特殊规则






outside of curves. Possibilities to control speed should be made specifically for the approach to lips, drop- offs and jumps.
Not all parts of the course need necessarily to be skied at full speed. Surfaces may be left in their natural state.
Obstacles against which competitors may be thrown if leaving the competition course should be as well protect- ed as possible with high safety nets, safety fences, pads or similar means if necessary, together with slip-sheets.    The function of safety installations must withstand weather conditions typical for alpine skiing.

702.4           Means of Transport
Access to the start must be provided by lifts or shuttle service.

703            Course Setting

703.1           Setting of the Gates

703.1.1             Gates must be set to delineate the desired racing line.

703.1.2             Before difficult jumps and difficult passages the speed should be controlled by appropriate course setting where possible.

703.1.3             At places where the outside gate must be removed, in exceptional cases decided by the Jury, the turning gate serves as a gate. (see art. 904.3)




并非比赛线路的所有部分都要全速滑行。赛道表面 可以保持自然状态。
对于运动员滑出赛道后有可能撞到的障碍物，应该 采用高安全网、安全护栏、垫子或其他类似手段尽 可能加强隔离防护。如有必要，还应安设防摔网。
安全装置必须经受得住典型的高山滑雪天气状况而 不致影响其防护功能。
702.4       交通方式
必须提供通达起点处的缆车或班车。


703       旗门设计
703.1       旗门的设计
703.1.1      设计的旗门要反映出预想的比赛路线。

703.1.2      在有难度的跳跃坡前和有难度的旗门绕行前，应尽 可能通过适当的旗门设计来控制速度。


703.1.3      如遇仲裁委员会决定必须去掉外侧旗门杆的特殊情 况，绕行杆将成为旗门（参见本规则第 904.3 条）。

COMPETITION RULES (ICR)

3rd Section   Particular Rules for the different Events 第三部分   各比赛项目的特殊规则






703.2          Preparation and Inspection of the Course

703.2.1             For all Downhill competitions listed in the FIS Calendar, the competition course should be completely prepared and race-ready before the first Jury inspection. It should be available with all of the installations as set out in the technical advisor’s or homologation report, or as deter- mined between the organiser and the Technical Delegate (for Olympic Winter Games, FIS World Championships and World Cup Referee or Assistant Referee) prior to the arrival of the teams.
703.2.2             Before the start of the training on the first official train- ing day, there must be an inspection by the Jury with the technical advisor, if present and generally also in the presence of the team captains or trainers.

703.2.3             Before the start of the first official training the competi- tors should conduct a complete inspection of the course.

703.2.4             The members of the Jury must be available to receive re- quests and suggestions regarding the course, training etc. from the competitors and trainers.

704            Official Training
Special regulations may be issued for Downhill training for the Olympic Winter Games, FIS World Ski Champi- onships, FIS World Cup and FIS Continental Cup.

703.2       比赛线路的准备和视察
703.2.1           《国际雪联竞赛日历》中所有滑降比赛的线路，必须 在仲裁委员会第一次视察时完全准备完毕并可用于 比赛。技术顾问或认证报告中所列的所有装置均应 做到随时可用，或按照组委会和技术代表（冬季奥 林匹克运动会、国际雪联世界锦标赛和世界杯裁判 长或助理裁判长）在参赛队伍到达前的决定备妥。




703.2.2             在第一个场地适应训练日开始训练之前，仲裁委员 会必须会同技术顾问（如果在赛事现场）视察一次 线路，视察时领队或教练通常也应在场。


703.2.3             场地适应训练开始前，运动员应对线路进行完整的 视察。

703.2.4             仲裁委员会成员应随时听取运动员、教练员对赛道、 训练等方面的要求和建议等。


704       场地适应训练
冬季奥林匹克运动会、国际雪联世界锦标赛、国际 雪联世界杯赛和国际雪联洲际杯赛的滑降训练可颁 布特别规定。






THE INTERNATIONAL SKI
COMPETITION RULES (ICR)

3rd Section   Particular Rules for the different Events 第三部分   各比赛项目的特殊规则






704.1          Obligation to Participate
Official training forms an integral part of the competi- tion. Competitors are required to participate in the train- ing. All qualified competitors entered for the competition must have been entered and drawn in all official training runs. This is also valid where substitutes are authorised by special rules.

704.2           Duration
Three days should be scheduled for the inspection and official training.

704.2.1             A reduction in the number of training days or at least one training run may be decided on by the Jury.

704.2.2              Official training need not necessarily be on consecutive days.

704.3          Race-ready Preparation
The entire facilities (start, course, and finish area) must be completely prepared and ready for racing by the first official training day.

704.3.1             All crowd control barriers must be completed.

704.4          First Aid and Medical Service
The first aid and medical services must be completely operational during all training. Details of the Medical Support Requirements are given in chapter 1 of the FIS Medical Guide.

704.1       参加的义务
场地适应训练是比赛的组成部分，要求运动员参加 训练。所有有资格参加比赛的运动员都必须抽签并 参加过场地适应训练的各轮滑行。此规则也同样适 用于经特殊规则授权参赛的替补运动员。



704.2            训练时间
应安排 3 天时间用以视察线路和进行场地适应训练。


704.2.1             仲裁委员会可决定缩短训练天数或至少进行 1 轮训 练滑行。

704.2.2             场地适应训练不一定要连续进行数天。
704.3       赛前准备
第一天场地适应训练时，整套设施（起点区、赛道、 终点区）必须完全设置好并做好竞赛准备。


704.3.1             所有用于观众管理的栅栏都必须设置完成。
704.4       急救和医疗服务
在各项训练期间，急救和医疗服务必须全面运行。 有关《医疗保障要求》的详细信息，参见《国际雪  联医疗指南》第一章。






THE INTERNATIONAL SKI
COMPETITION RULES (ICR)

3rd Section   Particular Rules for the different Events 第三部分   各比赛项目的特殊规则






704.5          Priority on the Lift Facilities to the Start
Organisers must arrange for competitors and specifically accredited officials to have assured priority on the lift facilities to the start in order to use the training times without waiting.

704.6           Training Numbers
Competitors must wear training numbers (bibs) for all official training.

704.7           Start Order
The Start Referee, or an official appointed by the Jury, must verify from a start list that the competitors start training in the order of the training start list, and that start intervals are maintained.

704.8          Timed Training

704.8.1             During at least one of the last two training days the times must be taken.
704.8.2             Recorded times must be given to the team captains at latest at the team captains meeting but may also be announced over the loud speaker or published on the scoreboard after each competitor’s run.

704.8.3            A competitor must participate in  at least  one timed training run.

704.5       通往起点区缆车的优先使用权
组织方必须安排运动员和特别注册的官员享有前往 起点的缆车优先使用权，以便他们充分利用训练时 间而无需等待。


704.6       训练号码
运动员参加所有场地适应训练时，必须佩戴训练号 码布。
704.7       出发顺序
起点裁判长或 1 名由仲裁委员会任命的官员根据出 发顺序表检查运动员在训练时是否按顺序出发，以 及出发时是否保持出发间隔。


704.8       计时训练
704.8.1             最后两天的训练中，至少有 1 天必须计时。


704.8.2            记录的时间最迟必须在领队会上交给各领队，但也 可以在运动员每轮滑行后通过扩音器公布，或在记 分板上公布。


704.8.3             运动员必须参加至少一次计时训练。






THE INTERNATIONAL SKI
COMPETITION RULES (ICR)

3rd Section   Particular Rules for the different Events 第三部分   各比赛项目的特殊规则






704.8.4              In case of a fall, or stopping, or being overtaken during a training run, competitors must leave the race line. Con- tinuing the Downhill training run is not permitted. They may, however, move along the edge of the course to the Finish.

704.8.5             In case of atmospheric changes (snowfall etc.) between the last training day and the day of the race, an inspec- tion of the course may be organised for the competitors on the day of the race.

704.8.6             Whenever possible, one training run should take place at the same time as that scheduled for the race.

705            Yellow Flag

705.1           Inspection
The Jury may, define the position of the yellow flags for the training and for the race if required which can be waved to alert the next competitor.The ﬂags must be positioned before the first inspection and should be rec- ognisable by the competitors.

705.2           Training
When competitors are stopped in training by the yellow ﬂag, they have the right to re-start from the point where they have been stopped.
At the request of the stopped competitors, a Jury mem- ber may allow them a re-run if this is possible from the

704.8.4             滑行训练中摔倒、停止或正在被超越的运动员必须 离开赛道，不允许继续进行滑降训练，可以沿赛道 边缘滑向终点。



704.8.5             训练日最后一天至比赛当日出现天气变化（如下雪 等）的，可于比赛当日再安排运动员视察一次赛道。



704.8.6             只要有可能，要安排一轮开滑时间与比赛的秩序册
中预定的开赛时间相同的训练滑行。

705       黄旗
705.1       视察
仲裁委员会可以确定训练和比赛的黄旗位置，需要 时可以挥动以提醒下一位参赛者。旗帜必须在第一 次视察前放置好，应做到为运动员所识别。



705.2       训练
训练中被黄旗拦下的运动员，有权从被拦下的地点 重新开始滑行。

经运动员申请，如果不影响比赛组织，且导致延迟 的原因确实情有可原，仲裁委员会的成员可 以允许





THE INTERNATIONAL SKI
COMPETITION RULES (ICR)


point of view of the organisation and any delay resulting there from. If a re-run is approved it is the responsibility of the competitors to present themselves to the start ref- eree before the last competitor has started, otherwise this approval will be withdrawn.

705.3           Race
When competitors are stopped during the race they have the right to a rerun provided that the Jury considers this possible from an organisational point of view. The Jury should ensure that the competitor’s re-run takes place before the last competitor on the start list of the race.

705.4           Obligation
When competitors are waved down by a yellow ﬂag they must stop immediately.

705.5           Commands
On the command“start stop! ”or“start stop, yellow ﬂag”the Start Referee must close the start and must re- spond immediately via radio confirming that the start is closed, and state the start number of the last competitor to have started as well of the start number of the compet- itor held at the start (“start stop confirmed, number 23 on course, number 24 at the start”).
The Jury member who called the“start stop”is also re- sponsible for requesting yellow ﬂag(s) that are necessary to stop competitor(s) on course.

该运动员重滑。获准重滑的运动员须在最后一名运 动员出发前向起点裁判长报到，否则撤销重滑。




705.3       比赛
运动员比赛期间被拦下，只要仲裁委员会从比赛组 织角度考虑认为可以重滑，运动员有权重滑。但仲 裁委员会应确保该名运动员在出发顺序表上的最后 一名运动员出发前开始重滑。


705.4       义务
黄色旗帜挥动（示意运动员停下来），运动员必须立 即停下来。
705.5       命令
听到“出发停止 !”或“出发停止，黄旗！ ”指令， 起点裁判长必须关闭起点。起点裁判长必须通过对 讲机立即回应且确认出发门关闭，并报告已出发的 最后 1 名运动员的出发号码，以及被拦在起点等待 出发运动员的出发号码（如 ：出发停止确认，第 23 号已上赛道，第 24 号在起点）。
发出“出发停止”指令的仲裁委员会成员还负责在 需要时要求挥黄旗让赛道上的运动员停下来。

COMPETITION RULES (ICR)

3rd Section   Particular Rules for the different Events 第三部分   各比赛项目的特殊规则






706            Execution of the Downhill

706.1           Downhill in One Run
A Downhill will be carried out in one run.

706.2          Downhill in Two Runs

706.2.1             A Downhill in two runs can be organised with the re- quired vertical drop as stated in the ICR.

706.2.2             The result will be determined by the addition of the two run times. The rule“Starting order for the 2nd run”(art.
621. 11) will be used.

706.2.3             All the rules for the Downhill are valid for the race in two runs. The Jury will rule in case of problems caused by the course, the training and the two runs.

706.2.4             The two runs should be run on the same day.

706.2.5             Downhill races carried out in two runs must be identified as such in the FIS Calendar, provided the competition course has a vertical drop according to art. 701.1.

706.2.6             In exceptional cases where carrying out the original Downhill is jeopardized (unfavourable snow or atmo- spheric conditions), the Jury is permitted to conduct the Downhill in two runs.

706       滑降比赛的实施
706.1       一轮滑行的滑降比赛
滑降比赛仅进行 1 轮滑行。

706.2       二轮滑行的滑降比赛
706.2.1             可以按照《国际滑雪竞赛规则》要求的垂直落差来 组织二轮滑行的滑降比赛。

706.2.2             比赛成绩为两次滑行时间之和，适用“第二轮滑行 出发顺序”规则（本规则第 621. 11 条）。


706.2.3             所有关于滑降比赛的规则对二轮滑行的比赛均适用。 因赛道、训练和二轮滑行引发的问题，由仲裁委员  会裁决。

706.2.4             二轮滑行应在同一天进行。

706.2.5             如果进行二轮滑行的滑降线路的垂直落差是按照本 规则第 701. 1 条确定的，则必须在《国际雪联竞赛 日历》中如实标明。

706.2.6             在特殊情况下，如果实施最初预定的滑降比赛有危 险（不利的雪况或者天气条件），允许仲裁委员会分 两轮滑行组织滑降比赛。

COMPETITION RULES (ICR)

3rd Section   Particular Rules for the different Events 第三部分   各比赛项目的特殊规则






707           Crash Helmet
All competitors and forerunners must wear a crash hel- met for official training as well as for the race that meets the FIS Equipment Specifications.
Soft ear protection is only permitted for helmets used in Slalom.

仅在回转比赛中允许使用带软护耳的头盔。

801.1.4             Entry League Races (ENL) Women and Men
- 80 m - 120 m (Men 140) Races in 3 runs:
- minimum 50 m

801.2           Gates
801.2.1             A slalom gate consists of two poles (art. 680) or where there is no outside pole the gate will consist of a turning pole.

801.2.2             Consecutive gates must alternate in blue and red.

801.2.3             A gate must have a minimum width of 4 m and a maxi- mum of 6 m.
The distance from turning pole to turning pole of succes- sive gates must not be less than 6 m and not more than 13 m (valid for all categories).
Exception U 16 - U 14 competitions:
- between 7 m and 11 m
The distance between gates within combinations (hairpin or vertical) must be not less than 0.75 m and not more than 1 m. The gates in hairpin or vertical combinations must be set in a straight line. Delayed gates must have a minimum distance of 12 m and a maximum distance of 18 m (U16- U 14 Competition 15 m) from turning pole to turning pole.

801.2       旗门
801.2.1       1 个回转旗门由 2 根回转旗门杆组成（本规则第 680
条），如果没有外侧旗门杆，则旗门由 1 个绕行杆 组成。
801.2.2       连续的旗门必须交替使用蓝色和红色。

801.2.3       旗门宽度至少 4 米，至多 6 米。

相邻两个旗门内侧杆之间的距离不得小于 6 米，不 得大于 13 米（适用于所有级别比赛）。
U 16-U14 比赛例外 ：
- 7 米到 11 米之间
组合旗门（发卡门或垂直门）间的距离不得小于 0.75 米，同时不得大于 1.00 米。发卡门或垂直门组合旗 门必须设置在一条直线上。延迟旗门从回转杆到回 转杆的间距最小 12 米，最大 18 米（U16-U14 比赛 15 米）。

802            The Courses

802.1          General Characteristics of the Course

802.1.1              At Olympic Winter Games and FIS World Ski Champi- onships the course must be set on slopes with a gradient of approximately 33% to 45%. It may even be below approximately 33%, but may exceed approximately 52% only in very short parts of the course.

802.1.2             The ideal slalom course, taking into consideration the drop and the gradient specified above, must include a series of turns designed to allow the competitors to com- bine speed with neat execution and precision of turns.

802.1.3             The Slalom should permit the rapid completion of all turns. The course should not require acrobatics incompati- ble with normal ski technique. It should be a technically

次数）：

- 垂直落差的 30% 至 35%，+/-3 次方向改变。 U 16-U14 比赛例外 ：
- 32% 至 38%，+/-3 次换向次数。

801.2.4.1     因不规则地形致使换向次数无法满足要求的，以认
证证书显示的准予例外的情形为准。



802       比赛线路
802.1       比赛线路的一般特征
802.1.1             在冬季奥林匹克运动会和国际雪联世界锦标赛上， 比赛线路必须设在坡度约为 33% 至 45% 的雪道上。 雪道坡度可以低于 33%，也可以超过 52%（仅限于  比赛线路中很短的部分）。


802.1.2            考虑到上述落差和坡度限制，理想的回转比赛线路 必须包括一系列转弯，其设置应使运动员将速度与 干净利落的动作和准确的转弯结合起来。


802.1.3             回转比赛中应允许运动员快速地完成所有转弯。其 比赛线路不应要求运动员采用与正常滑行技术不相 适应的特技动作。比赛线路应因地制宜巧妙安排，






THE INTERNATIONAL SKI
COMPETITION RULES (ICR)

3rd Section   Particular Rules for the different Events 第三部分   各比赛项目的特殊规则






clever composition of figures suited to the terrain, linked by single and multiple gates, allowing a ﬂuent run, but testing the widest variety of ski technique, including changes of direction with very different radius. Gates should never be set only down the fall-line, but so that some full turns are required, interspersed with traverses.

802.1.4              Preparation of the Course
Slalom competitions must be raced on a course surface that is as hard as possible. If snow falls during the race, the chief of course must ensure that it is packed or, if possible, removed from the course.

802.2           Width
The competition course should be approximately 40 m wide, if two runs are set on the same slope.

803            Course Setting

803.1           Course Setters

803.1.1              Pre-inspection
This inspection must be carried out by the course setter before the course is set. The Slalom should correspond to the average ability of the first 30 competitors.

803.2          Number of Gate Combinations
A Slalom must contain horizontal (open) and verti- cal (closed) gates as well as a minimum of one and a

由单个或多个旗门相连，保证运动员能流畅滑行， 同时又可以最大限度地检验运动员的滑行技巧，包 括滑行中进行转弯半径不等的变化方向动作。旗门  不应总设计成引导运动员沿滚落线下降，而应设置 一些完整的大弯间以之字型的穿越滚落线。


802.1.4      赛道的准备
回转比赛应在尽可能坚硬的雪面上进行。如在比赛 期间降雪，赛道长要么保证雪被压实，要么尽其所 能清除掉赛道上的降雪。


802.2       宽度
如果两轮滑行都在同一坡道上进行，则赛道至少应 为 40 米宽。
803       旗门设计
803.1       旗门设计员
803.1.1      预视察
预视察必须由旗门设计员在设计比赛线路前进行。 回转比赛线路的难度设置应与前 30 名运动员平均 水平相当。
803.2       组合旗门数量
回转线路必须包括水平横向旗门（开口旗门）和垂 直方向旗门（闭口旗门），至少一组至多三组垂直






THE INTERNATIONAL SKI
COMPETITION RULES (ICR)

3rd Section   Particular Rules for the different Events 第三部分   各比赛项目的特殊规则






maximum of three vertical combinations consisting of three to four gates and at least three hairpin-combina- tions consisting of two gates. It must also contain a min- imum of one and a maximum of three delay gate combi- nations.

803.2.1              U14 – U16
- U 14: minimum 2 and maximum 4 hairpin combinations and minimum 1 and maximum 2 vertical combination consisting of maximum 3 gates.
- U 16: minimum 3 and maximum 6 hairpin combinations and minimum 1 and maximum 3 vertical combinations consisting of 3 - maximum 4 gates.
- It must also contain a minimum of one and a maximum of three delayed turns。
The course should have no special technical difficulties. Flex-poles must be light poles (25 - 28.9 mm).

803.3           Gates and Combinations of Gates
The most important types of gates and combinations of gates are:
horizontal (open) gates, vertical (closed) gates, vertical combinations, and hairpin combinations and delayed gates combinations.

803.4           Setting
In setting Slalom the following principles should be ob- served:

旗门组合（每组中包括三到四个旗门），以及至少 三组由两个旗门构成的螺旋门。回转线路同时必须 包含至少一组至多三组蛇形门组合旗门。



803.2.1             U14 - U16
- U14 ：至少 2 组至多 4 组发卡门，至少 1 组至多 2 组垂直旗门组合，每组包括至多 3 个旗门。

- U16 ：至少 3 组至多 6 组发卡门，至少 1 组至多 3 组垂直旗门组合，每组包括 3 个至多 4 个旗门。

- 还必须包括至少 1 组至多 3 组蛇形转弯。 线路不应有特殊的技术难度。

弹力杆必须为轻质杆（25 至 28.9 毫米）。

803.3       旗门和旗门组合
最重要的旗门类型和旗门组合类型有 ：

水平横向旗门（开口旗门）、垂直竖向旗门（闭口旗  门）、垂直旗门组合、螺旋门组合以及蛇形旗门组合。


803.4       设计
设计回转线路时应遵循以下原则 ：






THE INTERNATIONAL SKI
COMPETITION RULES (ICR)

3rd Section   Particular Rules for the different Events 第三部分   各比赛项目的特殊规则






803.4.1             Avoidance of monotonous series of standardised combi- nations of gates.

803.4.2              Gates, which impose too sudden sharp braking on com- petitors, should be avoided, as they spoil the ﬂuency of the run without increasing the difficulties a modern Sla- lom should have.
803.4.3             It is advisable before difficult combinations of gates to set at least one gate which allows the competitor to ski through the difficult combination under control.

803.4.4             It is not advisable to set difficult gate passages either right at the beginning or end of the course. The last gates should be rather fast, so that the competitor passes the finish at a good speed.

803.4.5             Where possible the last gate should not be too close to the finish. It should direct competitors towards the middle part of the finish. If the width of the slope neces- sitates it, the last gate can be common to both courses, provided the prescribed alternation of blue and red gates is maintained.
803.4.6             The slalom poles should be fixed (screwed in) by the chief of course or the assistants immediately after they have been set, so that the course setter can supervise the operation.

803.4.1             避免单调不变地将一系列标准化旗门组合在一起。


803.4.2              避免设计迫使运动员必须突然急停的旗门，这会破 坏滑行流畅性且不能增加回转赛应有的难度。



803.4.3             建议在有难度的旗门组合前至少应设置一个旗门， 以使运动员在良好控制下滑过这一有难度的旗门 组合。

803.4.4             不建议在非常靠近起点和终点处设计有难度的旗门。 最后一个旗门应以能使运动员相当快速地通过终点 为宜。


803.4.5             在可能的情况下，最后一个旗门不应离终点太近， 该旗门应引导运动员滑向终点线的中间部分。若坡 道宽度有此需求，最后一道旗门可以为两条线路共 享，只要旗门颜色遵循红蓝交替即可。



803.4.6             赛道上的各旗门设计完成后，赛道长或其助手应立 即把回转旗门杆固定（拧入）到位，以便旗门设计 员能够监督操作过程。

COMPETITION RULES (ICR)

3rd Section   Particular Rules for the different Events 第三部分   各比赛项目的特殊规则






803.5           Checking the Slalom Course
The Jury must check that the course is ready for racing once the course setter has set it, paying special attention that:
- The slalom poles are firmly fixed (screwed in).
- The gates are in the right colour order.
- If necessary the position of the poles is marked.
- The numbers are in the right order on the outside poles.
- The poles are high enough above the snow.
- The two slalom courses are far enough from each other to avoid misleading the competitors.
- The reserve poles are correctly placed not to mislead the competitors.
- Start and finish are in accordance with art. 613 and 615.

804            Single Pole Slalom
All rules of the ICR are valid, except as follows:


804.1           Single Pole Slalom is permitted in all International FIS Competitions.

804.2           A Single Pole Slalom has no outside pole except the first and the last gate, a delayed gate and combinations (hair- pin, vertical).

804.3           Where there is no outside pole, both feet and ski tips must have passed the turning pole on the same side, fol- lowing the normal race line of the slalom crossing the

803.5       回转比赛线路的检查
旗门设计员设计好比赛线路后仲裁委员会须立即检 查，以确定线路是否可以进行比赛，检查时尤其应 注意 ：
- 回转旗门杆牢固地固定（拧紧）。
- 旗门颜色顺序正确。
- 如有必要，标出旗门杆的位置。
- 外侧旗门杆的号码顺序正确。
- 旗门杆在雪面上方的高度足够。
- 两条回转比赛线路之间保持足够远的距离，以免误 导运动员。
- 备用旗门杆放置正确，不致误导运动员。

- 起点终点符合本规则第 613 条和第 615 条。

804       单杆回转比赛
除下述内容外，《国际雪联滑雪竞赛规则》的所有条 款均有效 ：
804.1      国际雪联所有国际比赛都允许单杆回转比赛。


804.2      除第一道和最后一道旗门，以及蛇形旗门和旗门组 合（螺旋旗门、垂直旗门）外，单杆回转比赛不设 外侧旗门杆。

804.3      在没有外侧旗门杆的情况下，双脚和滑雪板前端必 须从同侧通过绕行杆，沿着正常回转赛道穿过绕行 杆之间的假想线。如果运动员有一只滑雪板脱落，

If com- petitors have not correctly crossed the imaginary line from turning pole to turning pole and does not follow the normal race line, they have to climb back up and pass around the missed turning pole.

805            The Start

805.1          Start Intervals
The start takes place at irregular intervals in Slalom. The chief of timing and calculations or assistant tells the starter when each competitor should start, in agreement with the Jury. The competitor on the course need not have passed the finish line before the next competitor starts.

805.2           Starting Order

805.2.1              In the first run in sequence of the start numbers.

805.2.2              For the second run see art. 621.11

805.3           Start Signal
As soon as the order for the next start is received, the

805       出发
805.1       出发间隔
在回转比赛中，出发间隔是不固定的。经商仲裁委 员会，计时计算长或其助理通知发令员各运动员应 出发的时间。下一位选手出发前，赛道上的运动员 不一定必已越过终点线。


805.2       出发顺序
805.2.1             第一轮滑行的出发顺序应按出发号码顺序出发。

805.2.2             第二轮滑行参见本规则第 621. 11 条。
805.3       出发信号
发令员接到准予下一个运动员出发命令后将提醒运

starter gives the competitor the warning“Ready”,“At- tention”,“Achtung”and a few seconds later the start signal“Go! Partez! Los! ”. The competitor must start within about 10 seconds after this order.
805.3.1             A competitor must appear, at latest one minute, after being called by the official. Early start times caused by the non-arrival of preceding competitors have to be tak- en into account. The start referee may however, permit a delay which, in the start referee’s opinion is due to “force majeure”. In doubtful cases, the start referee’s may allow the competitor a provisional start, inserted in the normal starting order. The start referee will make the necessary decisions.

805.4          Valid Start and False Start
Competitors must start according to art. 805.3, otherwise they will be disqualified.

806            Execution of the Slalom

806.1           Two runs
A Slalom must always be decided by two runs on two different courses.
Both courses must be used one after the other in the or- der decided by the Jury. Division of the competitors into two groups starting simultaneously on both courses is not permitted. Whenever possible, both runs should be held on the same day.

动员“预备”，几秒钟后，再发出出发信号“出发！” 运动员必须在这个信号发出后 10 秒内出发。



805.3.1             运动员在比赛官员点名后至少 1 分钟内必须出现。 必须考虑因前面运动员未到达而导致的提前出发时 间。不过，起点裁判长根据自己的判断可以“不可 抗力”为由，准予某次延误。如有疑问，可以允许 运动员临时出发，插入正常的出发顺序。起点裁判  长将作出必要的决定。




805.4       有效出发和错误出发
各运动员均应按照本规则第 805.3 条之规定出发， 否则将被取消资格。
806       回转比赛的实施
806.1       两轮滑行
回转比赛必须由在两条不同线路上进行的两轮滑行 来决定成绩。
两条线路必须按照仲裁委员会决定的顺序依次使用。 不允许将运动员分成两组同时在两条线路上开始比 赛。只要可能，两轮滑行应安排在同一天。






THE INTERNATIONAL SKI
COMPETITION RULES (ICR)

3rd Section   Particular Rules for the different Events 第三部分   各比赛项目的特殊规则





806.2
Limitations in the Second Run
The Jury has the right to reduce the number of compet- itors for the second run to half on the first run start list. The decision has to be made no later than one hour be- fore the start of the first run.
806.2
第二轮滑行的限制
仲裁委员会有权将参加第二轮滑行的运动员人数减 少到第一轮滑行出发顺序表的一半。该决定必须在 第一轮滑行开始一小时前作出。
806.3
Video and Film Control
At Olympic Winter Games, FIS World Ski Champion- ships, FIS World Cup and FIS European Cup the Organ- ising Committee must arrange for recordings on video, so that the whole Slalom can be recorded.
At the other FIS Calendar races, a video or film control is recommended.
806.3
录像与影片监控
在冬季奥林匹克运动会、国际雪联世界锦标赛、国 际雪联世界杯和国际雪联欧洲杯中，组委会必须安 排录像，以便记录整个回转比赛的过程。
《国际雪联竞赛日历》中的其他比赛建议采用录像或 影片监控。
807
Crash Helmet
All competitors and forerunners must wear a crash hel- met for official training as well as for the race that meets the FIS Equipment Specifications.
Soft ear protection is only permitted for helmets used in Slalom.
807
防护头盔
所有运动员和试滑员在场地适应训练和比赛时必 须穿戴符合《国际雪联竞赛器材具体规定》的防 护头盔。
仅在回转比赛中允许使用带软护耳的头盔。

901.1.5             Entry League Races (ENL) Women and Men
- 200 m - 250 m

901.2           The Gates

901.2.1             A giant slalom gate consists of 4 slalom poles (art.
680.2.1.2) and 2 gate panels.

901.2.2             The gates must be alternately red and blue. The gate panels are to be approx. 75 cm wide and approx. 50 cm high. They are fastened between the poles so that the lower edge of the panel is approx. 1 m above the snow and should be capable of tearing or breaking away from the pole (see also art. 690).
901.2.3             The gates must be at least 4 m and at most 8 m wide. The distance between the nearest turning poles of two

901.1.2       女子比赛线路
- 250 米 - 400 米

901.1.3      冬季奥林匹克运动会、国际雪联世界锦标赛和国际 雪联世界杯赛中，最小垂直落差为 300 米（男子和 女子）。

901.1.4      U16-U14 比赛线路
- 200 米 - 350 米
U16 的大回转比赛必须采用两轮滑行。U14 的大回 转比赛，组织者可以选择采用一轮或者两轮滑行。
901.1.5      入门级比赛（ENL）女子和男子
- 200 m - 250 m
901.2       旗门
901.2.1      大回转旗门由 4 根回转杆（参见本规则第 680.2.1.2 条）和 2 面旗门布组成。

901.2.2       旗门必须红色、蓝色交替。旗门布宽约 75 厘米，高 约 50 厘米。旗门布应系在两旗门杆之间，其底边距 离雪面 1 米左右，旗门布应可从旗杆上撕脱或拉下 （见本规则第 690 条）。



901.2.3      旗门宽度必须至少 4 米，至多 8 米。相邻两旗门绕 行杆的最小距离不得少于 10米。在U16-U14 比赛中，






THE INTERNATIONAL SKI
COMPETITION RULES (ICR)

3rd Section   Particular Rules for the different Events 第三部分   各比赛项目的特殊规则






successive gates must not be less than 10 m. In U 16 - U 14 competition the distance between turning pole and turning pole must be not more than 27 m.

901.2.4             The Giant  Slalom has to be set as follows (number of direction changes by rounding up or down of the deci- mals):
- 11% - 15% of the vertical drop in meters
- U 16 - U 14: 13% - 18% of the vertical drop
- Entry League (ENL): 13% - 15% of the vertical drop

902            The Courses

902.1          General Characteristics of the Courses
The terrain should preferably be undulating and hilly. The competition course should normally have a width of approximately 40m.
The inspector authorised to homologate the competition course decides whether this width is adequate and if nec- essary can order it to be widened. The inspector can also permit a width of less than approximately 40 m depending on the line and terrain requirements, as long as the areas of the course before and after the narrow part enable this.

902.2           Preparation of the Course
The competition course must be prepared as for the Downhill race. The parts of the course where gates are set and where competitors have to turn must be prepared as for a Slalom.

绕行杆和绕行杆之间的距离不得超过 27 米。



901.2.4             大回转旗门应按以下数据设置（经四舍五入调整后 的换向次数）：

- 垂直落差的 11%-15%（单位 ：米）；
- U 16 - U14 ：垂直落差的 13%-18% ；
- 入门级别（ENL）：垂直落差的 13%-15%。
902       比赛线路
902.1       比赛线路的一般特征
地形以起伏的丘陵地带为佳。赛道宽度一般应在 40 米左右。
经授权认证赛道的认证官可以决定上述宽度是否足 够，如有必要，可命令加宽。根据赛道线形和地形 的需要，只要赛道狭窄段前后的区域允许，认证官 也可以允许宽度不足 40 米。



902.2       比赛线路的准备
比赛线路必须比照滑降比赛线路做好准备。比赛线 路中设置旗门的部分及运动员须转弯处必须比照回 转比赛准备。






THE INTERNATIONAL SKI
COMPETITION RULES (ICR)

3rd Section   Particular Rules for the different Events 第三部分   各比赛项目的特殊规则






903            Course Setting

903.1           Setting
In setting a Giant Slalom the following principles should be observed:
903.1.1             The first run should be set the day before the race. Both runs can be set on the same course but the second run must be re-set.
903.1.2              The skilful use of the ground when setting a Giant Slalom is, in most cases, even more important than for a Slalom, since combinations play a less important role owing to the prescribed width of the gates and the greater distances be- tween them. It is therefore better to set mainly single gates, while exploiting the ground to the utmost. Combinations can be set, but mainly on uninteresting terrain.

903.1.3             A Giant Slalom consists of a variety of long, medium and short turns.Competitor should be free to choose their own line between the gates.
The full width of a hill should be used wherever possi- ble. At places where the outside gate must be removed in exceptional cases decided by the Jury the turning gate serves as a gate.

903.1.4             The course setter in setting the course for youth should take particular consideration of the physical ability ofthe competitors.

903       旗门设计
903.1       设计
设计大回转线路应遵循以下原则 ：


903.1.1       第一轮滑行的线路应在比赛前一天设计好。两轮滑 行可设在同一条赛道上，但第二轮滑行线路必须重 新设计。

903.1.2       在大多数情况下，设计大回转线路时，巧妙利用地 面特点比设计回转线路更为重要，因为旗门的宽度 和旗门之间的距离较大，组合旗门也就显得不太重 要。因此，最好主要设计单个旗门并最大限度地利 用场地。可以设置旗门组合但主要在平坦的地形上 设计。



903.1.3             大回转比赛线路由各种大、中、小转弯组成。在旗
门间运动员可自由选择自己的路线。

应尽可能利用整座山坡的宽度。在由仲裁委员会决 定的特殊情况下，在必须移除外侧旗门的地方由绕 行门来充当旗门。


903.1.4             旗门设计员在设计青少年比赛的赛道时，应特别考 虑到运动员的体能状况。






THE INTERNATIONAL SKI
COMPETITION RULES (ICR)

3rd Section   Particular Rules for the different Events 第三部分   各比赛项目的特殊规则






904           Single Gate Giant Slalom
All rules of the ICR are valid, except as follows:


904.1           Single Gate Giant Slalom is permitted only in Interna- tional FIS level Competitions (see art. 201.3.4, 201.3.5 and 201.3.6).

904.2           A Single Gate Giant Slalom has no outside gate, except for the first and the last gate and delayed gates.

904.3           Where there is no outside gate, both feet and ski tips must have passed the turning pole of the turning gate on the same side, following the normal race line of the Giant Slalom crossing the imaginary line from turning pole to turning pole. If a competitor loses a ski, without committing a fault, e.g. not by straddling a pole, then the tip of the remaining ski and both feet must meet both re- quirements. Where there is an outside gate (first and last gate, delayed gate) art. 661.4.1. is valid.

904.4          All rules and regulations dealing with the width of the course should be considered, as if there is an imaginary outside gate.

905            The Start
905.1           In the first run according to the start numbers (art . 621.3 and 622).

904       单门大回转比赛
除下述内容外，《国际雪联滑雪竞赛规则》的所有其 他条款均有效 ：
904.1      仅允许在国际雪联级别的国际比赛中设置单门
大回转比赛（详见本规则第 201.3.4、201.3.5 和 201.3.6 条）。
904.2      除第一个、最后一个和蛇形旗门外，单门大回转线 路不设外侧旗门。

904.3      在没有外侧旗门的旗门，双脚和滑雪板尖端必须从  同一侧通过回转门的绕行杆，沿着正常大回转赛道  穿过绕行杆之间的假想线。如果运动员一只滑雪板  脱落但没有犯规（如没有骑跨旗门杆），余下那只滑  雪板的尖端和双脚必须同时满足这两项要求。在有  外侧旗门的旗门（第一个和最后一个旗门、延迟旗门） 适用本规则第 661.4. 1 条。



904.4      所有涉及赛道宽度的规则和规定都应考虑，就好像 有一道假想的外侧旗门一样。


905       出发
905.1      第一轮滑行按照出发号码（本规则第 621.3 和第 622 条）出发。

906
Execution of the Giant Slalom
906
大回转比赛的实施
906.1
A Giant Slalom must always be decided by two runs (women and men).
The second run may be held on the same course, but the gates must be reset. Whenever possible, both runs should be held on the same day.
906.1
大回转比赛的成绩必须由两轮滑行决定（男子女子）。 第二轮滑行可在同一场地进行，但旗门必须重新设 计。只要可能，两轮滑行均安排在同一天。
906.2
Limitations in the Second Run
The Jury has the right to reduce the number of compet- itors for the second run to half on the first run start list. The decision has to be made no later than one hour be- fore the start of the first run.
906.2
第二轮滑行的限制
仲裁委员会有权将第二轮滑行的运动员人数减少到 第一轮滑行出发顺序表的一半。该决定必须在第一 轮滑行开始一小时前作出。
906.3
Video Control
Art. 806.3 is applied, if possible, also for Giant Slalom.
906.3
视频监控
如果可能，本规则第806.3条同样适用于大回转比赛。
907
Crash Helmet
All competitors and forerunners must wear a crash hel- met for official training as well as for the race that meets the FIS Equipment Specifications.
Soft ear protection is only permitted for helmets used in Slalom.
907
防护头盔
所有运动员和试滑员在场地适应训练和比赛时必 须穿戴符合《国际雪联竞赛器材具体规定》的防 护头盔。
仅在回转比赛中允许使用带软护耳的头盔。

1001          Technical Data

1001.1         Vertical Drop

1001.1.1           Men’s Courses
For Olympic Winter Games, FIS World Ski Champion- ships, FIS World Cups and Continental Cups:
- 400 m - 650 m
For all other FIS competitions:
- 350m – 650m

1001.1.2           Women’s Courses
For Olympic Winter Games, FIS World Ski Champion- ships and FIS World Cups:
- 400 m - 600 m
For all other FIS competitions:
- 350 m - 600 m

1001.1.3           U16 - U14 Courses
- 250 m - 450 m
1001.1.4 Entry League Races (ENL)
- 300 m - 500 m

1001.2         Course Length
The length of the course must be measured with either a measuring tape, a wheel or GPS and has to be published on the start list and the results.

1001      技术数据
1001.1     垂直落差
1001.1.1     男子比赛线路
冬季奥林匹克运动会、国际雪联世界锦标赛、国际 雪联世界杯和洲际杯赛 ：
- 400 米 - 650 米
国际雪联其他所有比赛 ：
- 350 米 - 650 米

1001.1.2      女子比赛线路
冬季奥林匹克运动会、国际雪联世界锦标赛和国际 雪联世界杯赛 ：
- 400 米 - 600 米
国际雪联其他所有比赛 ：
- 350 米 - 600 米

1001.1.3      U16-U14 赛道
- 250 米 - 450 米
1001.1.4 入门级比赛（ENL ）
- 350 米 - 500 米

1001.2      比赛线路长度
比赛线路长度应由测量尺、轮尺或 GPS 等工具测量 并公布在出发顺序表和成绩列表上。

COMPETITION RULES (ICR)

3rd Section   Particular Rules for the different Events 第三部分   各比赛项目的特殊规则






1001.3         Gates

1001.3.1          A Super-G  gate  consists of four slalom poles (art.
680.2.1.2) and two gate panels.

1001.3.2           The gates must be alternately red and blue. The gate panels are to be approx. 75cm wide and approx. 50cm high. They are fastened between the poles so that the lower edge of the panel is approx. 1m above the snow and should be capable of tearing or breaking away (art. 690).
1001.3.3            The gates must be at least 6 m and at most 8 m wide for open gates and at least 8 m and at most 12 m for vertical gates.

1001.3.4           The Super-G must be set as follows(number of direction changes by rounding up or down of the decimals):
For FIS level events 7% of the vertical drop equals the minimum number of direction changes. For Olympic Winter Games, FIS World Ski Championships, FIS World Junior Championships and Continental Cup level events 6% of the vertical drop equals the minimum num- ber of direction changes.
The distance between the turning poles of two successive gates must be at least 25 m (exception: art. 1003.1. 1).
U 16 - U 14 competitions: minimum 8%, maximum 12% direction changes of the vertical drop.
Entry League (ENL): minimum 7% of the vertical drop

1001.3      旗门
1001.3.1           超级大回转的旗门由 4 根回转旗门杆（本规则第
680.2.1.2 条）和 2 面旗门布组成。

1001.3.2           旗门必须红色、蓝色交替。旗门布宽约 75 厘米，高 约 50 厘米。旗门布应系在两旗门杆之间，其底边至 少应高出雪面 l 米左右，旗门布应可撕脱或可从旗 杆上拉下（参见本规则第 690 条）。



1001.3.3           开口旗门必须至少宽 6 米，至多宽 8 米。垂直闭口
旗门至少宽 8 米，至多宽 12 米。


1001.3.4           超级大回转必须按如下数据设置旗门（经四舍五入 调整后的换向次数）：
对于国际雪联级别的比赛，换向次数最少为垂直落 差的 7%。对于冬季奥林匹克运动会、国际雪联世界 锦标赛、国际雪联世界青少年锦标赛和洲际杯级别 的比赛，换向次数最少为垂直落差的 6%。


相邻两个旗门绕行杆间的距离至少应为 25 米（例外 参见本规则第 1003.1. 1 条）。
U 16 - U14 比赛 ：换向次数最小为垂直落差的 8%， 最大为 12%。
入门级别（ENL）：至少为垂直落差的 7%。






THE INTERNATIONAL SKI
COMPETITION RULES (ICR)

3rd Section   Particular Rules for the different Events 第三部分   各比赛项目的特殊规则






1002          The Courses

1002.1         General Characteristics of the Courses
The terrain should be undulating and hilly if possible. The competition course should normally have a width of approximately 30m.
The inspector authorised to homologate the competition course decides whether this width is adequate and if necessary can order it to be widened. The inspector can also permit a width of less than approximately 30m de- pending on the line and terrain requirements, as long as the areas of the competition course before and after the narrow part enable this.

1002.2         Preparation of the Course
The competition course must be prepared like a Down- hill course. The course sections on which there are gates and where the competitors alter their directions must be prepared for a Slalom.

1002.3        Free-skiing on the Competition Course
Competitors should be given the opportunity to free ski on the closed competition hill before the course is set if possible.

1002.4        Homologation of Youth Super-G courses
All competition courses used for U 16 - U 14 Super-G must be homologated. If the course to be used is ho- mologated for FIS Giant Slalom, then a safety inspection

1002      比赛线路
1002.1          比赛线路的一般特征
地形应选择起伏的丘陵地带。赛道宽度一般应在 30 米左右。
经授权认证赛道的认证官可以决定上述宽度是否足 够，如有必要，可要求加宽。根据赛道线形和地形 的需要，只要赛道狭窄段前后的区域允许，认证官 也可以允许宽度不足 30 米。




1002.2      比赛线路的准备
比赛线路必须比照滑降比赛线路做好准备。比赛线 路上设置旗门组的部分及运动员须转弯处必须比照 回转比赛线路准备。


1002.3      比赛坡道上的自由滑行
如果可能的话，在线路设计前应为运动员提供在封 闭的赛道上自由滑行的机会。


1002.4      青少年超级大回转赛道认证
所有用于 U16-U14 超级大回转的赛道都必须经过认 证。如果所使用的赛道为国际雪联认证的大回转赛 道，需要国际雪联技术顾问进行一次安全视察。

COMPETITION RULES (ICR)

by a FIS Technical Advisor is required.

1003          Course Setting

1003.1         Setting
In setting a Super-G the following principles should be observed:
1003.1.1           It is recommended to set the gates to make the best use of the terrain; Gate combinations according to art.
803.3 are allowed only in small numbers. The distance between the successive turning poles can in this case be less than 25 m, but must be at least 15 m.
1003.1.2           A Super-G should contain a variety of long and medium turns.Competitors should be absolutely free to choose their own line between the gates. It is not permitted to set only down the fall-line of the slope.

1003.1.2.1    At places where outside gate must be removed, in excep- tional cases decided by the Jury the turning gate serves as a gate.

1003.1.3           Where the terrain allows it jumps may be set.

1003.1.4           U 16 - U 14 Super-G should be carried out in a form of varied run. The basic form should consist of jumps and gliding elements. The choice of course and course set- ting has to follow the speed and the U 16 - U 14 level of



1003      旗门设计
1003.1     设计
超级大回转的比赛线路设计应遵循以下原则 ：


1003.1.1           建议充分利用地形来设计旗门。按照本规则第 803.3 条之规定，设计的旗门组合数量不宜过多。相邻两 道旗门的绕行杆间距可少于25米，但至少应为 15米。



1003.1.2           超级大回转应包括各种大中型转弯。运动员在旗门 间应有绝对的自由选择自己的滑行路线。旗门不得 仅沿着坡道的滚落线设置。


1003.1.2.1    在特殊情况下，在必须撤销外侧旗门的地方，仲裁 委员会可决定由绕行门充当旗门。


1003.1.3           在地形允许的地方可以设置跳跃区。

1003.1.4           U 16 - U14 超级大回转赛应以多种形式的滑行进行， 基本形式应包括跳跃和滑行元素。赛道的选择和设 置必须充分适应速度和 U 16 - U14 的技能水平。运 动员应学会掌控下的速度和滑行。

COMPETITION RULES (ICR)

skill. They should learn controlled speed and gliding.

1003.1.5           Course Setting for U14
Different courses must be adapted for U 14 and U 16, which should have turning radiuses corresponding to their age. The ski to be used is the appropriate Giant Sla- lom skis for U 14 events.

1005          Start
Starting order and start intervals according to art. 621.3 and 622.

1006          Execution of the Super-G   A Super-G will be carried out in one run.

1007          Crash Helmet
All competitors and forerunners must wear a crash hel- met for official training as well as for the race that meets the FIS Equipment Specifications.
Soft ear protection is only permitted for helmets used in Slalom.

1008          Yellow Flag
Art. 705 also applies.

1100          Combined

1100.1         Common Rules
Based on art. 201.6.2 and art. 201.6.9 Alpine Combined



1003.1.5     U14 级别的旗门设计
U14 和 U16 级别应采用转弯半径适合其年龄段的不 同张嘴。所用滑雪板应为 U14 级别比赛适用的大回 转滑雪板。


1005      出发
出发顺序和出发间隔按照本规则第 621.3 和第 622 条执行。
1006      超级大回转比赛的实施
超级大回转比赛应只进行 1 轮滑行。

1007      防护头盔
所有运动员和试滑员在场地适应训练和比赛时必须 穿戴符合《国际雪联竞赛器材具体规定》的防护头盔。
仅在回转比赛中允许使用带软护耳的头盔。


1008      黄旗
适用本规则第 705 条。

1100      全能项目
1100.1      通则
依据本规则第 201.6.2 条和第 201.6.9 条，高山滑雪

competitions may be held according to the technical reg- ulations of the events and special regulations approved by FIS.

1100.2         Combined competitions may be held at all levels. When special rules apply (for example, Olympic Win- ter Games, FIS World Ski Championships, World Cup, Continental Cups), these rules are considered an integral part ofthe ICR.

1100.3         The following possibilities of Combined events are possible:
- Alpine Combined
- Classical Combined
- Special forms of Combined events

1100.4         Combined competitions may be held as Single or Team events.

1100.5         Starting numbers given to the competitors for the first run remain the same for all runs.
1100.6         The results of a Combined competition are only counted if the competitor takes part in each event of the Com- bined and appears in the intermediate results.

1100.7         The Combined results are calculated by adding the race times of the single events or runs. Special forms ofCom- bined events (art. 1103) can be calculated according to other regulations.

全能赛可按照国际雪联批准的相应比赛项目的技术 规则和特殊规定举办。


1100.2     全能赛可在任一级别赛事中举行。当特殊规则适用  时（如冬季奥林匹克运动会、国际雪联世界锦标赛、 世界杯、洲际杯赛），此类规则被视为《国际雪联滑  雪竞赛规则》的一部分。


1100.3     下列比赛项目组合可列入全能项目 ：
- 高山滑雪全能 ；
- 传统全能 ；
- 特殊形式的全能项目。

1100.4     全能赛可作为单人或团队赛事举办。


1100.5     运动员在每轮滑行中延用第 1 轮滑行时的出发号码。


1100.6     只有参加了全能赛所有单项比赛且有中间成绩的运 动员才有权取得全能成绩。


1100.7     全能成绩由各单项比赛时间或各轮次滑行时间相加 而得。特殊形式全能项目（本规则第 1103 条）的成 绩根据其他相关规定计算。

COMPETITION RULES (ICR)

3rd Section   Particular Rules for the different Events 第三部分   各比赛项目的特殊规则






1100.8        The Organising Committee must state in the invitation how many competitors are qualified for the second and any subsequent runs. The Jury may change this number.

1100.9         The start order is determined for each event according to art.
621. For special forms of Combined events see art. 1103.2.

1100.10       Only interim results may be published for those events or runs already completed. The official results are only published when all events or runs have been completed.

1100.11       The sequence of the different races to be combined may be decided by the Organisers and must be announced in the race notice and the programme. Changes may be made by the Jury.

1101          Alpine Combined
1101.1         Is the result of a Downhill or Super-G run (speed event) and a single Slalom run held according to the technical regulations for Slalom and those for Downhill or Su- per-G. The Alpine Combined event consists of two runs. (see art. 621.3.3, 621.11.2, 627.7)


1101.2         Downhill and Super-G events of Alpine Combined must be held on courses specifically homologated for Down- hill or Super-G respectively.
The Slalom may be held on these courses.

1100.8     组委会必须在邀请函中说明参赛者有资格参加第二 轮及后续各轮比赛的人数。仲裁委员会可改变该 人数。

1100.9     根据本规则第 621 条决定各单项的出发顺序。全能 项目的特殊比赛形式请参见本规则第 1103.2 条。

1100.10    对已经完成的比赛项目或滑行只会发布中间成绩。 所有项目比赛或滑行结束后才能公布正式成绩。


1100.11    不同比赛项目的比赛顺序可由组织方决定，必须在 比赛通知及比赛秩序册中公布。仲裁委员会可作出 变更。


1101      高山滑雪全能
1101.1     高山滑雪全能由两部分组成 ：体现速度性的一轮滑 降或超级大回转滑行（竞速项目）和体现技巧的单 轮回转滑行。其举办是根据回转和滑降或超级大回 转的技术规则进行的，成绩也是这两类比赛项目之 和。因此，高山滑雪全能赛包括两轮滑行（参见本 规则第 621.3.3 条、第 621.11.2 条、第 627.7 条）。
1101.2     高山滑雪全能中的滑降和超级大回转单项比赛必须 分别在取得滑降或超级大回转认证的赛道上进行。
回转比赛可在此类场地中举行。






THE INTERNATIONAL SKI
COMPETITION RULES (ICR)

3rd Section   Particular Rules for the different Events 第三部分   各比赛项目的特殊规则






1101.3         If possible both runs should be held on one day (excep- tions can only be decided by the Jury).

1102          Classical Combined
1102.1         Is the result of a Downhill and a Slalom. Each event is to be considered separately.

1102.2         If the Slalom is held as the second event, those competi- tors marked with K or ZK start last in the second run, if they are not qualified within the top 30 competitors.

1103          Special forms of Combined events
1103.1         Combined competitions which consist of three (Triple) or four (Quadruple) events held according to art. 700 to 1000 are also permitted.

1103.2        FIS  may authorize Combined competitions which consist of one or several events according to art. 700 to  1000 and other FIS Disciplines or other types of sport (e.g. alpine skiing combined with a Nordic event or swimming or sailing event, etc.) . FIS approval is necessary for such Combined events . Participation and general regulations must be in accordance with the Regulations ofthe ICR.

1101.3     如果可能，两轮滑行均应在一天内进行（例外情况 只能由仲裁委员会决定）。
1102      传统全能
1102.1     比赛成绩为 1 轮滑降比赛和 1 轮回转比赛的成绩之 和。每个比赛项目的比赛成绩分别计算。

1102.2     如果将回转赛安排在第 2 轮，在第 1 轮比赛未进入 前 30 名的选手在其名单上标注 K 或 ZK，并将排在 第 2 轮比赛中后出发。

1103      特殊形式的全能赛事
1103.1     允许全能赛由三到四个比赛项目组成，并按照本规 则第 700 至第 1000 条举办。


1103.2     国际雪联可授权举办由单项或多项高山滑雪比赛项 目组成的全能比赛。其中有的单项可以是符合本规  则第 700 条至第 1000 条规定的高山滑雪比赛项目， 也可以是其他国际雪联竞赛分项或其他体育项目（如  混合了北欧两项、游泳或帆船等项目的高山滑雪比  赛等）。举办这种全能比赛需要得到国际雪联的批准。 这些比赛的参赛规则和总则规定必须遵循《国际雪  联滑雪竞赛规则》。






THE INTERNATIONAL SKI
COMPETITION RULES (ICR)

3rd Section   Particular Rules for the different Events 第三部分   各比赛项目的特殊规则






1210          General Team Competitions
1210.1        The staging of team competitions is permitted.
1210.2         In absence of any agreement to the contrary, a team con- sists of five competitors of which the three best times count for the result.
1210.3         The competitors of the individual teams must be named before the draw.
1210.4         FIS points will be awarded only if the individual events are conducted according to the rules ofthe ICR.

1210.5         The placing of the teams will be determined by addition of the race points of the three best competitors of each team. In case of a tie, the placing is determined by the result of the best individual competitors.

1210.6         For combined placing, the team score for each event is calculated according to art. 1100.7. In case of a tie, the best team is determined by the team placing in the order of Downhill, Super-G, Giant Slalom, and Slalom.

1211         Combined Team Event
The Event consists of two runs (Super-G & Slalom) and four series in each run.

1210      一般团体比赛
1210.1      可以举行团体比赛。
1210.2     如果没有相反的约定，每队由 5 名运动员组成，计 算其中 3 人最佳的比赛成绩。

1210.3     必须在抽签前指定各队的参赛运动员。



1210.4     各比赛项目只有按照《国际雪联滑雪竞赛规则》进行， 参赛运动员才能获得国际雪联积分。

1210.5     各队名次将根据本队最佳的 3 名运动员在比赛中获 得的国际雪联积分累计决定。出现平分的，平分的 各队的名次将由其个人成绩最佳的运动员决定。


1210.6     全能赛名次将根据本规则第 1100.7 条计算的各比赛 项目团体得分决定。出现平分的，将根据各队依次 在滑降赛、超级大回转赛、大回转赛和回转赛的排 名决定最佳团队。
1211      全能团体比赛
比赛由两轮滑行组成（超级大回转和回转），每轮滑 行包含 4 个回合。






THE INTERNATIONAL SKI
COMPETITION RULES (ICR)

3rd Section   Particular Rules for the different Events 第三部分   各比赛项目的特殊规则






1211.1         Participation
All Teams with at least 4 competitors (2 Men and 2 Women) that are qualified to participate in respective events (Super-G and Slalom) are authorized to enter.

1211.1.2            Participants per Team
Per Team and run a maximum of 2 Women and 2 Men must start. The total team size is limited to a maximum of 6 competitors.

1211.2         Competition courses
Women and Men ski on the same course.

1211.3         Enrollment
The Teams are enrolled in the reverse order of total FIS points. Women will receive bibs from 1 to 4 and Men from 5 to 8, ordered alphabetically.

1211.4         Ranking
The sum of rank positions of the competitors per Team from each of the series (1 competitor per team is a series) of both runs establishes the Winner of the Team Event.
In case of a tie of the total sum of rank positions, the number of best rank positions from individual series (1L, 2M, 3L, 4M, 5L, 6M, 7L and 8M) is considered. Should there still be a tie; the total sum of the times of all Series will count.

1211.1     参赛
至少有 4 名运动员（2 男 2 女）具备参加各单项比 赛（超级大回转和回转）资格的团队方可参赛。


1211.1.2     各队的参赛运动员
各队每轮滑行至多有 2 名女子和 2 名男子运动员必 须参赛。每队参赛人数限制在最多 6 人。


1211.2      比赛线路
女子比赛和男子比赛在相同线路上进行。

1211.3      登记
各队按国际雪联积分的倒序进行登记。各队女子运 动员的出发号码布从 1 号到 4 号，男子的出发号码 布从 5 号到 8 号，按字母顺序排列。
1211.4      排名
各队运动员在两项比赛中取得的每个回合比赛排名 （每队 1 名运动员滑行 1 次为 1 个回合）的总和，决
定团体比赛的优胜者。
总排名相同的，应计算各队每一回合最好排名的数 量（1L、2M、3L、4M、5L、6M、7L 和 8M）。 仍 出现平局的，计算所有回合的比赛总时间。






THE INTERNATIONAL SKI
COMPETITION RULES (ICR)

3rd Section   Particular Rules for the different Events 第三部分   各比赛项目的特殊规则






1211.5        Announcement of the competitors at the
start
For the Series 1 Women, 5 minutes before begin of the series.
For all other Series after the end of the preceding Series until 1 minute before begin of the next Series.
In case of non-announcement within the times fixed by the Jury, the competitor is not allowed to start = DNS.

1211.6         Start limitation
One and the same competitor must only start once per run at the FIS Combined Team Event.

1212         Mixed Team Parallel

1212.1         Type of Event
A Mixed Team Parallel event will be conducted as a par- allel using Giant Slalom gates and panels.

1212.2         Team Size
The total team size per Nation is limited to a maximum of 6 competitors; at least 2 competitors from one gender. A competitor can only start a run once.

1212.3         Team Entry
The entries for the Mixed Team Parallel (without names) must be within 24 hours before the scheduled start of the team event.

1211.5      起点检录

女子第 1 回合检录时间为该回合开始前 5 分钟。

其他各回合检录时间为前一回合结束后至当前回合 比赛开始前 1 分钟。
运动员在上述规定及仲裁委员会确定的时间内未检 录的，取消其出发资格，即未出发。
1211.6      出发限制
在国际雪联举办的团体全能比赛中，每名运动员每 轮滑行只能出发 1 次。
1212      高山滑雪团体比赛
1212.1      比赛类型
高山滑雪团体比赛以平行式比赛的方式进行，采用 大回转旗门和旗门布。
1212.2      团队规模
每个国家队的规模最多不超过 6 人，同一性别的运 动员至少有2人。每位运动员每轮滑行只能出发 1次。


1212.3      团队报名
高山滑雪团体比赛的报名（不记名）必须在秩序册 预定的团体赛开始时间前 24 小时完成。






THE INTERNATIONAL SKI
COMPETITION RULES (ICR)

3rd Section   Particular Rules for the different Events 第三部分   各比赛项目的特殊规则






1212.4         Team Ranking
The teams will be ranked in accordance the sum of each entered competitors FIS points, from lowest total points to highest.

1212.5         Seeding of the Teams
The entered teams will be seeded into heats (4, 8 or 16) based upon their ranking. A bracket list will be arranged as follows (Example for 8 Heats):
Heat 1: Nation ranked 1 vs Nation ranked 16(last)
Heat 2: Nation ranked 8 vs Nation ranked 9
Heat 3: Nation ranked 5 vs Nation ranked 12
Heat 4; Nation ranked 4 vs Nation ranked 13
Heat 5: Nation ranked 3 vs Nation ranked 14 (3rd last)
Heat 6: Nation ranked 6 vs Nation ranked 11
Heat 7: Nation ranked 7 vs Nation ranked 10
Heat 8: Nation ranked 2 vs Nation ranked 15 (2nd last)    The best nation, according to the team ranking, will re- ceive bib number 1 and the last nation will receive the last bib number.
Women will receive bibs starting from 1 and then Men, starting from 5, in alphabetical order. If a heat is incom- plete the remaining nation will automatically qualify for the next round (a bye).

1212.6         Running the Competition
Each individual leg between two opponents consists of one run.
The start order will be as follow (as an example  for

1212.4      团队排名
团队排名将根据各队运动员在比赛中获得的国际雪 联积分总和由低到高排列。


1212.5      种子队
参赛队伍将根据排名确定为各组（4 组、8 组或 16 组） 的种子队，由此形成分组安排如下（以 8 组为例）：
第 1 组 ：排名第 1 国 vs 第 16 国（最后 1 名）；
第 2 组 ：排名第 8 国 vs 第 9 国 ；
第 3 组 ：排名第 5 国 vs 第 12 国 ；
第 4 组 ：排名第 4 国 vs 第 13 国 ；
第 5 组 ：排名第 3 国 vs 第 14 国（倒数第 3 名）；
第 6 组 ：排名第 6 国 vs 第 11 国 ；
第 7 组 ：排名第 7 国 vs 第 10 国 ；
第 8 组 ：排名第 2 国 vs 第 15 国（倒数第 2 名）。
按照队伍排名情况，排名最高的国家队出发号码布 为 1 号，排名最低的国家出发号码布为最后 1 个号。

女子出发号码布从 1 号开始，男子从 5 号开始，按 字母顺序排列。如果某个分组仅有 1 支队伍，则该 国家将自动获得进入下一回合的资格（轮空）。


1212.6      进行比赛
以两个国家每一组个人对决作为一个回合。

出发顺序如下（以分组赛第 1 场为例）：

Heat 1):
“Course Red”Nation 1 W 1 against“Course Blue”Na- tion last W 1
